[[Source]](https://starwars.fandom.com/wiki/Template:Character)

:   "*I believe in the Rebel Alliance. I believe in its mission. I believe we will succeed. The Empire will be defeated, and freedom will return to this galaxy. I will not stop until we win, and then I will fight to make sure nothing like the Empire ever returns.*"
:   ―Leia Organa[[25]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_49_2020-25)

**Leia Skywalker Organa Solo** was a [Force-sensitive](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive") [human](/wiki/Human "Human") [Alderaanian](/wiki/Alderaanian "Alderaanian") [female](/wiki/Gender "Gender") [politician](/wiki/Politics "Politics"), [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi"), and [military](/wiki/Alliance_Military "Alliance Military") leader who served in the [Alliance to Restore the Republic](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic") during the [Imperial Era](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era") and the [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic") and [Resistance](/wiki/Resistance "Resistance") in the subsequent [New Republic Era](/wiki/New_Republic_Era "New Republic Era"). Shortly after birth on [Polis Massa](/wiki/Polis_Massa "Polis Massa"), she was adopted into the [House of Organa](/wiki/House_of_Organa "House of Organa")—the Alderaanian [royal](/wiki/King "King") family—and was raised as [Princess](/wiki/Princess "Princess") **Leia Organa** of [Alderaan](/wiki/Alderaan "Alderaan"), a [planet](/wiki/Planet "Planet") in the [Core Worlds](/wiki/Core_Worlds "Core Worlds") known for its dedication to pacifism. The princess was raised as the daughter of [Senator](/wiki/Senator "Senator") [Bail Prestor Organa](/wiki/Bail_Prestor_Organa "Bail Prestor Organa") and his [wife](/wiki/Marriage "Marriage"), [Queen](/wiki/Queen "Queen") [Breha Organa](/wiki/Breha_Organa "Breha Organa"), making her the heir to the [Alderaanian monarchy](/wiki/Alderaanian_monarchy "Alderaanian monarchy"). Instilled with the values of her adopted [homeworld](/wiki/Homeworld "Homeworld"), Organa devoted her life to the restoration of [democracy](/wiki/Democracy "Democracy") by opposing [authoritarian](/wiki/Fascism "Fascism") regimes, such as the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire") and the [First Order](/wiki/First_Order "First Order").

[Born](/wiki/Reproduction "Reproduction") in [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY") as **Leia Amidala Skywalker**, she was the daughter of the [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker") and Senator [Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala") of [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo"). Her birth occurred in the aftermath of the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"), which saw the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order") [purged](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge") and the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic") [reorganized](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") into the [Galactic](/wiki/Galaxy "Galaxy") Empire. With her [mother's](/wiki/Parent "Parent") [death](/wiki/Death "Death") in childbirth and her father's fall to the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force"), Leia and her [twin](/wiki/Twin "Twin") brother, [Luke](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker"), were separated to keep them hidden from the hands of her father and the [Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor"). As the adopted daughter of a politician, Leia grew up peacefully—albeit secluded—on Alderaan until she was kidnapped by mercenaries led by [Vect Nokru](/wiki/Vect_Nokru "Vect Nokru")—under the orders of the [Third Sister](/wiki/Reva_Sevander "Reva Sevander"), a member of the [Inquisitorius](/wiki/Inquisitorius "Inquisitorius")—in [9 BBY](/wiki/9_BBY "9 BBY"). Since he had fought alongside her adoptive father in the Clone Wars, [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi") went to Leia's rescue on [Daiyu](/wiki/Daiyu "Daiyu"), and, after evading the Empire's hand on [Mapuzo](/wiki/Mapuzo "Mapuzo") and [Jabiim](/wiki/Jabiim "Jabiim"), Leia was brought back to Alderaan. Years later, Leia succeeded Bail by representing their homeworld in the [Imperial Senate](/wiki/Imperial_Senate "Imperial Senate"), though secretly she supported the Rebellion. During the [Galactic Civil War](/wiki/Galactic_Civil_War "Galactic Civil War"), however, Alderaan was [destroyed](/wiki/Destruction_of_Alderaan "Destruction of Alderaan") along with its inhabitants and the royal family by the Empire's [DS-1 Death Star Mobile Battle Station](/wiki/DS-1_Orbital_Battle_Station "DS-1 Orbital Battle Station"), causing Organa to openly fight the [New Order](/wiki/New_Order "New Order") as one of the Rebel Alliance’s substantial heroes.

In the aftermath of the [Battle of Endor](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor "Battle of Endor"), Organa [married](/wiki/Wedding_of_Han_Solo_and_Leia_Organa "Wedding of Han Solo and Leia Organa") the [Corellian](/wiki/Corellian "Corellian") [smuggler](/wiki/Smuggler "Smuggler") [Han Solo](/wiki/Han_Solo "Han Solo") and learned the [Jedi arts](/wiki/Jedi_training "Jedi training") as her brother's [apprentice](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan") until giving birth to her son, [Ben Solo](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo"), on the [day](/wiki/Standard_day "Standard day") of the Empire's [capitulation](/wiki/Galactic_Concordance "Galactic Concordance") in [5 ABY](/wiki/5_ABY "5 ABY"). Her personal and political life suffered in the [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") that followed, with Ben turning to the dark side like his grandfather before him, adopting the persona of Kylo Ren, and the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/New_Republic_Senate "New Republic Senate") sidelining Organa's career. Adopting the [military rank](/wiki/Military_rank "Military rank") of [general](/wiki/General "General"), she led the Resistance and their efforts to oppose the rising First Order during the [Cold War](/wiki/Cold_War "Cold War") while seeking to make amends with Ben in hopes that her son will return to the [light side of the Force](/wiki/Light_side_of_the_Force "Light side of the Force") like her father during the Battle of Endor. Despite her efforts, the First Order succeeded in [destroying](/wiki/Hosnian_Cataclysm "Hosnian Cataclysm") the New Republic, and Organa's husband [died](/wiki/Battle_of_Starkiller_Base "Battle of Starkiller Base") at the hands of their estranged son in [34 ABY](/wiki/34_ABY "34 ABY"). Organa continued to lead the Resistance during the [war](/wiki/First_Order-Resistance_War "First Order-Resistance War") against the First Order, all the while passing on her Jedi training onto [Rey](/wiki/Rey_Skywalker "Rey Skywalker")—a Force-sensitive [scavenger](/wiki/Scavenger "Scavenger") from [Jakku](/wiki/Jakku "Jakku") and Luke’s apprentice.

As her health declined, Organa used her remaining strength to reach her son, calling him back to the light side. Following her death on [Ajan Kloss](/wiki/Ajan_Kloss "Ajan Kloss") in [35 ABY](/wiki/35_ABY "35 ABY"), her final actions inspired Rey and the Resistance to [defeat](/wiki/Battle_of_Exegol "Battle of Exegol") the [forces](/wiki/Final_Order "Final Order") of the [reborn](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning") Darth Sidious's [Sith Eternal](/wiki/Sith_Eternal "Sith Eternal") on [Exegol](/wiki/Exegol "Exegol") and spark an [uprising against the First Order](/wiki/Uprising_against_the_First_Order "Uprising against the First Order") across [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy"). The heir to three inheritances, Leia Skywalker Organa Solo's legacy passed on to the Jedi Rey Skywalker, the military leader [Poe Dameron](/wiki/Poe_Dameron "Poe Dameron") of the Resistance, and Ben Solo, her only child, who ultimately returned to the light before sacrificing his life for Rey and becoming one with the Force to join his mother and the [Skywalker family](/wiki/Skywalker_family "Skywalker family").

## Biography[]

### Pre-birth[]

:   "*There is another…Skywalker.*"
:   ―Serenity[[26]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-26)

Towards the [end](/wiki/Mission_to_Mustafar "Mission to Mustafar") of the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"),[[26]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-26) a [galactic](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy") conflict fought between the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic") and the [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems") that was engineered by the [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord") [Darth Sidious](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious"),[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_III-12) [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda") set out on a journey to discover the secrets of [immortality](/wiki/Force_spirit "Force spirit"). His journey [took](/wiki/Mission_to_Moraband "Mission to Moraband") him to [Moraband](/wiki/Moraband "Moraband"), the ancient [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith") [homeworld](/wiki/Homeworld "Homeworld"), where he faced visions of the future. At the end of his journey, the [Force Priestess](/wiki/Force_Priestesses "Force Priestesses"), [Serenity](/wiki/Serenity "Serenity"), who had guided his journey, told him that there was another Skywalker, and Yoda heard his voice from the future say so as well.[[26]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-26) These events not only alluded to the potential he would sense in Leia,[[27]](#cite_note-There_is_Another-27) but to what Yoda would tell her [twin](/wiki/Twin "Twin") brother, [Luke](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker"), about Leia in his last words, before his [death](/wiki/Death "Death").[[11]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-11)

### Early life[]

#### Birth[]

:   "*It's a girl.*"  
    "*Leia.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Padmé Amidala[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_III-12)

 [![Leia Amidala Skywalker was born after the fall of the Galactic Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/Midwife_droid_1.png/revision/latest?cb=20130215034827) [![Leia Amidala Skywalker was born after the fall of the Galactic Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/Midwife_droid_1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130215034827)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/Midwife_droid_1.png/revision/latest?cb=20130215034827) 

Leia Amidala Skywalker was born after the fall of the Galactic Republic.

 

Leia Amidala Skywalker[[28]](#cite_note-Updated_and_Expanded-28) was [born](/wiki/Reproduction "Reproduction") on the [asteroid](/wiki/Asteroid "Asteroid") of [Polis Massa](/wiki/Polis_Massa "Polis Massa")[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_III-12) two [days](/wiki/Standard_day "Standard day") after the [end](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") of the Clone Wars and the newly established [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire")'s [purge](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66") of the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order").[[2]](#cite_note-Siege_RR-2) She and her twin brother, Luke, who was born shortly before her, were the children of Republic [Senator](/wiki/Senator "Senator") [Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala"), who died shortly after the births, and [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker"), who had recently fallen to the [dark side](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force") of [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force").[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_III-12) She was left with a lasting impression of images and feelings of her mother that her brother did not: that their mother was "very beautiful, kind, but sad."[[11]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-11) Though Leia was unsure if she had really seen her mother or if she had just invented the memories to fill the hole in her life.[[29]](#cite_note-BtPotDS!-29)

Of the two Skywalker children, [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda") felt that Leia was more suited to be a Jedi, owing to her natural strength, will, and clarity (as opposed to her brother, who was impetuous, headstrong, unruly, and inattentive), wanting very much to train her.[[27]](#cite_note-There_is_Another-27) However, to protect the children from the Empire, [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Sidious, who ruled the Empire as [Galactic Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor") Palpatine, and the now–Sith [Lord](/wiki/Lord "Lord") [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Vader, Senator [Bail Prestor Organa](/wiki/Bail_Prestor_Organa "Bail Prestor Organa") agreed to adopt the infant Leia together with his [wife](/wiki/Marriage "Marriage"), [Queen](/wiki/Queen "Queen") [Breha](/wiki/Breha_Organa "Breha Organa") of [Alderaan](/wiki/Alderaan "Alderaan"), while [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi") personally watched over Luke, who would live with their [father's](/wiki/Parent "Parent") stepbrother [Owen Lars](/wiki/Owen_Lars "Owen Lars") and his wife [Beru](/wiki/Beru_Whitesun_Lars "Beru Whitesun Lars"), on the [planet](/wiki/Planet "Planet") [Tatooine](/wiki/Tatooine "Tatooine").[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_III-12)

#### Princess of Alderaan[]

:   "*My wife and I will take the girl. We've always talked of adopting a baby girl. She will be loved with us.*"
:   ―Bail Organa[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_III-12)

 [![The royal couple of Alderaan adopted the late Padmé Amidala's infant daughter, renaming her Leia Organa.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/00/Baby_leia.png/revision/latest?cb=20130206235750) [![The royal couple of Alderaan adopted the late Padmé Amidala's infant daughter, renaming her Leia Organa.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/00/Baby_leia.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130206235750)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/00/Baby_leia.png/revision/latest?cb=20130206235750) 

The royal couple of Alderaan adopted the late Padmé Amidala's infant daughter, renaming her Leia Organa.

 

Through adoption, Leia Amidala Skywalker became Leia Organa, formally becoming heiress of the [Royal Family of Alderaan](/wiki/House_of_Organa "House of Organa")[[28]](#cite_note-Updated_and_Expanded-28) through the [Name Day](/wiki/Name_Day "Name Day") ceremony.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14) Although it was common knowledge that she was adopted,[[30]](#cite_note-DB-Leia-bio-30) and everyone assumed that she was just another of the many, many children left orphaned by the Clone Wars,[[29]](#cite_note-BtPotDS!-29) she remained unaware of her biological parents' fates.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_III-12) When Leia was an infant, she was mesmerized by the fish in an [aquarium](/wiki/Aquarium "Aquarium") while her adoptive father read secret files concerning the former [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan") [Ahsoka Tano](/wiki/Ahsoka_Tano "Ahsoka Tano")'s presence on the agrarian [moon](/wiki/Moon "Moon") of [Raada](/wiki/Raada "Raada"). Bail later carried her after reading the files.[[31]](#cite_note-Ahsoka-31) On one occasion when Leia was a toddler she escaped from her [bath](/wiki/Bath "Bath") and ran wet and naked into the formal dining room interrupting a [diplomatic dinner](/wiki/Unidentified_diplomatic_dinner "Unidentified diplomatic dinner") and causing [WA-2V](/wiki/WA-2V "WA-2V") to chase after her.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

Leia was eventually told that her birth father had died during one of the last battles of the Clone Wars and that her birth mother had been injured and only lived long enough to give birth to her. However, Leia had no interest in her birth parents seeing her adoptive parents as the only family she ever needed. Often when Leia went to sleep her parents would tell her that they had waited a long time for a child, as part of the story about when her father had come home from some "mysterious mission" to surprise her mother with a baby girl in her arms.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

 [![As a small child, Leia believed that her mother had a bouquet of candlewick flowers inside her chest.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6a/CandlewickFlower-LeiaManga.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210725065434) [![As a small child, Leia believed that her mother had a bouquet of candlewick flowers inside her chest.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6a/CandlewickFlower-LeiaManga.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20210725065434)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6a/CandlewickFlower-LeiaManga.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210725065434) 

As a small child, Leia believed that her mother had a bouquet of candlewick flowers inside her chest.

 

As a small child, Leia believed that the glowing coming from inside her mother's chest was a bouquet of blooming [candlewick flowers](/wiki/Candlewick_flower "Candlewick flower"). She would eventually learn that the glowing was from Breha's [pulmonodes](/wiki/Pulmonodes "Pulmonodes"), which she had gotten after a near fatal [climbing accident](/wiki/The_accident "The accident") when she was sixteen, during her [Challenge of the Body](/wiki/Challenge_of_the_Body "Challenge of the Body"). She told Leia that she had chosen not to cover them up with skin through [bacta](/wiki/Bacta "Bacta") sessions, as they were proof that she had survived. Leia would eventually go on to meet other people with the same cybernetics.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

Sometime after her fourth birthday, Leia received her "big girl bed," which made her realize that she was too old to sleep in her parent's bed. Thus, she stopped doing so except when she fell ill and on one occasion when she watched a [holo](/wiki/Unidentified_holo "Unidentified holo") about [undead](/wiki/Zombie "Zombie") [gundarks](/wiki/Gundark "Gundark").[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14) During her childhood, Leia was taught by her father to appreciate the effort of Alderaan's workers, but also the importance of her duties as the planet's eventual [queen](/wiki/Queen "Queen")[[32]](#cite_note-PL2-32) and by her mother, that the life of royalty could be a very lonely and isolated one.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14) She would often stand alongside her parents, waiting through Alderaan's endless royal ceremonies, knowing that she could let no emotion show on her face.[[18]](#cite_note-Moving_Target-18)

 [![Organa had a royal upbringing that came with her station as princess of Alderaan.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/12/WA2V-LeiaManga.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200110190016) [![Organa had a royal upbringing that came with her station as princess of Alderaan.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/12/WA2V-LeiaManga.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20200110190016)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/12/WA2V-LeiaManga.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200110190016) 

Organa had a royal upbringing that came with her station as princess of Alderaan.

 

Leia considered her adoption by the Organas to be a privilege accompanied by duty and sacrifice. Ruling Alderaan would require giving up her freedom, her dignity, and even her private self in the service of a larger whole, but she worked hard to fulfill her parents' dreams for her and to be worthy of someday ruling her planet.[[33]](#cite_note-Queen's_Peril-33) Leia was also reared by several aunts, who gave her etiquette lessons to turn her into a proper patrician,[[34]](#cite_note-TPtSatFB-34) and lectured her about maintaining her appearance and the company she kept[[18]](#cite_note-Moving_Target-18) and schooled her in diplomacy-the skill of handling delicate relations.[[35]](#cite_note-Princess_Leia:_Royal_Rebel-35) Although Leia genuinely loved them, she refused to let them mold her into a simpering princess whose only aim in life was to find a suitable husband.[[34]](#cite_note-TPtSatFB-34) She once complained to one of her aunts that "being a princess had to be about more than silently doing one's duty," but her aunt replied with a sad smile that she had just described most of a princess's job.[[18]](#cite_note-Moving_Target-18)

Leia also had [educational droids](/wiki/CZ-series_tutor_droid "CZ-series tutor droid") for standard academic subjects and a dozen tutors in subjects such as pathfinding, diplomacy, piloting, navigation, and hand-to-hand-combat.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14) Leia also studied galactic politics, manners and rhetoric and took part in composition classes and diplomacy workshops.[[35]](#cite_note-Princess_Leia:_Royal_Rebel-35) Leia also attempted to get the hang of basic accounting during her childhood as her mother, as Alderaan's queen, had of the royal books and had to personally oversee the funding of all public works on the planet. Leia did well enough at it but hated every moment and within a week Breha released her with "a hug and a laugh." When Leia had tried protesting that she would need to learn if she was going to be queen Breha jokingly responded that all she needed to do was fall in love with someone who liked bookkeeping as then she could make her viceroy do it.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

#### Continued childhood[]

On one occasion when Leia was young, Bail, while he and Leia sat by the hearth in the royal family's private library, explained to her that the people of Alderaan loved and were loyal to the royal family as they showed them love and loyalty in return and that if they ever ceased to appreciate those around them, "from the highest lord to the humblest labourer," not only would they lose that loyalty, they would *deserve* to lose it. On another occasion Bail cradled Leia in his lap and pointed her towards the famous Alderaanian [mountain](/wiki/Mountain "Mountain") [Appenza Peak](/wiki/Appenza_Peak "Appenza Peak") and told Leia about how her mother had had to climb the mountain "all by herself" to become crown princess, something that greatly shocked the young Leia who couldn't even climb into her high bed without 2V's help.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

Breha would also chase Leia around the palace with her hair down and her dressing gown flowing behind her and with Leia trusting her mother to be no more than a few steps behind.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14) At one point, Leia escaped from the care of her [nanny droid](/wiki/Nanny_droid "Nanny droid") and ran through the gardens of the [royal palace](/wiki/Royal_Palace_of_Alderaan "Royal Palace of Alderaan") before finding her adoptive mother, Breha, reading in front of a statue of Leia's biological mother, Padmé Amidala. Staring up at the statue, Breha began to explain Amidala's long history, mesmerizing Leia. Breha began by explaining her start as an [Apprentice Legislator](/wiki/Apprentice_Legislator "Apprentice Legislator") in the [Royal House of Naboo](/wiki/Royal_House_of_Naboo "Royal House of Naboo") and the beginning of her long and arduous [political](/wiki/Politics "Politics") career from a very young age. She went on to explain the hardships she had faced while serving the government of [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo"), including her election as queen and the [Invasion of Naboo](/wiki/Invasion_of_Naboo "Invasion of Naboo")[[36]](#cite_note-So_Much_More-36) in [32 BBY](/wiki/32_BBY "32 BBY").

Calmly passing through her time as queen, Breha continued by explaining that Amidala may have been a capable fighter on the battlefield, but the most important battles she ever fought were in the [Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate"), using her words as her weapon as opposed to her [blaster](/wiki/Blaster "Blaster"), and that she would continue to fight in the Senate until lasting peace was brought to [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy"). Finally, Breha explained that Amidala had been a beacon of hope for the entire galaxy and that even though she had passed on, her symbol, her spark, remained. Ending her speech, Breha finally came to the point of what she had wished to say to Leia, explaining that the spark of hope that Amidala had left upon the galaxy continued to live inside Leia, a spark that would one day reignite hope within the galaxy.[[36]](#cite_note-So_Much_More-36)

During her childhood, Leia didn't have many friends her own age as, despite how egalitarian the Alderaanian monarchy was, there was always a dividing line between those who lived in the palace and those who lived outside its walls. Leia would gambol around on the rolling ground with some of the cooks' children but for the most part Leia's companions had been her parents.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14) At one point during her childhood, the princess met her [first member](/wiki/Unidentified_Wookiee_(Leia_Organa) "Unidentified Wookiee (Leia Organa)") of the [Wookiee](/wiki/Wookiee "Wookiee") race, who was a guest of her father's at a state dinner. That guest made a strong impression on her and, eventually, Bail Organa gifted her daughter a [Wookiee](/wiki/Leia_Organa%27s_doll "Leia Organa's doll") [doll](/wiki/Doll "Doll"), which she came to regard as some sort of guardian, watching over her in her room.[[37]](#cite_note-Hyperspace_Stories_2-37) By the time she was six, Leia had met a [king](/wiki/King "King") for the first time.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

In [10 BBY](/wiki/10_BBY "10 BBY"),[[38]](#cite_note-10_BBY-38) a week before her ninth Name Day Leia had hidden behind the screens in the palace's banquet hall when her parents had been dining alone. Being 'young and self-centred' Leia assumed they'd probably be discussing her presents. Instead, they'd been laughing and flirting, and Leia had ended up scurrying out red faced in time to avoid an unwelcome lesson in what spouses did [together](/wiki/Reproduction "Reproduction") in their private hours. This event had caused Leia to not venture behind the screens again[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14) till [3 BBY](/wiki/3_BBY "3 BBY").[[39]](#cite_note-Leia_Date-39) In 10 BBY,[[3]](#cite_note-Timelines-3) the nine-year-old princess ran away from the royal palace for the first time. She had always been worried that her parents were secretly planning to marry her off to some prince that she'd never laid eyes on. Leia hid in the woods for a week where she learned to hunt and survive in the woods until her parents' [guards](/wiki/Alderaan_Guard "Alderaan Guard") finally tracked her down. She later remembered that incident as the "best week of her life."[[40]](#cite_note-SW33-40)

#### Abducted on Alderaan[]

:   "*I'm not even a real Organa.*"  
    "*Don't ever say that. You are our child. You are an Organa in every way.*"
:   ―Leia and her father[[41]](#cite_note-Kenobi_Part_I-41)

Before a visit by her aunt's family[[41]](#cite_note-Kenobi_Part_I-41) in [9 BBY](/wiki/9_BBY "9 BBY"),[[42]](#cite_note-KenobiDate-42) Organa had her alien friend impersonate her to prank her mother. Instead of dressing up for the occasion, Organa spent time in the nearby woods, watching starships depart together with her [toy droid](/wiki/Toy_droid "Toy droid"), [L0-LA59](/wiki/L0-LA59 "L0-LA59") "Lola." After getting picked up from the forest by her mother and two Alderaanian guards, Organa was present at the landing dock with her family to receive the guests—aunt [Celly](/wiki/Celly_Organa "Celly Organa"), uncle [Kayo](/wiki/Kayo_Organa "Kayo Organa"), and cousin [Niano Organa](/wiki/Niano_Organa "Niano Organa").[[41]](#cite_note-Kenobi_Part_I-41)

 [![Leia and Niano arguing](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7f/LeiaNiano-KenobiPartI.png/revision/latest?cb=20220704171107) [![Leia and Niano arguing](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7f/LeiaNiano-KenobiPartI.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20220704171107)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7f/LeiaNiano-KenobiPartI.png/revision/latest?cb=20220704171107) 

Leia and Niano arguing

 

During the ensuing reception, Organa engaged Niano, who berated her for being polite to a droid and called her out for being adopted and thus not a "real Organa." The princess retorted by calling out Niano for being insecure. Later, she was told by her mother to apologize to Niano, and her father reassured her that she was an Organa in every way. Agreeing to apologize to her cousin, Organa instead ran into the nearby woods with Lola.[[41]](#cite_note-Kenobi_Part_I-41)

Unbeknown to the Organa family, the [Third Sister](/wiki/Reva_Sevander "Reva Sevander"), an [Inquisitor](/wiki/Inquisitorius "Inquisitorius") seeking to lure out the fugitive Jedi Master Kenobi, had hired [Vect Nokru](/wiki/Vect_Nokru "Vect Nokru") to kidnap Leia, hoping that her father would contact his old friend Kenobi. As Leia ran in the forest, she was ambushed by Nokru and his two associates, who pursued the princess, shooting an Alderaanian guard in the process. Departing for the planet [Daiyu](/wiki/Daiyu "Daiyu"), where the Third Sister planned to ambush Kenobi, the criminals tied Organa in a room aboard the starship. While attempting to free herself with the help of Lola, Nokru entered the room and took the toy droid, tossing it onto the floor.[[41]](#cite_note-Kenobi_Part_I-41)

#### Danger on Daiyu[]

On Daiyu, Organa was taken to [The Den](/wiki/The_Den "The Den"), a [spice](/wiki/Spice "Spice") laboratory where she was imprisoned in a backroom. The Third Sister's suspicions were correct, as the princess' father indeed reached out to Kenobi and managed to convince him to embark on a [mission](/wiki/Search_for_Princess_Leia "Search for Princess Leia") to rescue Organa. Following Bail Organa's lead to the planet, Kenobi eventually infiltrated The Den after advice from con artist [Haja Estree](/wiki/Haja_Estree "Haja Estree"). After overpowering Nokru and his crew, Kenobi found the room where Organa was being held and managed to convince her that he was there to rescue her on her father's behalf. The Third Sister, however, learning of Nokru's failure, placed a bounty on Kenobi; now chased by bounty hunters and criminals, Organa and Kenobi switched clothes to avoid attracting attention.[[43]](#cite_note-Kenobi_Part_II-43)

 [![Obi-Wan buys clothes for Leia in order to escape from Daiyu](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/50/Daiyu_marketplace.png/revision/latest?cb=20220706123334) [![Obi-Wan buys clothes for Leia in order to escape from Daiyu](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/50/Daiyu_marketplace.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220706123334)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/50/Daiyu_marketplace.png/revision/latest?cb=20220706123334) 

Obi-Wan buys clothes for Leia in order to escape from Daiyu

 

As the two traversed [Daiyu City](/wiki/Daiyu_City "Daiyu City") to the [Daiyu spaceport](/wiki/Daiyu_spaceport "Daiyu spaceport"), Organa was unconvinced that Kenobi was a real Jedi, asking him multiple times to prove it. The two were attacked by a bounty hunter, whom Kenobi dispatched, with Organa correctly deducing that she was being used as bait after she saw a hologram of Kenobi. No longer believing Kenobi to be sent by her father, the princess fled through the city streets with Kenobi in pursuit. Their chase attracted the attention of bounty hunters, however, with several targeting Kenobi as he pursued the fleeing Organa across rooftops. Reaching the end of a roof, Organa attempted to make the jump to another building but fell short; as she was falling to her demise, Kenobi used the Force to levitate her safely to the ground, and Organa finally believed that Kenobi was a Jedi.[[43]](#cite_note-Kenobi_Part_II-43)

Arriving at the spaceport, Organa and Kenobi witnessed Imperial forces—including [stormtroopers](/wiki/Stormtrooper "Stormtrooper") and [Inquisitors](/wiki/Inquisitor "Inquisitor")—locking down the facility to prevent all travel. They were then confronted by Estree who, after a change of heart, advised the fugitives to make for a [cargo port](/wiki/Daiyu_cargo_port "Daiyu cargo port") across the city. Before Organa and Kenobi could enter a cargo transport, however, the Third Sister arrived in the hangar and prepared for a confrontation with Kenobi. While Kenobi prepared for a showdown, Organa ran to the transport, where she watched as the Third Sister taunted Kenobi. Before a confrontation between the two could occur, however, the Third Sister's superior, [the Grand Inquisitor](/wiki/The_Grand_Inquisitor "The Grand Inquisitor"), arrived at the hangar and told her to stand down. Unwilling to let the Grand Inquisitor take credit for the capture of Kenobi, the Third Sister stabbed her superior in the abdomen, allowing Organa and Kenobi to escape aboard the cargo transport, bound for the planet [Mapuzo](/wiki/Mapuzo "Mapuzo").[[43]](#cite_note-Kenobi_Part_II-43)

#### Peril on Mapuzo[]

:   "*I didn't do it on purpose. I didn't mean to run away. I used to do it all the time. I just…It was just for fun.*"
:   ―Leia Organa to Obi-Wan Kenobi[[44]](#cite_note-Kenobi_Part_III-44)

 [![Leia Organa and Obi-Wan Kenobi travel to a rendezvous point on Mapuzo.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ea/KenobiOrganaMapuzo-KenobiPartIII.png/revision/latest?cb=20220611234617) [![Leia Organa and Obi-Wan Kenobi travel to a rendezvous point on Mapuzo.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ea/KenobiOrganaMapuzo-KenobiPartIII.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220611234617)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ea/KenobiOrganaMapuzo-KenobiPartIII.png/revision/latest?cb=20220611234617) 

Leia Organa and Obi-Wan Kenobi travel to a rendezvous point on Mapuzo.

 

As the shuttle traveled to its destination, Leia asked Kenobi if they were almost there and if he could use the Force to make it get them there faster. He told her that the Force didn't work that way, which prompted her to ask how it worked and what it felt like. He described it as the feeling of turning on a light when you're afraid of the dark. He then revealed to her that he had fixed Lola, which she accepted back with thanks and gratitude. The cargo shuttle soon after landed on Mapuzo, which was under the control of the Galactic Empire. Kenobi told Leia to pretend to be his daughter and that they were farmers from [Tawl](/wiki/Tawl "Tawl"), asking her to use a fake name and to not talk to anyone.[[44]](#cite_note-Kenobi_Part_III-44)

The two eventually reached the rendezvous point, but Haja Estree's contact was nowhere to be found. Leia waved down a nearby vehicle and convinced the driver, a man named [Freck](/wiki/Freck "Freck"), to drive them to the nearest space port. Freck agreed, and they climbed on the back. Along the way, Freck revealed that he was a staunch supporter of the Empire, which "Luma" and "Orden" agreed to avoid suspicion. Soon after, Freck stopped and offered a ride to a squad of traveling stormtroopers. Leia told the troopers that the reason that they came to Mapuzo was because it was her mother's homeworld. Trying to corroborate, Kenobi accidentally referred to Leia by her real name, which caught the attention of the troopers. Kenobi quickly covered the mistake by claiming that "Luma" simply reminded him of her deceased mother "Leia." Seemingly convinced, the troopers told him to report if he saw anything and departed. Because of the story he gave, Leia questioned if Kenobi knew her "real" mother, believing that he had been lying and hiding something from her the entire time. She even asked if he was her birth father, which he denied. Leia shared with Obi-Wan that she frequently thinks of what her birth family looked like, with which Kenobi empathized.[[44]](#cite_note-Kenobi_Part_III-44)

The transport eventually arrived at an Imperial checkpoint, where stormtroopers had a [Viper probe droid](/wiki/Viper_probe_droid "Viper probe droid") scan Kenobi, but he shot the droid with a blaster and started a fight between him and the troopers. One trooper held Leia and put a blaster to her head, ordering Kenobi to put his blaster down or he would shoot her. Kenobi pretended to put his blaster down before shooting the trooper. They were confronted by more troopers as they tried to escape, but [Tala Durith](/wiki/Tala_Durith "Tala Durith"), under the guise of an Imperial officer shot them down. She revealed that she was Estree's contact. She brought Leia and Kenobi to a nearby settlement and stated that they needed to lay low for a few hours until one of her [pilots](/wiki/Pilot "Pilot") could take them off-world. While they waited for Tala, Leia clutched Lola and expressed regret for running away, saying that she didn't mean for all of this to happen and that she wanted to go home. Kenobi assured her that it wasn't her fault. The two took shelter in Durith's workshop, where she introduced Leia to her [loader droid](/wiki/Loader_droid "Loader droid"), [NED-B](/wiki/NED-B "NED-B"), who Leia then introduced to Lola. Tala revealed that she secretly works to help Jedi and other [Force-sensitives](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive"), which Leia was intrigued by. When night fell, the trio departed for the spaceport, but Kenobi sensed a disturbance in the Force as Darth Vader arrived with inquisitors and Imperial forces, terrorizing civilians, and killing at random to draw Kenobi out. Kenobi told Tala to get Leia to Alderaan while he distracted Vader. As Durith and Leia headed to the spaceport, Leia convinced Durith to return and help Kenobi, and that she could reach the ship by herself. Durith reluctantly agreed and left Leia alone to go back and help Kenobi. However, as Leia headed to the ship, she ran into the Third Sister, who had arrived first and killed the pilot. The inquisitor tried to win Leia's trust, but Leia, sensing danger, instead turned and ran,[[44]](#cite_note-Kenobi_Part_III-44) though the inquisitor eventually caught her and took her prisoner.[[45]](#cite_note-Kenobi_Part_IV-45)

#### Prisoner of Fortress Inquisitorius[]

:   "*You can't keep me here. My father is Bail Organa, he's a senator. I am a princess of Alderaan!*"
:   ―Leia Organa to her captors in the Fortress Inquisitorius[[45]](#cite_note-Kenobi_Part_IV-45)

Leia was taken to and held in the [Fortress Inquisitorius](/wiki/Fortress_Inquisitorius "Fortress Inquisitorius") on the ocean moon of [Nur](/wiki/Nur "Nur"). At one point, she defiantly told her stormtrooper captors that she was the daughter of a senator and a Princess of Alderaan, and thus could not keep her there. The Third Sister Reva then entered the interrogation room, stating that the Empire didn't tolerate Jedi sympathizers. She also claimed that Kenobi was dead and that nobody was coming for Leia. She then told Leia that the Inquisitors intercepted a transmission on [Balnab](/wiki/Balnab "Balnab") the [previous year](/wiki/10_BBY "10 BBY"), which exposed a secret network known as [the Path](/wiki/Hidden_Path "Hidden Path") and later uncovered another safehouse in two systems. She asked Leia for her help in locating other members of the Path. When Leia asked how Kenobi died, Reva claimed that he was burned to death on Mapuzo. She further claimed that the other members of the Path abandoned Kenobi and then offered to let Leia return to her family if she revealed where the Path was. Leia replied that she didn't know anything about the Path, prompting the Inquisitor to reiterate her demand.[[45]](#cite_note-Kenobi_Part_IV-45)

Reva performed a mind probe of Leia, who remained defiant, leaving Reva unable to breach her mind and extract any information. While Reva was distracted, Leia released L0-LA59 from her pocket, but Reva caught the droid before it could do anything. She revealed to Leia that she had a droid when she was younger but that it was taken from her. Reva attempted to secure Leia's cooperation by claiming that the people she was trying to protect were not coming for her and that she alone could save herself from pain before reiterating her question. Leia pretended to cooperate but asked Reva to promise that nobody will get hurt and if she could speak to her father. With Leia unwilling to cooperate, Reva ordered the stormtrooper guards to prepare Leia for [torture](/wiki/Torture "Torture"). Leia remained defiant and vowed not to tell her captors anything. The stormtroopers fastened Leia into a torture harness while Leia cried for help. Reva became determined to extract the information that she believed Leia possessed through torture. As the machine lit up, the Third Sister gave Leia a final chance, but she refused to cooperate.[[46]](#cite_note-Kenobi_Part_VI-46)

However, Kenobi had not really died on Mapuzo, he and Durith had traveled to [Jabiim](/wiki/Jabiim "Jabiim") and met up with the rest of the Path. Kenobi devised a plan to rescue Leia and asked the Path leader [Kawlan Roken](/wiki/Kawlan_Roken "Kawlan Roken") to help him accomplish it. He was reluctant but eventually agreed and helped Durith sneak into the Fortress disguised as an Imperial Officer, who then allowed Kenobi to swim in through the underside of the Fortress by opening it from the inside. As two needles approached Leia on the torture machine, Kenobi sensed that she was in danger and asked Durith to create a distraction. She sent an officer into the interrogation chamber saying she had a message, which successfully pulled the Third Sister away from Leia. Kenobi then shut down the lights in the interrogation chamber, took out both stormtrooper sentries with his lightsaber, and freed Leia from the torture harness. Leia was relieved that Kenobi was alive and told him that she did not tell the Empire anything.[[45]](#cite_note-Kenobi_Part_IV-45)

 [![Leia is rescued by Ben.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/85/Rescue-of-Leia-Part4.png/revision/latest?cb=20220828173841) [![Leia is rescued by Ben.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/85/Rescue-of-Leia-Part4.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/270?cb=20220828173841)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/85/Rescue-of-Leia-Part4.png/revision/latest?cb=20220828173841) 

Leia is rescued by Ben.

 

Leia and Kenobi were pursued by a seeker droid through the Fortress, just as the Fortress's alarms began to ring. Kenobi took out the pursuing seeker droid and stormtroopers with his lightsaber in the fortress' corridors, allowing him and Leia to flee into a tunnel. As Reva, a [Purge Trooper](/wiki/Purge_Trooper "Purge Trooper"), and stormtrooper reinforcements closed in on them, Kenobi deflected their blasts, sealing the blast door on their end of the tunnel. While Kenobi used the Force to delay a cracking window, Tala reunited with Leia. The Purge trooper and stormtroopers forced their way through the door and Kenobi released the broken window, causing the tunnel to flood and allowing the trio escape onto the other side of the tunnel after sealing the blast door. The three reached the main hangar, Kenobi hiding Leia under an Imperial greatcoat he decided to don.[[45]](#cite_note-Kenobi_Part_IV-45)

But before Leia, Tala, and Kenobi could escape, Reva and several Purge troopers and stormtroopers caught up with them, Reva motioning for the assembled Imperial soldiers to shoot them. Before the Imperials could carry out their execution, a pair of [T-47 airspeeders](/wiki/T-47_airspeeder "T-47 airspeeder") strafed the Imperial forces on the platform. Leia, Tala, and Kenobi took advantage of the chaos to flee. Path member [Sully Stark](/wiki/Sully_Stark "Sully Stark") landed her airspeeder and evacuated Leia, Tala, and Kenobi. On the ride back to Jabiim, Kenobi sat beside Leia, who extended a hand to her rescuer. But Leia's droid Lola beeped and glowed red, the Third Sister having put a tracker in it.[[45]](#cite_note-Kenobi_Part_IV-45)

#### Jabiim and escape[]

:   "*I'm going to need a ladder.*"
:   ―Leia Organa, to Roken[[47]](#cite_note-Kenobi_V-47)

Upon arrival to Jabiim, after being greeted by the relived refugees, Leia and Kenobi ran into [Haja Estree](/wiki/Haja_Estree "Haja Estree"). Kenobi quickly sent Leia off to Tala while he spoke with Roken about getting the princess back to Alderaan. Roken explained that he would help however he could, but only after he'd gotten his people to safety; they'd already held off on getting them to safety in order to rescue Leia. Kenobi agreed, promising they'd do anything they could to help.

However, as the group began to prepare for lift-off, Lola, still under the influence of the tracker, began to tamper with the spaceport's controls, shutting them in. Upon overhearing Roken and Kenobi discussing the impossibility of their crawling in the vents to find the source of the problem due to their size, Leia volunteered her assistance. Roken initially dismissed her, but Kenobi convinced him to give her a chance to help, instructing Estree to watch over her.

As the Empire closed in on them, Leia worked to find the source of the shutdown. Upon finding it, the corrupted Lola lunged at the stunned princess, who quickly caught the droid and removed the restraining bolt that had been affixed to and corrupted the droid. Afterwards, Leia quickly located the source of the issue and fixed it, leaving the ship free to escape.

 [![Battle of Jabiim occurs](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9d/LightEmUp-OWKpV.png/revision/latest?cb=20220720004743) [![Battle of Jabiim occurs](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9d/LightEmUp-OWKpV.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220720004743)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9d/LightEmUp-OWKpV.png/revision/latest?cb=20220720004743) 

Battle of Jabiim occurs

 

Understanding that Vader would allow his personal hate to overpower military logic, Kenobi decided to draw away the pursuing Imperials by leaving the freighter to catch Vader's attention. Although Organa was outraged that Kenobi was not keeping his word that they would stay together, the Jedi asked [Haja Estree](/wiki/Haja_Estree "Haja Estree") to bring her to Alderaan so he could confront Vader. Before Kenobi's departure, he met with her again to give her Tala's holster, but he did not give her the blaster due to her young age, which Organa quickly noticed. She also hid her droid Lola in the Jedi Master's robe to comfort him. Indeed, comforted upon noticing the droid after landing on a nearby [barren moon](/wiki/Unidentified_barren_moon "Unidentified barren moon"), Kenobi then [confronted](/wiki/Fight_on_a_barren_moon "Fight on a barren moon") Vader and drew on his memories of Organa and her secret twin to triumph over his former apprentice, whom he left beaten before returning to Tatooine in time to witness the redemption of Reva.[[46]](#cite_note-Kenobi_Part_VI-46)

#### Returning home[]

:   "*Princess Leia Organa, you are wise, discerning, kindhearted. These are qualities that came from your mother. But you are also passionate and fearless, forthright. And these are gifts from your father. Both were exceptional people who bore an exceptional daughter.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi, to Leia[[46]](#cite_note-Kenobi_Part_VI-46)

 [![Organa family say goodbye to Obi-Wan](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d9/AlderaSpaceport-OWKpVI.png/revision/latest?cb=20220805043315) [![Organa family say goodbye to Obi-Wan](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d9/AlderaSpaceport-OWKpVI.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/270?cb=20220805043315)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d9/AlderaSpaceport-OWKpVI.png/revision/latest?cb=20220805043315) 

Organa family say goodbye to Obi-Wan

 

At the same time, Organa was returned home to Alderaan. Despite missing Lola, Organa dressed herself the following day and included Tala's holster in her outfit, which her mother quickly noticed but approved of. Walking out to the landing pad on the impression they would be welcoming another family visit, she asked her father, who noticed her new outfit, whether they could change the way their rules operated, which Bail agreed to. To her joy, it was Kenobi and Lola who then stepped out onto the landing pad, returning Lola to Organa's care. After Leia suggested the Jedi get rest, Kenobi admitted to the girl that he had known her birth parents and promised her they had passed down their gifts to her. Asking her to keep their friendship a secret to protect them both, Kenobi and Organa shared a hug and bid farewell.[[46]](#cite_note-Kenobi_Part_VI-46)

The young Organa's adventure with Kenobi was her first experience dealing with the true realities of galactic life in the Imperial Era:[[48]](#cite_note-Insider_225-48) whereas she had been told the Empire existed to protect the galaxy,[[44]](#cite_note-Kenobi_Part_III-44) she had witnessed the day-to-day struggle of average citizens, the troubles brought on by piracy and corruption, and the crushing level of inhumanity displayed by Imperial agents. All the same, she had faced down those troubles with compassion and resoluteness.[[48]](#cite_note-Insider_225-48)

### Teenage years[]

#### Learning skills[]

Once warned to stay away from [Wilhuff Tarkin](/wiki/Wilhuff_Tarkin "Wilhuff Tarkin") by her father, the [Grand Moff](/wiki/Grand_Moff "Grand Moff") made an official visit to Alderaan when she was thirteen. Leia crept along the halls of the palace behind the two men, listening to their cold, tense conversation. During the occasion, she realized he was nothing more than a merciless murderer and [slaver](/wiki/Slavery "Slavery").[[34]](#cite_note-TPtSatFB-34)

 [![The young princess developed combat skills and was fluent in several languages.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6f/PrincelyLessons-PrincessLeia2.png/revision/latest?cb=20150506000735) [![The young princess developed combat skills and was fluent in several languages.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6f/PrincelyLessons-PrincessLeia2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150506000735)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6f/PrincelyLessons-PrincessLeia2.png/revision/latest?cb=20150506000735) 

The young princess developed combat skills and was fluent in several languages.

 

Leia followed her adoptive father's footsteps into politics, becoming a [junior legislator](/wiki/Junior_legislator "Junior legislator") by the age of fourteen.[[13]](#cite_note-Bloodline-13) On Leia's first trip to [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant")[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14) in [5 BBY](/wiki/5_BBY "5 BBY"),[[49]](#cite_note-Coruscant_Date-49) to serve as an aide to her father, she had flown with her father there on the royal [yacht](/wiki/Yacht "Yacht") *[Polestar](/wiki/Polestar "Polestar")* where Bail pointed out landmarks making legendary places become real to her at last. Despite having grown up in palaces, Leia, like nearly everyone else, was overwhelmed by seeing the bustle and brilliance of Coruscant for the first time and Bail had laughed at her wide eyes.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

In Leia's teenage years, she learned to shoot with a [Drearian Defense Conglomerate](/wiki/Drearian_Defense_Conglomerate "Drearian Defense Conglomerate") [Defender sporting blaster pistol](/wiki/Defender_sporting_blaster_pistol "Defender sporting blaster pistol"), one often used by aristocrats of her social standing.[[50]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-50) Once she turned sixteen, Leia was allowed to receive some martial training with a personal instructor—her family had deemed necessary for her to learn the basics of self-defense, given her royal status and risk of abduction. She thoroughly enjoyed that training, which not only made her feel physically strong, but also allowed her to be released from the tension of her etiquette lessons. Thanks to her instructor, Leia learned to keep her mind clear and focused on the moment.[[34]](#cite_note-TPtSatFB-34) She was also taught how to ride, even becoming an Alderaanian junior champion in steeplechase.[[18]](#cite_note-Moving_Target-18)

On one occasion, Leia was sparring against one of her family's servants outside the city, instead of being in [language](/wiki/Language "Language") study, when her father picked her up. During their trip, she expressed her lack of enthusiasm in the politics her mother had to deal with, when the [Viceroy](/wiki/Viceroy "Viceroy") explained to her what Alderaan meant, and what she would have to do one day as its queen—to carry on the legacy of Alderaan's harmonic culture with pride, even at the expense of what she wanted.[[32]](#cite_note-PL2-32) Bail also told her tales of the Jedi, defenders of the old Republic; the young princess also overheard him talking of Darth Vader's [powers](/wiki/Force_power "Force power").[[34]](#cite_note-TPtSatFB-34)

#### Day of Demand[]

:   "*It is I, Leia Organa, princess of Alderaan. I come before you to hear you acknowledge that on this day it is known I have reached my sixteenth year.*"
:   ―Leia Organa[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

 [![Leia Organa's Day of Demand](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/24/DayofDemand-LeiaManga.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190518201131) [![Leia Organa's Day of Demand](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/24/DayofDemand-LeiaManga.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190518201131)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/24/DayofDemand-LeiaManga.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190518201131) 

Leia Organa's Day of Demand

 

Prior to her daughter's [Day of Demand](/wiki/Day_of_Demand "Day of Demand") Breha had an in-depth discussion with Leia about love and duty, bringing the [Rhindon Sword](/wiki/Rhindon_Sword "Rhindon Sword") with her which she placed on [Leia's bed](/wiki/Leia%27s_bedroom "Leia's bedroom"). Breha explained the significance of the Rhindon Sword, such as how she would attach it to Leia's waist on her wedding day, and reassured Leia that when the time came, she would get to choose her own spouse.[[51]](#cite_note-Princess_and_Scoundrel-51)

Shortly after her sixteenth birthday and on the sixteenth anniversary of her original Name Day, it was [Leia's Day of Demand](/wiki/Leia_Organa%27s_Day_of_Demand "Leia Organa's Day of Demand"), which marked the day that the heir to the throne of House Organa would claim their right to it, hosted in the palace [throne room](/wiki/Royal_Palace_of_Alderaan_throne_room "Royal Palace of Alderaan throne room"). Leia wore a white dress with a cape, a [silver](/wiki/Silver "Silver") headband with a [pearl](/wiki/Pearl "Pearl") charm and had her hair done in the complicated traditional style. The outfit had been a compromise with a simple white dress for Leia and bold silver jewellery for 2V. As she held the Rhindon Sword, Leia presented Bail and Breha with her challenges to test her body, heart, and mind and prove her worthy to become queen of Alderaan. Leia was to climb the [Appenza Peak](/wiki/Appenza_Peak "Appenza Peak"), represent Alderaan in the [Apprentice Legislature](/wiki/Apprentice_Legislature "Apprentice Legislature"), and undertake missions of charity and mercy to needy planets paying all cost from her share of the royal purse. Several senators were in attendance including [Mon Mothma](/wiki/Mon_Mothma "Mon Mothma") of [Chandrila](/wiki/Chandrila "Chandrila"). When the ceremony finished Leia curtsied towards her parents who beamed proudly before the guests started to crowd them Bail and Breha turned to greet them rather than congratulate Leia. Although Leia's distant cousin Lord [Mellowyn](/wiki/Mellowyn "Mellowyn") of [Birren](/wiki/Birren "Birren") told Leia that she was wonderful, Leia was still upset as she took this as confirmation of what she had suspected of the past six months, that her parents no longer cared and were ignoring her as they had begun ebbing away from her.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

Later that night, after 2V had left Leia's room as she was worried it put the princess in danger, Leia watched the thunderstorm outside, which she had recently discovered that she loved as she liked the wildness, the unpredictability and even the distant danger and she treasured it because it was one of the few things that she hadn't shared with her parents yet and belonged to her, from her window as she promised herself that the next day she would take up her next challenge and prove herself, doing something too great for her parents to ignored.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

 [![For her first mercy mission, Leia visited the planet Wobani.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ec/ChallengeoftheHeart-LeiaManga.png/revision/latest?cb=20190615042718) [![For her first mercy mission, Leia visited the planet Wobani.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ec/ChallengeoftheHeart-LeiaManga.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190615042718)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ec/ChallengeoftheHeart-LeiaManga.png/revision/latest?cb=20190615042718) 

For her first mercy mission, Leia visited the planet Wobani.

 

Shortly after the [Day of Demand](/wiki/Day_of_Demand "Day of Demand") ceremony, and three weeks before the next session of the Apprentice Legislature began, Leia undertook her first mission, where she traveled to [Wobani](/wiki/Wobani "Wobani") to assist the population that was still suffering from the effects of the [Commodities Enhancement Program](/wiki/Commodities_Enhancement_Program "Commodities Enhancement Program"). [Captain](/wiki/Captain "Captain") [Raymus Antilles](/wiki/Raymus_Antilles "Raymus Antilles") accompanied her onboard the [CR90 corvette](/wiki/CR90_corvette "CR90 corvette") *[Tantive IV](/wiki/Tantive_IV "Tantive IV")*. After distributing supplies to the starving population, Leia decided to take as many refugees as she could back to Alderaan with them. She and [Lieutenant](/wiki/Lieutenant "Lieutenant") [Ress Batten](/wiki/Ress_Batten "Ress Batten") spoke with Imperial [Major](/wiki/Major "Major") [Tedam](/wiki/Tedam "Tedam"), who told her that she was not allowed to help the refugees. Undeterred, Leia hired around one hundred refugees and transported them back to Alderaan.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

On their way back to Alderaan, the *Tantive IV* passed through the [Bryx sector](/wiki/Bryx_sector "Bryx sector"). Leia saw the damaged [Calderos Station](/wiki/Calderos_Station "Calderos Station"), but before she could figure out who attacked it, [TIE fighters](/wiki/TIE/ln_space_superiority_starfighter "TIE/ln space superiority starfighter") ordered them to leave the sector. Little did she know, rebel forces working for her father had [attacked](/wiki/Attack_on_Calderos "Attack on Calderos") the outpost. When she returned to Alderaan, Breha welcomed the refugees, bringing an entourage along to assist them, but demanded that Leia return with her to the palace.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

The two went to the royal family's private library where Breha lectured Leia on her actions on Wobani and not telling her parents about it. Breha told Leia that her actions ruined the work of Bail, Mothma and their allies in the senate to negotiate the relocation of the Wobani population. When Leia asked her about Calderos, she was warned not to go near dangerous places.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

#### Serving in the Apprentice Legislature and discovering a rebellion[]

:   "*For my Challenge of the Mind, I will no longer merely assist my father in the Imperial Senate but will also represent our world in the Apprentice Legislature.*"
:   ―Leia Organa[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

 [![Harp Allor being pulled on a travois.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d2/Travois-LeiaManga.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190728020354) [![Harp Allor being pulled on a travois.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d2/Travois-LeiaManga.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190728020354)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d2/Travois-LeiaManga.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190728020354) 

Harp Allor being pulled on a travois.

 

Leia joined the [Chandrilan Pathfinding Corps](/wiki/Chandrilan_Pathfinding_Corps "Chandrilan Pathfinding Corps") class led by [Chief](/wiki/Chief "Chief") [Pangie](/wiki/Pangie "Pangie") to train for her ascent of Appenza Peak. Her classmates were other Apprentice Legislators [Chassellon Stevis](/wiki/Chassellon_Stevis "Chassellon Stevis"), [Harp Allor](/wiki/Harp_Allor "Harp Allor"), [Sssamm Ashsssen](/wiki/Sssamm_Ashsssen "Sssamm Ashsssen"), [Amilyn Holdo](/wiki/Amilyn_Holdo "Amilyn Holdo"), and [Kier Domadi](/wiki/Kier_Domadi "Kier Domadi"), who also represented Alderaan. The class was organised by her mother who claimed it was to allow Leia to better get to know her fellow Apprentice Legislators, but Leia suspected that it was so that she didn't have to feel guilty about not spending time with her. As the class had been organised by Alderaan's queen the first lesson took place on Alderaan. Five hours later, the group came to a clearing where Pangie left the group on her [hoversled](/wiki/Hoversled "Hoversled") telling them that she would send help to anyone not back at the [chalet](/wiki/Pathfinding_class_chalet "Pathfinding class chalet") by nightfall but that they would be kicked out of the class. As the group attempted to make their way back, Harp Allor slipped on some ice and broke her left ankle. This caused the group to break into two with Leia being amongst those who chose to stay with Harp though Chassellon Stevis claimed that Leia only did so because her reputation would be ruined if it got out that she had left Harp. The remaining students bandaged Harp's ankle and made a [travois](/wiki/Travois "Travois") to help transport her. Holdo, with the help of Ashsssen, managed to make a [toboggan](/wiki/Toboggan "Toboggan") out of a [tent](/wiki/Tent "Tent") which allowed them to travel down the mountain. The group were drinking [mocoa](/wiki/Mocoa "Mocoa") at the chalet when Stevis' group arrived at sunset. The class would later practice on the [Rivoche Ranges](/wiki/Rivoche_Ranges "Rivoche Ranges") on the planet [Eriadu](/wiki/Eriadu "Eriadu") before traveling to Coruscant to participate in government matters.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

 [![At age sixteen, for her Challenge of the Mind, Leia represented her world in the Apprentice Legislature.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/76/ApprenticeLegislator-LeiaManga.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190728020838) [![At age sixteen, for her Challenge of the Mind, Leia represented her world in the Apprentice Legislature.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/76/ApprenticeLegislator-LeiaManga.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190728020838)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/76/ApprenticeLegislator-LeiaManga.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190728020838) 

At age sixteen, for her Challenge of the Mind, Leia represented her world in the Apprentice Legislature.

 

At the opening of the Apprentice Legislature, where Leia wore a high collar purple dress, the guest speaker was the recently promoted Wilhuff Tarkin who made a speech before the Apprentice Legislature speaking about the interest the then Senator Palpatine had taken in him when he was a student and the importance of the Apprentice Legislature in the wider Empire. Though Leia privately disapproved of his views of the Apprentice Legislature she still clapped along with the others as Tarkin stepped down from the dais.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

Later the Apprentice Legislature attended the reception that celebrated Tarkin's promotion to [Grand Moff](/wiki/Grand_Moff "Grand Moff") where Leia gravitated towards the people she'd met in her pathfinding class. When Leia realised that Harp's sponsor, [Winmey Lenz](/wiki/Winmey_Lenz "Winmey Lenz"), was in attendance she felt sadness at her father not being there. Tarkin greeted several of the Apprentice Legislators and was intrigued by Leia, noting her violation of Imperial rules on Wobani, and wondered if she would become a similar senator to her father.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

 [![In the first debate of the Apprentice Legislature, Leia successfully campaigned for Arreyel](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/29/Arreyel-LeiaManga.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190908024419) [![In the first debate of the Apprentice Legislature, Leia successfully campaigned for Arreyel](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/29/Arreyel-LeiaManga.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190908024419)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/29/Arreyel-LeiaManga.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190908024419) 

In the first debate of the Apprentice Legislature, Leia successfully campaigned for Arreyel

 

At the first proper session of the Apprentice Legislature Leia watched as the others introduced themselves and learnt that Stevis had an interest in buying and refurbishing antique speeders, Holdo had an interest in astrology and Domadi had taken part in Clone Wars reenactments. Leia introduced herself as well, mentioning her status as princess, but couldn't think of something personal to add like everyone else had so simply told everyone that she liked storms. Later, during a debate over the location of a new [Imperial Academy](/wiki/Imperial_Academy "Imperial Academy"), Leia successfully argued for the planet [Arreyel](/wiki/Arreyel "Arreyel") claiming that it was the planet that would best benefit from it.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

After making connections between hyperspace routes between Calderos Station and multiple nearby planets, and Arkanis, Leia attempted to discover the means of the attack on Calderos by investigating the mining world of [Crait](/wiki/Crait "Crait"). She and Batten traveled to the planet in the *Polestar*. Upon their arrival, Leia was immediately detained by a group of what appeared to be insurgents, but once they learned she was the Princess of Alderaan, they brought her to their campsite, where Leia discovered Bail was operating a [rebel base](/wiki/Crait_outpost "Crait outpost"). Leia was shocked to learn that her father was operating an underground rebel group and was responsible for the attack on Calderos Station. Bail was equally shocked that despite the erased data, his daughter was able to track him. Bail and his personal [diplomatic](/wiki/Diplomat "Diplomat") [cruiser](/wiki/Cruiser "Cruiser") *[Tantive III](/wiki/Tantive_III "Tantive III")* escorted the *Polestar* home, and Leia erased the data upon Bail's request. He and Breha, who also helped run their operation, forbid Leia to talk about or become involved with their anti-Imperial efforts as they believed not getting her involved was the best way to protect her.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

#### Humanitarian missions and meeting Panaka[]

:   "*No other Imperial authority will be able to seize control very soon. For a few days, or even a few weeks, maybe the queen of Naboo can be a true queen again.*"
:   ―Leia Organa, to Dalné after the assassination of Quarsh Panaka[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

 [![Leia meeting with Dalné at the secondary royal palace.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/34/SecondaryRoyalPalace-LeiaManga.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210612044255) [![Leia meeting with Dalné at the secondary royal palace.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/34/SecondaryRoyalPalace-LeiaManga.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210612044255)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/34/SecondaryRoyalPalace-LeiaManga.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210612044255) 

Leia meeting with Dalné at the secondary royal palace.

 

Continuing her humanitarian work, Leia and Batten traveled to [Onoam](/wiki/Onoam "Onoam"), one of [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo")'s [moons](/wiki/Moon "Moon"). While the *Polestar* hung in orbit Leia felt an unexpected pang as she looked at Naboo. Leia met with [Queen](/wiki/Monarch_of_Naboo "Monarch of Naboo") [Dalné](/wiki/Daln%C3%A9 "Dalné") at the [secondary royal palace](/wiki/Secondary_royal_palace "Secondary royal palace"), who welcomed the opportunity for Leia to try to fix the massive strikes by the local [workers](/wiki/Miner "Miner") who toiled in the [Onoam mines](/wiki/Onoam_mine "Onoam mine"). Leia met with [Brel Ti Vorne](/wiki/Brel_Ti_Vorne "Brel Ti Vorne"), a representative for the miners, to whom Leia gifted five hundred sets of supplies, each consisting of safety belts, atmosphere masks, portable force fields that can purify air, and other safety gear. However, Ti Vorne told Leia that they could not accept the gifts because their Imperial overseers had been confiscating their equipment and selling it for profit.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

An outraged Leia arranged to meet with [Moff](/wiki/Moff "Moff") [Quarsh Panaka](/wiki/Quarsh_Panaka "Quarsh Panaka"), who invited her and Queen Dalné to his [chalet](/wiki/Quarsh_Panaka%27s_chalet "Quarsh Panaka's chalet") to discuss the issue over [tea](/wiki/Tea "Tea"). After changing into the Naboo [jubilation dress](/wiki/Jubilation_dress "Jubilation dress") that was typically worn at times of rejoicing and for meeting officials for the first time. Once inside, Panaka greeted the pair but when his eyes turned to Leia they grew wide in shock and the tea from Panaka's cup began to splash onto the floor. The dress was worn previously by Amidala to celebrate the liberation of Naboo from the Trade Federation. Panaka noticed Leia looked like the late Queen Padmé Amidala, whom Panaka had been very close with.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

 [![Leia left the chalet of Moff Panaka mere minutes before his death.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/41/PanakaAssassination.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210701003256) [![Leia left the chalet of Moff Panaka mere minutes before his death.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/41/PanakaAssassination.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210701003256)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/41/PanakaAssassination.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210701003256) 

Leia left the chalet of Moff Panaka mere minutes before his death.

 

Panaka vowed to find the Imperial officials responsible, and then began to question Leia about her birth mother and father. When Leia revealed that she was almost exactly sixteen and adopted, knowing almost nothing about her birth parents, Panaka realized that she could be the Queen's daughter. Leia was confused, and a little uncomfortable, with Panaka's questions and left shortly after with Dalné but after a few steps outside the chalet a massive explosion destroyed the office, killing Panaka and throwing Leia and Dalné to the ground. Leia witnessed a miner in a breathing mask fleeing the scene. [Stormtroopers](/wiki/Stormtrooper "Stormtrooper") secured the area and treated Leia and Dalné for minor injuries.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

Upon her return to Alderaan, Leia attempted to find out if her parents were involved in [Panaka's death](/wiki/Strike_on_Onoam "Strike on Onoam"), an accusation that greatly angered her father, but Breha explained that the bombing was the work of an extremist group known as the [Partisans](/wiki/Partisans "Partisans") led by a man called [Saw Gerrera](/wiki/Saw_Gerrera "Saw Gerrera"). Breha also explained to Leia that Bail was reluctant to accept that the rebellion needed to be on a large scale to be successful, due to his experiences in the Clone Wars.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

Soon after, Leia undertook another diplomatic mission to the sickened world of [Chal Hudda](/wiki/Chal_Hudda "Chal Hudda"). As [diseases](/wiki/Disease "Disease") ravaged the [swampy](/wiki/Swamp "Swamp") planet, Leia delivered vaccines to the ailing population. The [Chalhuddan](/wiki/Chalhuddan "Chalhuddan") leader, [Occo Quentto](/wiki/Occo_Quentto "Occo Quentto"), at first refused the vaccines, but then agreed to take them by making a deal with Leia, wanting help not from 'saviors' but from equals. He agreed to do Leia a favor soon.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

Upon her return to Coruscant the next day, Leia would learn of the fate of Arreyel, the planet she lobbied to receive the next Imperial Academy. Imperial engineers had discovered a radiation source within the mantle of the planet, and Emperor Palpatine had given the population six weeks to evacuate without compensation so the energy could be used to power planet-wide Imperial factories. Compounding Leia's frustration, the Apprentice Legislatures received a special commendation for recommending Arreyel. A few days later Leia snuck into the passageways surrounding the palace's banquet hall, for the first time in years, where she overheard her parents and their allies discussing Panaka's death and weather to implore further violence into their plans.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

 [![Senator Mon Mothma became a friend and mentor to Leia](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/86/New_Senator_Mothma.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180712095757) [![Senator Mon Mothma became a friend and mentor to Leia](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/86/New_Senator_Mothma.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180712095757)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/86/New_Senator_Mothma.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180712095757) 

Senator Mon Mothma became a friend and mentor to Leia

 

Then, Leia and the [astromech droid](/wiki/Astromech_droid "Astromech droid") [R2-D2](/wiki/R2-D2 "R2-D2") brought relief to the planet [Chasmeene](/wiki/Chasmeene "Chasmeene"), which was suffering after being punished for failing to meet Imperial quotas. They brought food, seeds, and agricultural equipment to help restart the economy. Leia went a step further by collecting evidence to prove the Empire had committed crimes against the people of Chasmeene.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

Leia brought the information to Mon Mothma in [her office](/wiki/Mon_Mothma%27s_Senate_office "Mon Mothma's Senate office"), but Mothma explained that it did very little as most of the galaxy already knew that the Empire was evil. Mothma did reassure her however that once the Empire was defeated this type of evidence would be important and that she should pay attention to what was going on around her.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

#### First actions as a rebel[]

:   "*You're learning the most powerful lesson of all, my daughter. You're learning how to fall.*"
:   ―Breha Organa, to Leia, while climbing Appenza Peak[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

 [![Amilyn Holdo helped Leia rescue her father.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f0/Young_Amilyn_Holdo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20240402200913) [![Amilyn Holdo helped Leia rescue her father.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f0/Young_Amilyn_Holdo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20240402200913)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f0/Young_Amilyn_Holdo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20240402200913) 

Amilyn Holdo helped Leia rescue her father.

 

Leia would soon discover her parents were building a [fleet](/wiki/Rebel_Alliance_Navy "Rebel Alliance Navy") over the planet [Paucris Major](/wiki/Paucris_Major "Paucris Major"). Bail forced Leia to swear an oath of secrecy before she accompanied him to Coruscant to serve as his senatorial aide. During her duties, she once again ran into Grand Moff Tarkin, who had called her into his office. Tarkin pretended to show concern for her and bragged to Leia about Imperial security forces, including noting the Empire was trying to achieve peace in the Paucris System. Realizing Tarkin was telling her that they had discovered rebel forces in the system, Leia raced to warn her father, but when she was unable to contact him, she contacted Breha and Mon Mothma. After telling them, Mothma told Leia to go to Paucris Major and warn them of an impending attack. However, the *Polestar* was on Alderaan, so Mothma gave Leia [credits](/wiki/Galactic_Credit_Standard "Galactic Credit Standard") to hire a ship.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

Leia ran into Stevis and Holdo at the spaceport trying to hire the *[Mighty Oak Apocalypse](/wiki/Mighty_Oak_Apocalypse "Mighty Oak Apocalypse")* to take Stevis to a [speeder](/wiki/Speeder "Speeder") auction on [Arkanis](/wiki/Arkanis "Arkanis") and Holdo to Gatalenta to participate in a meditative retreat. Holdo, who knew of Leia's rebel connections, convinced Stevis to stay behind and allowed Leia to hire the *Mighty Oak Apocalypse* to travel to the planet [Pamarthe](/wiki/Pamarthe "Pamarthe"). Leia explained her mission to Holdo, who understood the importance of helping her friend and joined her. However, once they arrived on Pamarthe, they learned that a storm was preventing all ships from leaving the planet. Thinking fast, Leia found a Chalhuddan ship. She told them to contact Occo Quentto, who told his men to bring them to Paucris Major to repay his debt to her.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

They arrived in the Paucris System and Leia broadcast a message to the rebels, telling them that Tarkin had discovered them. The rebels began to [evacuate](/wiki/Evacuation_of_Paucris_Major "Evacuation of Paucris Major") their [base](/wiki/Rebel_base_(Paucris) "Rebel base (Paucris)") and initiated [self-destruct](/wiki/Self-destruct_mechanism "Self-destruct mechanism") protocols on the [orbital](/wiki/Orbit "Orbit") landers to destroy all evidence. As the ships began to jump away, Leia and Holdo were the only ones left to witness a concerned Domadi arriving in the system in a [starcutter](/wiki/Starcutter "Starcutter") civilian transport.
