Unfortunately, he landed at the platform, unaware that it was about to self-destruct. He was mortally wounded when the platforms exploded. Leia flew their ship over to save him, but it was too late. He died in Leia's arms, asking her to turn over the information he had gathered on the rebellion to the Empire, to put the needs of Alderaan above the rest of the galaxy. Then, an Imperial ship arrived, and Holdo pretended they were an astrological survey group, convincing the Imperials to let them go. Domadi was brought back to Alderaan, where his family was told that he died saving Leia from a small-craft accident in Alderaan's atmosphere. Leia swore to help her parents with their rebellion moving forward.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

Shortly after, Leia was officially [invested](/wiki/Coronation_of_the_Alderaanian_heir "Coronation of the Alderaanian heir") as crown princess of Alderaan. The night before, Leia gave her [keepsake chest](/wiki/Leia_Organa%27s_keepsake_chest "Leia Organa's keepsake chest") to her father to show that she had outgrown her use for it. Mon Mothma was present at the ceremony along with Batten, Holdo, and Stevis. Her father placed the [Heir's Crown](/wiki/Heir%27s_Crown "Heir's Crown") on her head and, as she looked at Alderaan through the stain glass windows of the throne room, she thought of how her friends, her parents and her world were things that the Empire could never take away from her.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

#### Relief mission to Lothal[]

:   "*But you're a Princess; you don't have to risk your life doing this!*"  
    "*I feel like because I can fight, I have to, for those who cannot. And I think you might be the same way.*"
:   ―Leia Organa and Ezra Bridger[[52]](#cite_note-A_Princess_on_Lothal-52)

 [![Princess Leia at the time of her visit to Lothal](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/50/PrincessLeia-SWR.png/revision/latest?cb=20221121011520) [![Princess Leia at the time of her visit to Lothal](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/50/PrincessLeia-SWR.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20221121011520)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/50/PrincessLeia-SWR.png/revision/latest?cb=20221121011520) 

Princess Leia at the time of her visit to Lothal

 

In 3 BBY,[[3]](#cite_note-Timelines-3) Organa, while serving as her father's [aide](/wiki/Aide "Aide") in the [Imperial Senate](/wiki/Imperial_Senate "Imperial Senate"), devised a plan to give the rebels three [*Sphyrna*-class Hammerhead corvettes](/wiki/Sphyrna-class_Hammerhead_corvette "Sphyrna-class Hammerhead corvette"), ostensibly by going on a relief mission on [Lothal](/wiki/Lothal "Lothal"), where the rebels would apparently steal the [ships](/wiki/Starship "Starship"). She was greeted by [Kanan Jarrus](/wiki/Kanan_Jarrus "Kanan Jarrus") and [Ezra Bridger](/wiki/Ezra_Bridger "Ezra Bridger"), who were respectively disguised as a stormtrooper and an [Imperial cadet](/wiki/Imperial_cadet "Imperial cadet"), as well as Lieutenant [Yogar Lyste](/wiki/Yogar_Lyste "Yogar Lyste"), who knew that Organa often had a large majority of her ships become "stolen" by rebel agents. Consequently, Lyste implemented stricter security measures against what he assumed was another "meddling delegation from Alderaan," ultimately complicating her plan to transfer the cruisers to the rebels by placing [gravity locks](/wiki/Gravity_lock "Gravity lock") on the ships, along with ordering two [AT-ATs](/wiki/All_Terrain_Armored_Transport "All Terrain Armored Transport") to guard them.[[52]](#cite_note-A_Princess_on_Lothal-52)

Organa then requested she use Lyste's [shuttle](/wiki/Sentinel-class_landing_craft "Sentinel-class landing craft"), and she flew with Jarrus and Bridger to former [Governor](/wiki/Governor "Governor") [Ryder Azadi](/wiki/Ryder_Azadi "Ryder Azadi")'s hideout. Upon arrival, they found stormtroopers had apprehended Ryder. The *[Ghost](/wiki/Ghost "Ghost")* appeared and opened fire: Jarrus, Bridger, and Organa feigned being taken hostage by Ryder and the crew. On board, Organa bonded with Bridger after learning he had recently lost his parents, assuaging his fears the rebellion might not be worth fighting. They then resolved to find a way to steal the corvettes.[[52]](#cite_note-A_Princess_on_Lothal-52)

Still disguised, Jarrus and Bridger used the *[Phantom](/wiki/Phantom "Phantom")* to escort Organa back to the depot, distracting a surprised Lyste while Ryder, [Sabine Wren](/wiki/Sabine_Wren "Sabine Wren"), and [C1-10P](/wiki/C1-10P "C1-10P") disabled the gravity locks and commandeered the ships. During the ensuing firefight, she saw Jarrus use his [lightsaber](/wiki/Kanan_Jarrus%27_lightsaber "Kanan Jarrus' lightsaber") to down an AT-AT, and Bridger use [telekinesis](/wiki/Telekinesis "Telekinesis") to disarm a pair of stormtroopers, which gave her the opportunity to grab one of the [rifles](/wiki/E-11_medium_blaster_rifle "E-11 medium blaster rifle") and use it against the troopers. When Bridger boarded the last corvette, she ordered him to make it appear they were struggling and [stun](/wiki/Stun "Stun") her. When Lyste came to her aid, she berated him for his failure, and requested a shuttle home, taunting Lyste for having lost his own.[[52]](#cite_note-A_Princess_on_Lothal-52)

After her mission to Lothal, Organa sent a classified communique to Mon Mothma, agreeing with General [Jan Dodonna](/wiki/Jan_Dodonna "Jan Dodonna")'s assessment that the nascent [Alliance to Restore the Republic](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic")'s strongest [starfighter](/wiki/Starfighter "Starfighter") assets would be the [X-wing starfighters](/wiki/X-wing_starfighter "X-wing starfighter"), [A-wings](/wiki/A-wing "A-wing"), [UT-60D U-wing starfighter/support crafts](/wiki/UT-60D_U-wing_starfighter/support_craft "UT-60D U-wing starfighter/support craft"), and [A/SF-01 B-wing starfighters](/wiki/A/SF-01_B-wing_starfighter "A/SF-01 B-wing starfighter"). She then informed Mothma of a potential manufacturer that would allow them to manufacture X-wings in secret, asserting that it would not be enough to steal ships for the Rebel Alliance Navy.[[53]](#cite_note-RebelStarfighters-53)

#### Bounty of trouble[]

:   "*Leia, you keep fighting on the inside. I'll keep fighting on the outside.*"  
    "*I hope one day we can fight together.*"
:   ―Sabine Wren and Leia Organa[[54]](#cite_note-Bounty_of_Trouble-54)

Sometime after the mission on Lothal,[[55]](#cite_note-Leia_Chronicles-55) Organa was escorted by two stormtroopers in [Garel City](/wiki/Garel_City "Garel City") on the planet [Garel](/wiki/Garel "Garel"). As the group passed a doorway, the [Mandalorian](/wiki/Mandalorian "Mandalorian") rebel Sabine Wren distracted the troopers with a yellow paint bomb and kidnapped the princess via a lasso. Before the stormtroopers realized what had happened, Wren shut the gate. Inside the gate, Sabine introduced herself to Leia and told her that she had been sent to "capture" her and collect a data tape valuable to the rebellion. Organa told Wren that she had hidden the data tape from the Empire to prevent the government from learning she was working with the rebellion.[[54]](#cite_note-Bounty_of_Trouble-54)

 [![Organa provided Sabine Wren with Imperial data tapes containing the locations of several military bases.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Leia_and_Sabine_-_FoD.png/revision/latest?cb=20170710115507) [![Organa provided Sabine Wren with Imperial data tapes containing the locations of several military bases.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Leia_and_Sabine_-_FoD.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170710115507)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Leia_and_Sabine_-_FoD.png/revision/latest?cb=20170710115507) 

Organa provided Sabine Wren with Imperial data tapes containing the locations of several military bases.

 

Meanwhile, the stormtroopers were using an [arc welder](/wiki/Arc_welder "Arc welder") to cut through the door. With their time running out, Organa and Wren retrieved the data tape from an interface unit, with Leia telling Sabine that the tape would provide the rebellion with the locations of several Imperial bases. Before they were allowed to escape, the droid [bounty hunter](/wiki/Bounty_hunter "Bounty hunter") [IG-88](/wiki/IG-88B "IG-88B") cornered them with a blaster. Wren detonated a second paint bomb and confused the bounty hunter. The duo returned to the blaster, with Wren hiding in a corner away from the stormtroopers. When the troopers managed to get through the door, Organa told them to defend her from IG-88. While the troopers and the droid bounty hunter exchanged fire, Leia and Sabine snuck outside. Organa handed Wren the data tape. Sabine thanked Leia before the princess headed back to the building, hoping that one day they could fight together.[[54]](#cite_note-Bounty_of_Trouble-54)

#### Imperial senator[]

:   "*It will be nice to have such a pretty face in the Senate.*"
:   ―Emperor Palpatine to Leia Organa[[34]](#cite_note-TPtSatFB-34)

 [![Though a member of the Imperial Senate, Organa secretly supported the Alliance to Restore the Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/90/Leia_Imperial_Senate.png/revision/latest?cb=20190313200457) [![Though a member of the Imperial Senate, Organa secretly supported the Alliance to Restore the Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/90/Leia_Imperial_Senate.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190313200457)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/90/Leia_Imperial_Senate.png/revision/latest?cb=20190313200457) 

Though a member of the Imperial Senate, Organa secretly supported the Alliance to Restore the Republic.

 

Leia eventually took her father's place in the Imperial Senate, becoming the youngest senator elected. Her aunts protested and argued that she'd be better off finding a prince for husband, whereas the press claimed she was a "princess playing dress-up" and not a real [diplomat](/wiki/Diplomat "Diplomat") and politician. Spending the days leading up to her election listing out her grievances, intent on addressing the [Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor") directly and bluntly, Leia was presented by her father to Emperor [Palpatine](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious") on [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant"), with all the newly elected officials. However, when she met the Imperial ruler, she was frightened by his disturbing aura of evil that she was left speechless and dropped into a half-curtsy. At some point, Organa met the Emperor's [apprentice](/wiki/Sith_apprentice "Sith apprentice") and enforcer, Darth Vader (both unaware that they were biological father and daughter) and dealt with him.[[34]](#cite_note-TPtSatFB-34) In her early days at the Senate, Organa discovered that betrayal always came from those who acted the friendliest.[[56]](#cite_note-HttJ-56)

Despite her sincere desire for real change and reform, Organa soon realized that no other senator seemed to share her ideals,[[34]](#cite_note-TPtSatFB-34) as the Senate had become a mere ceremonial institution that sycophantically validated Palpatine's every decree,[[57]](#cite_note-Tarkin-57) and no delegate ever dared test the Emperor's patience. Unable to understand how the other senators could ignore the Empire's crimes in the [Outer Rim Territories](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories"), Organa devoted herself to aid the suffering across the galaxy. On one occasion, she rescued an orphaned baby [Wookiee](/wiki/Wookiee "Wookiee") from the ruins of a village destroyed by Imperial forces. Yet, to her annoyance, the first question she was asked was who she was wearing, and the media continued to reduce her to the label of princess, paying no attention to her humanitarian work.[[34]](#cite_note-TPtSatFB-34)

 [![Leia served as Junior Senator of Alderaan.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/LeiaJuniorSenator.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20171006000323) [![Leia served as Junior Senator of Alderaan.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/LeiaJuniorSenator.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/100?cb=20171006000323)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/LeiaJuniorSenator.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20171006000323) 

Leia served as Junior Senator of Alderaan.

 

Eventually, Leia's leadership and diplomatic skills made the public come to care about her, enough that any whisper of mistreatment would "set the [HoloNet](/wiki/HoloNet "HoloNet") on fire."[[34]](#cite_note-TPtSatFB-34) During her tenure as an Imperial senator, Organa had to deal with the [Givin](/wiki/Givin "Givin"), a mathematically inclined species. At the time, she memorized a few equations that proved useful when she dealt with Givin and their custom of [greeting maths](/wiki/Greeting_maths "Greeting maths").[[56]](#cite_note-HttJ-56) At some point, she argued in favor of a bill that would tighten the labor rights of refugees, therefore keeping them safe from exploitation. The bill passed and cost chief operating officer for one of Coruscant's biggest manufacturing plats billions, eventually resulting in the COO putting a bounty out on Organa and fellow bill supporter Mon Mothma.[[51]](#cite_note-Princess_and_Scoundrel-51)

Eventually, Leia would join the [Alliance to Restore the Republic](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic"), seeing it as her chance to help the [galaxy](/wiki/Galaxy "Galaxy"), shortly before her [mission](/wiki/Secret_mission_to_Tatooine "Secret mission to Tatooine") to Tatooine.[[34]](#cite_note-TPtSatFB-34) [Weeks](/wiki/Standard_week "Standard week") before the mission, Organa attended a reception and ball at the [Imperial Palace](/wiki/Imperial_Palace "Imperial Palace"), like many other members of the Imperial Senate. This was just a few days after she delivered a speech in the Senate about increasing Alderaan's mercy missions to outlying systems the Empire had forgotten or neglected. Despite her popularity, her speech received mixed criticisms, as many in the Core Worlds believed that the Empire was already providing the necessary aid and that Alderaan's "meddling" was becoming too important. During the ball, Organa danced with [Imperial](/wiki/Imperial_Academy "Imperial Academy") [cadet](/wiki/Cadet "Cadet") [Thane Kyrell](/wiki/Thane_Kyrell "Thane Kyrell"); he, however, noticed she was paying little attention to him, likely because she was distracted and had a lot on her mind.[[58]](#cite_note-LS-58)

### Galactic Civil War[]

#### A diplomatic mission[]

:   "*Your Highness. The transmission we received. What is it they've sent us?"*  
    *"Hope.*"
:   ―Raymus Antilles and Leia Organa[[59]](#cite_note-Rogue_One-59)

 [![During the Battle of Scarif, Organa acquired the Death Star plans through the sacrifice of Rogue One.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f1/LeiaReceivesthePlans.png/revision/latest?cb=20170529223512) [![During the Battle of Scarif, Organa acquired the Death Star plans through the sacrifice of Rogue One.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f1/LeiaReceivesthePlans.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170529223512)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f1/LeiaReceivesthePlans.png/revision/latest?cb=20170529223512) 

During the Battle of Scarif, Organa acquired the Death Star plans through the sacrifice of Rogue One.

 

During the [Galactic Civil War](/wiki/Galactic_Civil_War "Galactic Civil War"), after the transference of the Alliance's headquarters from [Dantooine](/wiki/Dantooine "Dantooine") to [Yavin 4](/wiki/Yavin_4 "Yavin 4"), and a [battle](/wiki/Battle_of_Scarif "Battle of Scarif") for the [technical readout](/wiki/Death_Star_plans "Death Star plans") of the [Death Star](/wiki/DS-1_Orbital_Battle_Station "DS-1 Orbital Battle Station"),[[59]](#cite_note-Rogue_One-59) Organa volunteered for the mission to transport the plans, against the wishes of her father. He reluctantly allowed her to go but requested that she seek [General](/wiki/Jedi_General "Jedi General") Obi-Wan Kenobi on Tatooine after intercepting the plans.[[34]](#cite_note-TPtSatFB-34)

Originally Admiral [Raddus](/wiki/Raddus "Raddus") was intended to escort Organa to Tatooine to meet with Kenobi. Raddus's ship,[[60]](#cite_note-Absolutely_Everything_Updated_and_Expanded-60) the *[Profundity](/wiki/Profundity "Profundity")*,[[61]](#cite_note-R1_novel-61) however, was diverted to [Scarif](/wiki/Scarif "Scarif") once the fighting began.[[60]](#cite_note-Absolutely_Everything_Updated_and_Expanded-60) A squadron of Rebels calling themselves "[Rogue One](/wiki/Rogue_One "Rogue One")" managed to obtain the plans and beam them to Raddus' ship. The plans were copied onto a [datacard](/wiki/Datacard "Datacard") by a squadron of Rebel soldiers still on the *Profundity*, which had been disabled by the [*Imperial*-class Star Destroyer](/wiki/Imperial-class_Star_Destroyer "Imperial-class Star Destroyer") *[Devastator](/wiki/Devastator "Devastator")*. Darth Vader led a boarding party onto the ship and massacred the entire squadron, but not before a [fleet trooper](/wiki/Unidentified_fleet_trooper "Unidentified fleet trooper") handed the disc off to another man, [Toshma Jefkin](/wiki/Toshma_Jefkin "Toshma Jefkin"). He barely escaped Vader and got aboard the *Tantive IV*, which promptly detached from the *Profundity* and fled from the battle, setting a course for Tatooine with the plans for the superweapon. Vader, however, had spotted the Rebel ship and began tracking it to Tatooine,[[59]](#cite_note-Rogue_One-59) later issuing an **arrest-on-sight decree** for the capture of Organa.[[62]](#cite_note-Scum_&_Villainy-62)

Before jumping to lightspeed, Captain Antilles personally handed Senator Organa the datacard carrying the plans and asked her what they had been sent by the Rogue One squad; smiling, she replied with a simple enigmatic word: "hope." Minutes later, Leia learned from the ship's senior officers that the *Tantive IV*'s impaired hyperdrive was causing it to leave a residual energy signature which could allow the Empire to track the ship. To make matters worse, she also learned that the ship's weapons and shields were barely functional because of the attack on the *Profundity*, whose feedback had affected the *Tantive IV*. The [bosun](/wiki/Unidentified_Tantive_IV_bosun "Unidentified Tantive IV bosun") then informed Leia that the Empire had issued a priority red directive to stop all ships matching the description of a CR-90 corvette.[[63]](#cite_note-Raymus-63)

 [![Organa's ship was attacked by Vader's flagship, the Devastator.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/02/Devastatortantiveiv.png/revision/latest?cb=20201017104531) [![Organa's ship was attacked by Vader's flagship, the Devastator.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/02/Devastatortantiveiv.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20201017104531)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/02/Devastatortantiveiv.png/revision/latest?cb=20201017104531) 

Organa's ship was attacked by Vader's flagship, the *Devastator*.

 

The crew of the *Tantive* looked to the princess for guidance,[[63]](#cite_note-Raymus-63) believing that she would be able to lead them out of the tangled net they found themselves in.[[34]](#cite_note-TPtSatFB-34) After a brief exchange with Jefkin, a man visibly shaken by what he had seen aboard the *Profundity*, Organa and Captain Antilles shared a grim realization that Darth Vader himself was after them as well. At a quarter of a parsec from their destination, the motivator on the ship finally gave out, forcing them to rely on sublight speed for the rest of the journey to Tatooine. Before they could reach the planet, however, their ship was hit by a [Star Destroyer](/wiki/Star_Destroyer "Star Destroyer").[[63]](#cite_note-Raymus-63)

#### Captured by the Empire[]

:   "*I don't know what you're talking about. I'm a member of the Imperial Senate on a diplomatic mission to Alderaan.*"  
    "*You are part of the Rebel Alliance and a traitor. Take her away!*"
:   ―Leia Organa and Darth Vader[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)

As Organa and her ship approached Tatooine, Captain Antilles ordered the crew to fire back at the Star Destroyer, but their efforts were of little use;[[63]](#cite_note-Raymus-63) the *Devastator*, the ship that had hunted them from Scarif,[[64]](#cite_note-Bucket-64) had caught them in a tractor beam right above the planet. As [stormtroopers](/wiki/Stormtrooper "Stormtrooper") led by Darth Vader boarded the *Tantive IV*, Organa ran through the access hallways of the ship with the datacard in hand, desperate to find a way to deliver them to safety. Amid the shadowy corridors, she encountered R2-D2 and realized that the astromech could conceal the tapes.[[34]](#cite_note-TPtSatFB-34)

 [![With no way to escape Vader, Organa sent R2-D2 to deliver the Death Star plans to Obi-Wan Kenobi.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/52/Futureoftherebellion.png/revision/latest?cb=20201017185458) [![With no way to escape Vader, Organa sent R2-D2 to deliver the Death Star plans to Obi-Wan Kenobi.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/52/Futureoftherebellion.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20201017185458)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/52/Futureoftherebellion.png/revision/latest?cb=20201017185458) 

With no way to escape Vader, Organa sent R2-D2 to deliver the Death Star plans to Obi-Wan Kenobi.

 

Before she could instruct the droid of her plans, she was met by Antilles, who urgently requested that the senator flee in an [escape pod](/wiki/Escape_pod "Escape pod"). Organa, however, had other ideas and, after sharing a bittersweet goodbye with her old friend, ordered the captain to save as many members of the crew as he could.[[63]](#cite_note-Raymus-63) Alone with R2, she recorded a [message](/wiki/Hologram "Hologram") for [General](/wiki/General "General") Kenobi, begging him to return from exile to deliver the plans to her father on Alderaan. After finishing her message, the princess inserted the data card into the astromech and instructed him to take his own escape pod to Tatooine below. She then parted ways with R2 as his counterpart, the [protocol droid](/wiki/Protocol_droid "Protocol droid") [C-3PO](/wiki/C-3PO "C-3PO"), approached. Watching the droids as they scampered away, Organa drew [her blaster](/wiki/Satine%27s_Lament "Satine's Lament") and prepared to find her own way off the captured vessel.[[34]](#cite_note-TPtSatFB-34)

In another part of the ship, Antilles was captured and killed by Vader, who commanded his soldiers to hunt Organa down and bring her to him alive to get more info out of her.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) Retreating further into the access hallways, the princess found herself cornered by a squad of stormtroopers led by [TK-9091](/wiki/TK-9091 "TK-9091"), who spotted the visage of Organa's pale [white](/wiki/Color "Color") dress within the dark corridor. Hoping to buy time for R2 to escape, the senator blasted the trooper and attempted to run in the opposite direction,[[34]](#cite_note-TPtSatFB-34) but she was rendered unconscious by a [stun](/wiki/Stun "Stun") blast from [TK-4601](/wiki/Tarvyn_Lareka "Tarvyn Lareka") and collapsed to the floor. While she lay on the ground, the trooper, whose birth name was Tarvyn Lareka, pondered how a beautiful individual like the princess could coldly kill his Imperial comrades. As Organa came to, she attempted to resist against the stormtroopers, but Lareka forced her into a pair of [stuncuffs](/wiki/Stuncuffs "Stuncuffs") and threatened to blast her again. Before she was escorted to Vader, Lareka spontaneously removed his [helmet](/wiki/Stormtrooper_armor "Stormtrooper armor") and locked eyes with Organa, reminding her that the troopers she fought were flesh and blood. However, this act also reminded Lareka of this fact as well.[[64]](#cite_note-Bucket-64)

 [![Leia Organa stood defiant against Darth Vader, refusing to let the hidden plans fall back into the Empire's hands.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/76/Vader_spots_a_continuity_error.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200608114422) [![Leia Organa stood defiant against Darth Vader, refusing to let the hidden plans fall back into the Empire's hands.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/76/Vader_spots_a_continuity_error.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20200608114422)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/76/Vader_spots_a_continuity_error.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200608114422) 

Leia Organa stood defiant against Darth Vader, refusing to let the hidden plans fall back into the Empire's hands.

 

The other soldiers shoved her back through the main corridors and past the lifeless bodies of the rebels who had died defending the princess, including Antilles.[[34]](#cite_note-TPtSatFB-34) She was brought before Vader, who had witnessed the *Tantive*'s escape from Scarif.[[59]](#cite_note-Rogue_One-59) Even still, Organa defiantly feigned ignorance of the Sith Lord's accusations, refusing to acknowledge that she had any part in the theft of the plans. Growing angry with the fiery senator, Vader ordered her to be taken aboard the *Devastator* and commanded his subordinate [Daine Jir](/wiki/Daine_Jir "Daine Jir") to inform the Senate that Organa and the other passengers had mysteriously died.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)

Once aboard the Star Destroyer, Leia managed to incapacitate her stormtrooper escorts and make her way to a [hangar](/wiki/Hangar "Hangar"), hoping to take a [shuttle](/wiki/Shuttle "Shuttle") and flee to Tatooine. Vader, however, had anticipated Organa's moves and met her in the landing bay. After stunning the princess by informing her that the Imperial Senate had been [dissolved](/wiki/Dissolution_of_the_Imperial_Senate "Dissolution of the Imperial Senate"), the Sith Lord brought her to the ship's command bridge. As the Destroyer exited hyperspace, Organa was able to see the Death Star in person for the first time as Vader promised that she would be its first "guest."[[34]](#cite_note-TPtSatFB-34) Organa's presence aboard the Death Star was kept a secret to all except for those who needed to know.[[65]](#cite_note-End_of_Watch-65)

#### Princess of dust[]

:   "*I grow tired of asking this, so it will be the last time. Where is the rebel base?*"  
    "*Dantooine. They're on Dantooine.*"  
    "*There.* […] *Continue with the operation. You may fire when ready.*"
:   ―Wilhuff Tarkin and Leia Organa[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)

The captive princess was transported to the Death Star and escorted to [Detention Block AA-23](/wiki/Detention_Block_AA-23 "Detention Block AA-23"). Her presence as a [prisoner](/wiki/Prisoner "Prisoner") aboard the station was questioned by the officers who recognized her as an Imperial Senator, a designation that should have granted her diplomatic immunity. Nevertheless, Organa was locked away in [Cell 2187](/wiki/Cell_2187 "Cell 2187"), a small room that she unsuccessfully attempted to find an escape from. Although he technically had no proof that the princess was affiliated with the Rebel Alliance, Vader was more than certain of her deception and returned to her cell with an [IT-O Interrogation Unit](/wiki/IT-O_interrogation_droid "IT-O interrogation droid"), an [interrogator droid](/wiki/Interrogation_droid "Interrogation droid") equipped with a powerful [mind probe](/wiki/Mind_probe "Mind probe"). Organa was submitted to the droid's truth serum, a drug that painfully altered her senses to coerce her into revealing the location of the Rebel base. Despite the persuasive hallucinations elicited by the serum, however, Leia resisted and refused to give up the information.[[34]](#cite_note-TPtSatFB-34)

 [![Organa stood defiantly against Tarkin's intimidation.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f2/StandingUpToTyranny-SWCT.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20251025210544) [![Organa stood defiantly against Tarkin's intimidation.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f2/StandingUpToTyranny-SWCT.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20251025210544)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f2/StandingUpToTyranny-SWCT.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20251025210544) 

Organa stood defiantly against Tarkin's intimidation.

 

Following her interrogation, Organa's life was scheduled to be terminated by the man she had met years ago, Grand Moff Tarkin, though the governor had one more tool to make her talk: Alderaan.[[34]](#cite_note-TPtSatFB-34) Within the [overbridge](/wiki/Overbridge_(Death_Star_I) "Overbridge (Death Star I)") of the Death Star, Organa was brought before Tarkin,[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) whom she mocked by imitating his accent.[[13]](#cite_note-Bloodline-13) To Organa's horror, he then gave her an ultimatum, threatening to use the station to destroy her [homeworld](/wiki/Homeworld "Homeworld") unless she disclosed the base's location. Hoping to save both her people and her Alliance, the princess falsely confessed that the [base](/wiki/Dantooine_base "Dantooine base") was still on Dantooine.[[34]](#cite_note-TPtSatFB-34) Both Tarkin and Vader believed her deception, although [one](/wiki/Unidentified_Imperial_Navy_Trooper_(Leia_Organa) "Unidentified Imperial Navy Trooper (Leia Organa)") of the [Navy Troopers](/wiki/Imperial_Navy_Trooper "Imperial Navy Trooper") present on the bridge sensed that Organa was lying. That individual, however, chose not to speak up after sympathizing with the pain the princess had endured under the interrogator droid.[[66]](#cite_note-Change_of_Heart-66)

With the weapon already in position within the [Alderaan system](/wiki/Alderaan_system "Alderaan system"), Tarkin unveiled his own deception and fired upon the planet.[[66]](#cite_note-Change_of_Heart-66) Praying that the Death Star would somehow have a failure,[[67]](#cite_note-A_New_Hope_-_The_Film_Novel-67) Leia was forced by Vader to remain still and watch as her entire civilization was [annihilated](/wiki/Destruction_of_Alderaan "Destruction of Alderaan") in one swift stroke,[[66]](#cite_note-Change_of_Heart-66) her father[[68]](#cite_note-Eclipse-68)—whom she silently apologized to as the Death Star's ray hit Alderaan[[67]](#cite_note-A_New_Hope_-_The_Film_Novel-67)—and mother included. Bail and Breha died without knowing Leia[[68]](#cite_note-Eclipse-68) was on the station above them,[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) although they assured each other she was alive directly before the explosion reached their palace.[[68]](#cite_note-Eclipse-68)

After Admiral [Conan Antonio Motti](/wiki/Conan_Antonio_Motti "Conan Antonio Motti") confirmed the entire world had been destroyed, Tarkin ordered Organa be taken back to her cell, ignoring her protests. Escorted by stormtroopers, Navy troopers, and Vader himself, Organa left the room silently[[69]](#cite_note-Age_of_Rebellion_Tarkin-69) but felt emotionally wrecked and utterly alone. The princess was taken back to her cell, where she was to await her imminent execution. Recalling her father's voice, Leia mustered what strength she could, her only hope of justice resting within the memory banks of a droid she had sent to Tatooine.[[34]](#cite_note-TPtSatFB-34)

#### Fateful meeting and daring escape[]

:   "*What the hell are you doing?*"  
    "*Somebody has to save our skins. Into the garbage chute, flyboy.*"
:   ―Han Solo and Leia Organa, as the latter blasts a hole in the trash grate[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)

 [![Leia was aided by Luke Skywalker and Han Solo; the trio would go on to change the galaxy forever.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/Leiadeathstar.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20071008054722) [![Leia was aided by Luke Skywalker and Han Solo; the trio would go on to change the galaxy forever.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/Leiadeathstar.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20071008054722)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/Leiadeathstar.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20071008054722) 

Leia was aided by Luke Skywalker and Han Solo; the trio would go on to change the galaxy forever.

 

While Organa was detained by the Empire, the droids R2-D2 and C-3PO had come under the possession of her twin brother, Luke Skywalker, on Tatooine. Equally as unaware of his parentage as Leia, Skywalker discovered his sister's message and delivered the astromech to Obi-Wan Kenobi, now going by the name of "Ben." The group hired the [smugglers](/wiki/Smuggler "Smuggler") [Han Solo](/wiki/Han_Solo "Han Solo") and [Chewbacca](/wiki/Chewbacca "Chewbacca") for passage to Alderaan aboard the *[Millennium Falcon](/wiki/Millennium_Falcon "Millennium Falcon")* but were stunned to learn that the planet had been blown away. During this discovery, the *Falcon* was captured by the Empire and taken aboard the Death Star, forcing the fugitives to infiltrate the base, split up, and plan an escape. Upon learning that the princess was held within the station, however, Skywalker convinced the party to lead a [rescue mission](/wiki/Rescue_of_Princess_Leia "Rescue of Princess Leia") for her.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)

Disguising themselves as stormtroopers and pretending to take Chewbacca as their prisoner, Skywalker and Solo marched into the [Detention Level](/wiki/Detention_Level "Detention Level") and freed Organa, who was underwhelmed by the duo's efforts until she learned that Kenobi had accompanied them. Cut off from the cell bay's exit by Imperial soldiers, Leia took matters into her own hands; grabbing hold of Skywalker's [blaster rifle](/wiki/Blaster_rifle "Blaster rifle"), she shot out the cover of a trash chute[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) she had noticed when she was first brought aboard[[34]](#cite_note-TPtSatFB-34) and led her would-be rescuers down into a [garbage pit](/wiki/Garbage_masher_3263827 "Garbage masher 3263827"). After surviving an encounter with a [dianoga](/wiki/Omi "Omi") and narrowly avoiding being crushed by the [trash compactor](/wiki/Garbage_compactor "Garbage compactor"), Organa came at odds with Captain Solo's rough nature and informed the trio that they would do as she told them in the future. The rebels were nearly able to regroup aboard the *Falcon*—a ship that failed to impress the princess—when Leia and Luke were separated from the group by stormtroopers during their escape.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)

 [![Solo tells Organa that he's only helping her for the money.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a3/InItForTheMoney-SWZ85.png/revision/latest?cb=20210228065438) [![Solo tells Organa that he's only helping her for the money.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a3/InItForTheMoney-SWZ85.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/270?cb=20210228065438)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a3/InItForTheMoney-SWZ85.png/revision/latest?cb=20210228065438) 

Solo tells Organa that he's only helping her for the money.

 

Pursued by Vader's troops, the twins found themselves at a dead end, coming to a stop over a chasm within the battle station. With stormtroopers firing upon them and no way to extend the bridge, Leia gave Luke a kiss on the cheek for luck as he used a [grappling hook](/wiki/Grappling_hook "Grappling hook") to swing themselves across the gap. The two met up again with Solo and Chewbacca and made their way to the *Falcon*. As the group boarded the [freighter](/wiki/Freighter "Freighter"), Kenobi engaged Darth Vader in a [lightsaber duel](/wiki/Lightsaber_duel "Lightsaber duel") and gave his life to allow for the princess and the others to escape.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)

The old Jedi's death devastated Luke, prompting Leia—who had herself experienced terrible loss— to comfort him as Solo piloted the ship away from the Death Star. After fending off the station's sentry fighters, the ship made the jump to hyperspace mostly undamaged. Organa correctly assumed that the Empire had planted a [homing beacon](/wiki/Homing_beacon "Homing beacon") on the vessel to discover the rebel base. Nevertheless, the group continued to Yavin 4, finally delivering the Death Star plans within R2 to the Alliance.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)

#### Battle of Yavin[]

:   "*You're safe. When we heard about Alderaan, we feared the worst.*"  
    "*We've no time for our sorrows, Commander. You must use the information in this R2 unit to help plan the attack. It's our only hope.*"
:   ―General Vanden Willard and Leia Organa[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)

Arriving at the [Yavin](/wiki/Yavin_Prime "Yavin Prime") moon, Organa oversaw R2's transfer to General [Vanden Willard](/wiki/Vanden_Huyck_Willard "Vanden Huyck Willard") at the [Great Temple](/wiki/Great_Temple "Great Temple"), the Alliance's base of operations. While Willard was quick to express his joy that the princess had escaped tragedy on Alderaan, Organa allowed no time for sorrow and quickly moved to have the data within the astromech droid analyzed. Utilizing the beacon attached to the *Millennium Falcon*, the Death Star entered the [Yavin system](/wiki/Yavin_system "Yavin system") and began preparations to fire on the moon.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) Rumors made their way through the Rebel flight crews that Organa had returned with vital intelligence on the station, but morale remained low; pilots like [Dex Tiree](/wiki/Dex_Tiree "Dex Tiree") felt that the Rebellion's meager troopers were greatly outmatched, even with the plans the princess had secured.[[70]](#cite_note-Sparks-70) Short on manpower, Organa commended Skywalker for his skills, prompting Willard to arrange a [flight simulator](/wiki/Flight_simulator "Flight simulator") test for the farm boy and allowing him to join the Alliance's [Starfighter Corps](/wiki/Rebel_Alliance_Starfighter_Corps "Rebel Alliance Starfighter Corps").[[34]](#cite_note-TPtSatFB-34)

After analyzing R2's schematics, the Alliance discovered a flaw in the Death Star's design[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) deliberately created by the turncoat [scientist](/wiki/Scientist "Scientist") [Galen Erso](/wiki/Galen_Walton_Erso "Galen Walton Erso").[[59]](#cite_note-Rogue_One-59) General [Jan Dodonna](/wiki/Jan_Dodonna "Jan Dodonna") briefed Organa and the rest of the Rebellion, explaining that a direct hit on one of the station's [thermal exhaust ports](/wiki/Thermal_exhaust_port "Thermal exhaust port") would destroy the entire base. With this information, the rebel pilots prepared to attack the Death Star in [X-wing starfighters](/wiki/T-65B_X-wing_starfighter "T-65B X-wing starfighter"), small [snub-fighters](/wiki/Snub-fighter "Snub-fighter") that could evade the station's larger defenses. During the preparations, Organa arranged for Solo to be paid the reward he demanded for her rescue and allowed the smuggler to leave, despite Skywalker's protests. Organa remained in the Alliance's command center as [Red](/wiki/Red_Squadron_(Rebel_Alliance) "Red Squadron (Rebel Alliance)"), [Gold](/wiki/Gold_Squadron_(Rebel_Alliance) "Gold Squadron (Rebel Alliance)"),[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) and [Green Squadrons](/wiki/Green_Squadron_(Rebel_Alliance) "Green Squadron (Rebel Alliance)") engaged the Death Star in the [Battle of Yavin](/wiki/Battle_of_Yavin "Battle of Yavin").[[70]](#cite_note-Sparks-70)

 [![Organa monitored the Battle of Yavin from the Alliance's headquarters.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/50/Massassi_Station_Opcenter.png/revision/latest?cb=20201017103701) [![Organa monitored the Battle of Yavin from the Alliance's headquarters.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/50/Massassi_Station_Opcenter.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20201017103701)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/50/Massassi_Station_Opcenter.png/revision/latest?cb=20201017103701) 

Organa monitored the Battle of Yavin from the Alliance's headquarters.

 

Organa watched as the Alliance pilots were picked off one by one, obliterated by TIE fighters. Darth Vader himself would have destroyed Skywalker had it not been for Solo, who returned to aid the Rebellion aboard the *Falcon* and blasted [Vader's fighter](/wiki/Darth_Vader%27s_TIE_Advanced "Darth Vader's TIE Advanced") away from the battle. With no obstacles in his way, Skywalker successfully destroyed the Death Star just as it began its firing sequence,[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) sending the personnel on Yavin 4 into celebration. In the moments after their victory, Alliance chief [mechanic](/wiki/Technician "Technician") [Nera Kase](/wiki/Nera_Kase "Nera Kase") witnessed the princess mouth words up to the sky before rushing out to greet the returning pilots.[[71]](#cite_note-grounded-71)

#### Aftermath of the Disaster[]

:   "*The mourning is endless: my father, my mother, my friends, my city, my world. Every time I fail, I fail them. And no victory is great enough to bring them back.*"
:   ―Leia [decades](/wiki/Standard_decade "Standard decade") later writing her thoughts about the Disaster after she received *[the Rebel Files](/wiki/The_Rebel_Files "The Rebel Files")*[[72]](#cite_note-Star_Wars:_The_Rebel_Files-72)

 [![Princess Leia honored Luke Skywalker and Han Solo for their part in the Death Star's destruction.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/83/Sw4-Leia2.png/revision/latest?cb=20201017103020) [![Princess Leia honored Luke Skywalker and Han Solo for their part in the Death Star's destruction.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/83/Sw4-Leia2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20201017103020)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/83/Sw4-Leia2.png/revision/latest?cb=20201017103020) 

Princess Leia honored Luke Skywalker and Han Solo for their part in the Death Star's destruction.

 

After the surviving [Rebel pilots](/wiki/Rebel_pilot "Rebel pilot") returned from successfully turning the Empire's greatest weapon into nothing but a layer of dust orbiting Yavin,[[73]](#cite_note-DV1-73) the personnel of the Yavin 4 base honored the heroes by orchestrating an [award ceremony](/wiki/Royal_Award_Ceremony "Royal Award Ceremony") for them.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) As Organa waited for them to enter the hall, she felt entirely alone, even with other Alderaanians present that shared her loss of their world. With Alderaan destroyed and her parents with it, she would never become the queen her parents had prepared her to be. She was already prepared for a long war as ruling a planet and running a rebellion had much in common. She would not let her grief stop her, and she would celebrate their victory. When she saw the Heroes of the Rebellion enter the hall, she did not feel so alone.[[33]](#cite_note-Queen's_Peril-33) Organa, wearing an Alderaanian gown,[[74]](#cite_note-Costumes-74) handed out the medals to newcomers Skywalker and Solo.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)

The time for celebration would soon be over. Painfully aware of the loss of Alderaan, she asked the Rebels to take a moment of silence to honor and remember all those who had died when her homeworld was destroyed. It was brief, for Dodonna announced their need to [evacuate](/wiki/Evacuation_of_Yavin_4 "Evacuation of Yavin 4") Yavin 4 since the Empire now knew of their location. Organa then shared a moment of banter with Solo and a moment of rapport with Skywalker before they parted ways. Left alone, Organa noticed a lone female [pilot](/wiki/Pilot "Pilot") paying respects to the memorial statue of her parents, Bail and Breha.[[75]](#cite_note-PL1-75)

#### Hunted by the Empire[]

:   "*I am sorry my Queen.*"  
    "*Don't address me that w—*"  
    "*It must be, my test will come soon. As we speak the Imperial are hunting down all surviving Alderaanians.*"  
    "*All? How do you know?*"  
    "*Word travels through the Rebel forces too much to be simply rumor.*"
:   ―Evaan Verlaine and Leia Organa[[75]](#cite_note-PL1-75)

 [![Evaan Verlaine informed Organa about rumors regarding the Empire's hunt for all remaining Alderaanians.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9b/LeiaEvaanYavin-PrincessLeia1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150322044243) [![Evaan Verlaine informed Organa about rumors regarding the Empire's hunt for all remaining Alderaanians.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9b/LeiaEvaanYavin-PrincessLeia1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150322044243)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9b/LeiaEvaanYavin-PrincessLeia1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150322044243) 

Evaan Verlaine informed Organa about rumors regarding the Empire's hunt for all remaining Alderaanians.

 

Afterwards, Organa changed into a less luxurious outfit and asked [Admiral](/wiki/Admiral "Admiral") [Gial Ackbar](/wiki/Gial_Ackbar "Gial Ackbar") to have an audience with Dodonna. The [Mon Calamari](/wiki/Mon_Calamari "Mon Calamari") pointed her in the right direction, and she approached Dodonna, who was busy searching for a location for the new Rebel base. She informed him that she yearned to assist, to scout for a new base location, but the General disagreed by telling her that the best thing for her to do at the time was to grieve her recent loss, given that the Empire had placed a 10,000,000 [credit](/wiki/Galactic_Credit_Standard "Galactic Credit Standard") [bounty](/wiki/Bounty "Bounty") on her just hours before, he stated the Princess would not leave Yavin "under anything less than a full military escort" and dismissed her.[[75]](#cite_note-PL1-75)

Defeated, she left and again briefly ran into Ackbar, but they quickly parted ways.[[75]](#cite_note-PL1-75) She continued to assist in the evacuation, but then she received word from Lieutenant [Caluan Ematt](/wiki/Caluan_Ematt "Caluan Ematt"), leader of the [Shrikes](/wiki/Shrikes "Shrikes")—who was alone after the death of his team, and on the run from the [Imperial Security Bureau](/wiki/Imperial_Security_Bureau "Imperial Security Bureau"). Organa then asked Solo to run an errand for the Rebellion, and rescue Ematt from [Cyrkon](/wiki/Cyrkon "Cyrkon"). Ultimately, Solo accepted the mission, and he and Chewbacca [rescued](/wiki/Cyrkon_Extraction "Cyrkon Extraction") Ematt with the *Falcon*.[[76]](#cite_note-Smuggler's_Run-76)

Organa then focused on the evacuation effort once again, when she met the Rebel pilot from earlier, [Evaan Verlaine](/wiki/Evaan_Verlaine "Evaan Verlaine"), who revealed that the Empire was rumored to be hunting all surviving [Alderaanians](/wiki/Alderaanian "Alderaanian") throughout the galaxy. Now aware of her people's situation, she enlisted both Verlaine and R2-D2's help for a self-imposed [mission](/wiki/Mission_to_rescue_the_survivors_of_Alderaan "Mission to rescue the survivors of Alderaan") to save the survivors of Alderaan. With the astromech, she recorded a decoy hologram of herself, and sent it to Dodonna's quarters during the night, to apologize for disobeying his orders. Meanwhile, the trio made their escape from Yavin on a [T-1 shuttle](/wiki/Jan_Dodonna%27s_T-1_shuttle "Jan Dodonna's T-1 shuttle"), but as they departed, their [shuttle](/wiki/T-1_shuttle_(Rebel_Alliance) "T-1 shuttle (Rebel Alliance)") was pursued by Skywalker and [Wedge Antilles](/wiki/Wedge_Antilles "Wedge Antilles") on their [X-wing starfighters](/wiki/T-65B_X-wing_starfighter "T-65B X-wing starfighter").[[75]](#cite_note-PL1-75)

 [![Princess Leia confronted Lord Junn, a friend of the House of Organa, after he betrayed her.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f6/LeiaConfrontsJunn-PrincessLeia2.png/revision/latest?cb=20170917112034) [![Princess Leia confronted Lord Junn, a friend of the House of Organa, after he betrayed her.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f6/LeiaConfrontsJunn-PrincessLeia2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170917112034)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f6/LeiaConfrontsJunn-PrincessLeia2.png/revision/latest?cb=20170917112034) 

Princess Leia confronted Lord Junn, a friend of the House of Organa, after he betrayed her.

 

Nevertheless, Verlaine outsmarted them and made the jump to Naboo,[[75]](#cite_note-PL1-75) and landed on its [capital](/wiki/Capital "Capital"), [Theed](/wiki/Theed "Theed"). Posing as Imperial [auditors](/wiki/Auditor "Auditor"), they came across a mural of the late Padmé Amidala (who unbeknownst to her, was her biological mother), and Organa momentarily saw the images' head turn to look at her, in what she dismissed as an illusion. They were soon approached by Lord [Junn](/wiki/Junn "Junn"), her old friend, who invited them to [his villa](/wiki/Junn%27s_palace "Junn's palace"). Organa requested that Junn arrange their meeting with [Mul Sanaka](/wiki/Mul_Sanaka "Mul Sanaka"), owner of [Club Deeja](/wiki/Club_Deeja "Club Deeja") in [Keren](/wiki/Keren "Keren"), and employer of the [Melodic Order](/wiki/Melodic_Order "Melodic Order")—the cloister of Alderaanian [musicians](/wiki/Musician "Musician") they were looking for. When he did so, Organa, Verlaine, and R2-D2 made their way to the club and met Sanaka, with whom they tried to negotiate over the Alderaanians.[[32]](#cite_note-PL2-32)

However, Sanaka and his [Besalisk](/wiki/Besalisk "Besalisk") guards tried to capture them, already aware of her identity. As Organa and her companions resisted, Sanaka attempted to kill her, foiled only by the intervention of [Uwa Pareece](/wiki/Uwa_Pareece "Uwa Pareece"), the Melodic Order's leader, who had been discreetly following the princess. Organa then had her lead them to the Order, whom she invited to follow her on her crusade. Once they agreed, Organa returned to Junn's palace, and made him explain why he had betrayed them to Sanaka. Finally, Organa demanded a [luxury yacht](/wiki/Luxury_yacht "Luxury yacht") with enough capacity to relocate the Melodic Order, and he agreed to give her the *[Lord Junn](/wiki/Lord_Junn "Lord Junn")*. Soon thereafter, the gathered Alderaanians departed for [Sullust](/wiki/Sullust "Sullust") in the Outer Rim.[[32]](#cite_note-PL2-32)

#### Alderaan's survival[]

:   "*We're not our enemy. We are Alderaan. We answer rage with wisdom. We answer fear with imagination. We answer war with hope. If one life with a single drop of Alderaanian blood survives, Alderaan survives. If one life with passion for Alderaanian creativity survives, Alderaan survives. And we are, each of us, important. And whatever happens, I bow to all of you, and to our future.*"
:   ―Leia Organa[[77]](#cite_note-PL5-77)

The two starships soon arrived in the [Sullust system](/wiki/Sullust_system "Sullust system"), where Organa, Verlaine, and R2-D2 engaged the [Sullustan](/wiki/Sullustan "Sullustan") [Tivvy](/wiki/Tivvy "Tivvy"), who led them to the [Alderaan Enclave](/wiki/Alderaan_Enclave "Alderaan Enclave"). During the journey, an Alderaanian [rifle](/wiki/Rifle "Rifle") [squad](/wiki/Squad "Squad") tried to apprehend them, but Organa and her companions quickly disarmed them, and requested to see their leader, [Preserver](/wiki/Preserver "Preserver") [Jora Astane](/wiki/Jora_Astane "Jora Astane"), who refused to submit to Organa's authority. She suspected her to be a traitor—particularly so after the replay of one of her ships' transmissions: [Tace](/wiki/Tace "Tace")'s innocent disclosing of their location to her sister, [Tula](/wiki/Tula "Tula"), an Imperial under the watchful eye of [Commander](/wiki/Commander "Commander") [Dreed](/wiki/Dreed "Dreed").[[78]](#cite_note-PL3-78)

 [![Organa and Verlaine entered the Alderaan Enclave together on Sullust.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/07/LeiaArrivesAlderaanEnclave-PrincessLeia3.png/revision/latest?cb=20160729175019) [![Organa and Verlaine entered the Alderaan Enclave together on Sullust.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/07/LeiaArrivesAlderaanEnclave-PrincessLeia3.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20160729175019)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/07/LeiaArrivesAlderaanEnclave-PrincessLeia3.png/revision/latest?cb=20160729175019) 

Organa and Verlaine entered the Alderaan Enclave together on Sullust.

 

Learning that [Dreed's Imperial cruiser](/wiki/Dreed%27s_Star_Destroyer "Dreed's Star Destroyer") had entered Sullust's [orbit](/wiki/Orbit "Orbit"), Astane ordered her men to kill Organa and Verlaine, forcing the two to escape into a polluted [waterway](/wiki/Water "Water") beneath the [Eyewell](/wiki/Eyewell "Eyewell"). From there, they herded [rockrenders](/wiki/Rockrender "Rockrender") to attack stormtroopers in the battle against the Alderaanians in the Enclave above. Once the skirmish was over, and the Imperials had been defeated, Astane finally accepted Organa as their sovereign.[[78]](#cite_note-PL3-78)

On her request, [Nien Nunb](/wiki/Nien_Nunb "Nien Nunb") successfully led the Alderaanian survivors off Sullust, and Organa awarded him [chalcedony waves](/wiki/Chalcedony_waves "Chalcedony waves") from her late mother, only for Astane and [Covis](/wiki/Covis "Covis") to bring Tace before her. Organa discussed the problem with Tace over some [tea](/wiki/Tea "Tea"); knowing her to be innocent, Organa decided to draw her sister out. She then appointed Pareece and Astane to negotiate with the Alderaanians living in [Espirion](/wiki/Espirion "Espirion") and had Tace ask Tula about her location. The plan backfired when Dreed threatened to kill Tula because of the inquiry, prompting Organa to trade herself for Tula on [Skaradosh](/wiki/Skaradosh "Skaradosh"), where she met Dreed as she placed herself back in Imperial custody.[[79]](#cite_note-PL4-79) The Imperials were soon attacked by a group of her followers, including Verlaine and Nunb, before she could board Dreed's shuttle. On his *[Mellcrawler](/wiki/Mellcrawler "Mellcrawler")*, Nunb smuggled them out of the system, outrunning Dreed's Star Destroyer on its way to destroy the Alderaanians on Espirion.[[77]](#cite_note-PL5-77)

 [![Organa addressed her fellow Alderaanians over Espirion.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b4/LeiaAddressesAlderaanians-PrincessLeia5.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150918121629) [![Organa addressed her fellow Alderaanians over Espirion.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b4/LeiaAddressesAlderaanians-PrincessLeia5.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20150918121629)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b4/LeiaAddressesAlderaanians-PrincessLeia5.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150918121629) 

Organa addressed her fellow Alderaanians over Espirion.

 

Although surprised to see Espirion's orbit filled with starships of Alderaanian survivors who had gotten her message, Organa told the fleet to take battle stations. She also witnessed Tace and Tula's reunion, just before meeting with Pareece and Astane to talk about their failed mission to the planet below. This angered Organa, as she had been counting on Espirion's military support against the incoming Star Destroyer, but after Verlaine's encouraging words, Organa sent an inspiring message to her fleet—which R2-D2 retransmitted to the Alderaanians below, prompting [Beon Beonel](/wiki/Beon_Beonel "Beon Beonel") to send the *[Espirion Multi](/wiki/Espirion_Multi "Espirion Multi")* to destroy Dreed's [cruiser](/wiki/Cruiser "Cruiser").[[77]](#cite_note-PL5-77)

After a celebration held among the surviving Alderaanians, Organa told Verlaine of her return to the Alliance, given she had never intended to abandon it forever, for their people would never be safe while the Emperor was in control. Verlaine claimed they needed their princess, but Organa suggested that she should elect one then, appointing Verlaine as her would-be successor. Ultimately, Organa and R2-D2 returned to Yavin 4, where she reunited with Skywalker, Solo, Chewbacca, and C-3PO.[[77]](#cite_note-PL5-77)

#### Mission to Tibrin[]

Organa and Skywalker undertook a mission to [Tibrin](/wiki/Tibrin "Tibrin") with [Jaahn Liddle](/wiki/Jaahn_Liddle "Jaahn Liddle") and [Tadd](/wiki/Tadd_Marteens "Tadd Marteens"). Posing as diplomats from [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo")'s [House Berenko](/wiki/House_Berenko "House Berenko"), they were allowed to land in the capital of Tibrin. They were greeted by [Mariod](/wiki/Mariod "Mariod") [Govi](/wiki/Govi "Govi"), and they discussed the possibility of the [Ishi Tib](/wiki/Ishi_Tib "Ishi Tib") and Rebel Alliance working together. Suddenly, a squadron of stormtroopers attacked, and the Rebels tried to hold off the Imperials. A grenade knocked out Skywalker, and Organa fell from a platform but managed to hold on to the ledge. Organa could only watch as the stormtroopers dragged Skywalker onto their shuttle and flew away.[[80]](#cite_note-SWA_4-80)

Disguised as an Imperial officer transferred from the *Malevolence* to the *[Stormbringer](/wiki/Stormbringer "Stormbringer")*, Organa snuck aboard the ship on which Skywalker was held captive. Using an explosion in the hangar, she took the clearance card of a stormtrooper and used it to find out where Skywalker was being held. She then crawled through ventilation shafts to come to Skywalker's position. Just before he was going to get tortured, Organa appeared and stunned the Imperials holding him. When they escaped, they had no place to run as there were Imperials everywhere. Skywalker convinced Organa to trust him, and together they got into an escape pod which they launched towards Tibrin. Just as the *Stormbringer* was about to fire on the pod, [*Marsheem*-class heavy cruisers](/wiki/Marsheem-class_heavy_cruiser "Marsheem-class heavy cruiser") appeared from Tibrin's moon and attacked the *Stormbringer*, destroying it completely. Later, they said goodbye to the Ishi Tib and thanked them for their help.[[81]](#cite_note-SWA_6-81)

#### Aboard the *Promise*[]

:   "*When you get betrayed, it's never by someone who looks like Vader. Betrayal always comes wrapped up in a friendly cloak. It's one of the first things I learned in the Senate.*"
:   ―Leia Organa to Luke Skywalker[[56]](#cite_note-HttJ-56)

With the [Alliance Fleet](/wiki/Rebel_Alliance_Navy "Rebel Alliance Navy") hiding in the [Sujimis sector](/wiki/Sujimis_sector "Sujimis sector") over [Orto Plutonia](/wiki/Orto_Plutonia "Orto Plutonia"), Organa helped coordinate the Rebel efforts with the rest of the [Alliance High Command](/wiki/Alliance_High_Command "Alliance High Command"), and in the company of C-3PO. During her stay on the *[Redemption](/wiki/Redemption "Redemption")*, Organa suggested to Ackbar and [Chancellor](/wiki/Chancellor_(Rebel_Alliance) "Chancellor (Rebel Alliance)") Mon Mothma that they sent someone to open a secret supply of weapons for the Alliance with the [Chekkoo clan](/wiki/Chekkoo_clan "Chekkoo clan") of [Rodia](/wiki/Rodia "Rodia"), a [mission](/wiki/Mission_to_Rodia_(Luke_Skywalker) "Mission to Rodia (Luke Skywalker)") for which Skywalker volunteered.[[56]](#cite_note-HttJ-56)

Following his return from Rodia, Organa and Ackbar met with Skywalker as soon as he landed the *[Desert Jewel](/wiki/Desert_Jewel "Desert Jewel")* on the *[Promise](/wiki/Promise "Promise")* to talk about his [encounter](/wiki/Skirmish_over_Llanic "Skirmish over Llanic") over [Llanic](/wiki/Llanic "Llanic"), during which he had saved a [Kupohan](/wiki/Kupohan "Kupohan") ship from Imperial attack. Though he apologized for it, Organa revealed he had done the right thing, as the ship carried vital intelligence about a Givin [cryptologist](/wiki/Cryptologist "Cryptologist") from [Denon](/wiki/Denon "Denon"), [Drusil Bephorin](/wiki/Drusil_Bephorin "Drusil Bephorin"), willing to help the Alliance, if the Rebels were able to safely transport her and her family to [Omereth](/wiki/Omereth "Omereth"). Organa and Ackbar assigned Skywalker, [Nakari Kelen](/wiki/Nakari_Kelen "Nakari Kelen") and the *Desert Jewel* to the [mission](/wiki/Mission_on_Denon "Mission on Denon"), though Organa warned Skywalker not to trust blindly on Kelen. After their return from an [errand](/wiki/Mission_to_Fex "Mission to Fex") for Kelen's [father](/wiki/Fayet_Kelen "Fayet Kelen") and the *Jewel*'s modifications, Organa and Ackbar further debriefed Skywalker and Kelen, and she specifically instructed them to greet Bephorin with maths to earn her trust.[[56]](#cite_note-HttJ-56)

#### The Dragon Void Run[]

:   "*Don't give up hope just yet. If there's one thing I'm sure of... Han Solo is a survivor. And he'll survive this.*"
:   ―Leia Organa to Airen Cracken[[82]](#cite_note-HS3-82)

Sometime after the outpost was established on Reamma, Organa sent rebel operatives [Adame](/wiki/Adame "Adame") and [Selentia](/wiki/Selentia "Selentia") after Solo and Chewbacca with a specific mission in mind for the smugglers. Leia sent a holographic message to Solo, telling him that the Alliance needed his ship and that there would be a reward.[[83]](#cite_note-HS1-83)

Rejecting the idea, Han confronted Leia on a rebel frigate. The two argued about the fact that she wanted to use his ship. As the duo continued to argue as they made their way through a hallway, General [Airen Cracken](/wiki/Airen_Cracken "Airen Cracken"), the head of Security and Intelligence for the Rebel Alliance, intercepted them. Cracken was unsure about Solo and the mission in general. Organa, however, vouched for him, even telling the general that he could do the mission himself. Although Cracken was hesitant, he agreed with Leia. They informed Solo of the mission, which was to find rebel informants, find a mole within the ranks, and prevent them from being murdered. They told him of the legendary [Dragon Void Run](/wiki/Dragon_Void_Run "Dragon Void Run"), a dangerous race that made its way to three planets, each of which had a rebel informant on it. Due to the race's legendary status, Solo agreed. To make his reason for leaving convincing, Leia punched Han in the face, telling him to never come back. Solo and his co-pilot left the Alliance frigate and made their way to the race.[[83]](#cite_note-HS1-83)

When Solo and Chewbacca arrived on the [first planet](/wiki/Unidentified_planet_(Dragon_Void_Run) "Unidentified planet (Dragon Void Run)"), Solo was promptly arrested by Imperial authorities. Organa and Cracken watched this on a viewscreen. Although Cracken thought the mission was compromised, Leia called Han a "survivor," knowing that he could get out of this situation. Chewbacca, however, found the first informant, a [Duros](/wiki/Duros "Duros") named [Bot](/wiki/Bot "Bot"). However, Solo was let go by the Imperials, and the race continued.[[82]](#cite_note-HS3-82)

Solo and Chewbacca continued the race and met another informant, [Dorae](/wiki/Dorae "Dorae"), on the second planet. After making their way to the third planet, the duo found the final informant, an [Elomin](/wiki/Elomin "Elomin") by the name of [Aran](/wiki/Aran_(Elomin) "Aran (Elomin)"), and his bodyguard, a [Falleen](/wiki/Falleen "Falleen") named [U'Il](/wiki/U%27il "U'il"). When they left the third planet, everyone but the Elomin made their way to the cockpit. As Solo continued to race, the group found Aran murdered.[[84]](#cite_note-Han_Solo_4-84) Through deduction, Han realized that it was Bot who had committed to crime under the influence of brainwashing. The Duros was subdued, and the race was finished. Solo and Chewbacca brought the remaining informants back to the Alliance. It was revealed that the bodyguard U'Il was the informant carrying a master list with names the rebellion needed to keep safe. She gave the list to Organa. She and Solo talked about him staying with the rebellion longer than he initially thought he would.[[85]](#cite_note-Han_Solo_5-85)

#### Attack on Cymoon 1[]

:   "*Remind me never to attack another weapons factory.*"
:   ―Leia Organa[[86]](#cite_note-SW3-86)

Alongside Skywalker, Solo, Chewbacca, R2-D2, and C-3PO,[[87]](#cite_note-SW1-87) Organa led[[17]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_2-17) a [mission](/wiki/Assault_on_Cymoon "Assault on Cymoon") on the Imperial [factory](/wiki/Factory "Factory") world of [Cymoon 1](/wiki/Cymoon_1 "Cymoon 1"), where they would infiltrate and destroy [Weapons Factory Alpha](/wiki/Weapons_Factory_Alpha "Weapons Factory Alpha"). After capturing a shuttle whose passenger was an emissary of [Jabba](/wiki/Jabba_Desilijic_Tiure "Jabba Desilijic Tiure") the [Hutt](/wiki/Hutt "Hutt") sent to negotiate with the Empire on shipping raw materials from [Hutt-controlled space](/wiki/Hutt_Space "Hutt Space") to Imperial facilities, Organa and Skywalker disguised themselves as [bodyguards](/wiki/Bodyguard "Bodyguard") to escort Solo (who, they agreed, would pose as the envoy) with R2-D2 into the factory. Greeted by [Overseer](/wiki/Overseer "Overseer") [Aggadeen](/wiki/Aggadeen "Aggadeen"), they entered the facility only to reveal themselves as rebels and incapacitate Aggadeen's stormtroopers, with the Overseer revealing the [power core's](/wiki/Reactor "Reactor") location before Organa knocked him out as well.[[87]](#cite_note-SW1-87)

 [![The Rebels make their way to the main power core.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/48/ToTheMainPowerCore-2015StarWars1.png/revision/latest?cb=20150214082437) [![The Rebels make their way to the main power core.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/48/ToTheMainPowerCore-2015StarWars1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20150214082437)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/48/ToTheMainPowerCore-2015StarWars1.png/revision/latest?cb=20150214082437) 

The Rebels make their way to the main power core.

 

Once the four made their way to the central power station, Organa, Solo, and R2-D2 rigged the power core. As they awaited Skywalker's return, Organa thanked the [Corellian](/wiki/Corellia "Corellia") [smuggler](/wiki/Smuggler "Smuggler") for taking such a risk for the Alliance yet questioned Solo about whether he had an ulterior motive for doing so. Their conversation was interrupted by Skywalker's arrival with Imperial slaves. Though Organa was unsure of Skywalker's decision and determination to have the slaves escape with them, Solo accepted it and prompted them to escape the facility as soon as possible.[[87]](#cite_note-SW1-87)

When they were alerted by Chewbacca of Vader's arrival, Organa ordered the Wookiee to kill the [Dark Lord of the Sith](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith "Dark Lord of the Sith") even at the expense of them, blaming him for Alderaan's destruction. However, Vader sensed danger and protected himself from Chewbacca's shot, putting the entire moon on alert of their presence. Completely surrounded and having lost contact with Chewbacca, they came across a [hangar](/wiki/Hangar "Hangar"), and, though Organa noticed Skywalker's absence, she and Solo procured an [All Terrain Armored Transport](/wiki/All_Terrain_Armored_Transport_(Galactic_Civil_War) "All Terrain Armored Transport (Galactic Civil War)") [walker](/wiki/Walker "Walker") for themselves, just as Skywalker engaged Vader in [combat](/wiki/Lightsaber_combat "Lightsaber combat").[[87]](#cite_note-SW1-87)

 [![Han and Leia argue while escaping the factory aboard the stolen AT-AT.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/HanAndLeiaArgue-2015StarWars2.png/revision/latest?cb=20150214081610) [![Han and Leia argue while escaping the factory aboard the stolen AT-AT.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/HanAndLeiaArgue-2015StarWars2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150214081610)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/HanAndLeiaArgue-2015StarWars2.png/revision/latest?cb=20150214081610) 

Han and Leia argue while escaping the factory aboard the stolen AT-AT.

 

Organa, Solo, R2-D2, and several slaves boarded the AT-AT. Solo piloted it through the factory before stepping on a subterranean corridor, almost crushing Skywalker and Vader. Once Solo almost stepped on a [Twi'lek](/wiki/Twi%27lek "Twi'lek") slave, Organa called him out on it, but he claimed only wanting to get them out of there, while R2-D2 and a pair of [Jawas](/wiki/Jawa "Jawa") worked to have its [cannons](/wiki/Cannon "Cannon") operational. Though the Sith Lord almost tore the walker apart with the Force, the astromech droid informed them that the cannons were ready, and Organa hit the button to fire. They not only temporarily incapacitated Vader, but also blasted their way out of the facility.[[17]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_2-17)

Once outside, their walker only received more blaster fire; Organa, then, realized the Imperials had stopped the reactor's meltdown, and Vader caught up with them and destroyed the walker's legs with [his](/wiki/Darth_Vader%27s_lightsaber "Darth Vader's lightsaber") [lightsaber](/wiki/Lightsaber "Lightsaber"), throwing it off. From the rubble, Organa carried Solo and led the slaves to safety, when Skywalker met with her and told her he would finish their mission. Disobeying Organa's orders, Skywalker used his stolen [speeder bike](/wiki/Speeder_bike "Speeder bike") to destroy the power core. Soon enough, they made their way to the *Millennium Falcon* and barely escaped with their lives. On the ship, she thanked Skywalker for completing the mission, trying to encourage him, but his morale was at rock bottom.[[86]](#cite_note-SW3-86) Before long, the *Falcon* rendezvoused with the Rebel fleet.[[88]](#cite_note-SW4-88)

#### An estranged wife[]

:   "*And here I thought* one *Solo was bad. Now I get to listen to* two *of them. Lucky me.*"
:   ―Leia Organa[[89]](#cite_note-SW10-89)

 [![Confronted by Solo over the parts needed to repair the Millennium Falcon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/HanAndLeiaTalk-2015StarWars5.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150720050140) [![Confronted by Solo over the parts needed to repair the Millennium Falcon](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/HanAndLeiaTalk-2015StarWars5.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20150720050140)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/HanAndLeiaTalk-2015StarWars5.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150720050140) 

Confronted by Solo over the parts needed to repair the *Millennium Falcon*

 

Organa met with the rest of the Alliance High Command and expressed her desire to continue the offensive against the Empire; however, Ackbar and Mothma dissuaded Organa from her course of action since they believed she was overtaxing her team. The princess next met with Skywalker, who asked her to let him (and R2-D2) go to Tatooine in search of [Kenobi's home](/wiki/Ben_Kenobi%27s_home "Ben Kenobi's home").[[88]](#cite_note-SW4-88) Later, Solo inquired about several parts needed to repair his ship, but Organa told him that he needed to work to obtain what he wanted—offering him a mission to be her copilot while they scouted for possible locations for the new Alliance base. Aboard a stolen [*Lambda*-class shuttle](/wiki/Lambda-class_T-4a_shuttle "Lambda-class T-4a shuttle"), the *[Invictus](/wiki/Invictus "Invictus")*, they had a run-in with a pair of [TIE fighters](/wiki/TIE/ln_space_superiority_starfighter "TIE/ln space superiority starfighter"), and Solo piloted the *Invictus* to an unnamed planet near the [Monsua Nebula](/wiki/Monsua_Nebula "Monsua Nebula").[[90]](#cite_note-SW5-90)

Upon landing, Organa followed Solo to one of his smuggling dens, where he offered the princess some [Corellian wine](/wiki/Corellian_wine "Corellian wine") to celebrate their survival. Organa, however, misinterpreted his gesture and refused to drink the wine, stormily leaving the den at once. As Solo followed suit, claiming he would rather seduce a [gundark](/wiki/Gundark "Gundark"), the *[Volt Cobra](/wiki/Volt_Cobra "Volt Cobra")* arrived; [Sana Starros](/wiki/Sana_Starros "Sana Starros") disembarked and revealed herself to be Solo's estranged wife, much to Organa's shock.[[91]](#cite_note-SW6-91) Though Solo tried to explain, Starros recognized Organa (and the bounty on her head) and had the *Invictus* destroyed with her ship's voice-activated weaponry.[[92]](#cite_note-SW8-92)

 [![Leia meets Starros](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/10/StarrosSoloAndOrgana-2015StarWars8.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180818234122) [![Leia meets Starros](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/10/StarrosSoloAndOrgana-2015StarWars8.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20180818234122)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/10/StarrosSoloAndOrgana-2015StarWars8.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180818234122) 

Leia meets Starros

 

Holding the two at gunpoint, Starros contacted the Star Destroyer above them to negotiate Organa's bounty, while Solo tried to convince her to let them go. However, Organa had other plans—pushing Solo against Starros, taking her by surprise, she drew a concealed EC-17 blaster from her clothes to aim it at both "Solos." With the TIE fighters and [TIE/sa bombers](/wiki/TIE/sa_tactical_bomber "TIE/sa tactical bomber") already above them,[[92]](#cite_note-SW8-92) and [Imperial pilots](/wiki/Imperial_Starfighter_Pilot "Imperial Starfighter Pilot") closing in to arrest her, Organa resisted, whereas Solo confessed he was also a Rebel (and so, bound to be captured), prompting Starros to take the two to her ship to escape the planet.[[93]](#cite_note-SW9-93) While in [hyperspace](/wiki/Hyperspace "Hyperspace"), Organa contacted the Alliance, and was informed of Skywalker's captivity on [Nar Shaddaa](/wiki/Nar_Shaddaa "Nar Shaddaa"). She convinced Starros to transport them to the moon, by agreeing to let her recover her "husband" once they reached the "Smuggler's Moon."[[89]](#cite_note-SW10-89) Solo disliked the deal and confronted Organa about it, but she refused to listen to his explanation.[[94]](#cite_note-SW11-94)

 [![Organa using a lightsaber on Nar Shaddaa](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/15/LightsaberBattleInGrakkusArena-2015StarWars12.png/revision/latest?cb=20160729173510) [![Organa using a lightsaber on Nar Shaddaa](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/15/LightsaberBattleInGrakkusArena-2015StarWars12.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20160729173510)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/15/LightsaberBattleInGrakkusArena-2015StarWars12.png/revision/latest?cb=20160729173510) 

Organa using a lightsaber on Nar Shaddaa

 

Upon arrival at Nar Shaddaa, they located C-3PO and Chewbacca, who had engaged the bounty hunter [Dengar](/wiki/Dengar "Dengar") after refusing to reveal Solo's location. Outgunned by Organa and Solo,[[94]](#cite_note-SW11-94) Dengar was defeated when Chewbacca threw him off the roof; thus, they carried on with their original objective: to free Skywalker from [Grakkus the Hutt](/wiki/Grakkus_Jahibakti_Tingi "Grakkus Jahibakti Tingi"). Organa, Solo, Chewbacca, and Starros made their way to [Grakkus' palace arena](/wiki/Palace_of_Grakkus_the_Hutt "Palace of Grakkus the Hutt"), and realized their blasters had been disabled by an EMP charge, Imperials were swarming the place and a [beast](/wiki/Kongo "Kongo") was wreaking havoc. Separated from Starros, they instead found R2-D2, who provided them with lightsabers; they promptly [used](/wiki/Rescue_of_Luke_Skywalker "Rescue of Luke Skywalker") the weapons to reach Skywalker at the center of the arena. However, instead of reuniting with him, Organa sought Starros and rescued her from under a pile of rubble. Starros then explained she was not Solo's real wife, and the two women reached an understanding before escaping Nar Shadda.[[95]](#cite_note-SW12-95)

#### Eneb Ray's infiltration[]

:   "*If this fails, we'll have no agents left on Coruscant. This is an enormous risk.*"  
    "*So was Yavin.*"
:   ―Leia Organa and Eneb Ray[[96]](#cite_note-SWA1-96)

Sometime after the Battle of Yavin, Organa sent rebel spy [Eneb Ray](/wiki/Eneb_Ray "Eneb Ray") to Coruscant to infiltrate the Imperial Senate, pretending to be the senator Tharius Demo. After he uploaded shipping and procurement data for the Core sectors to the rebellion, he contacted Leia via hologram. She gave him the mission to extract [Nadea Tural](/wiki/Nadea_Tural "Nadea Tural") and other rebel-sympathetic senators from [Arrth-Eno Prison Complex](/wiki/Arrth-Eno_Prison_Complex "Arrth-Eno Prison Complex") and prevent them from being executed. After the conversation ended, Ray made his way to the prison complex on Coruscant. After breaking in, Eneb found the prisoners, who informed him that the Emperor would be coming to the complex.[[96]](#cite_note-SWA1-96)

Ray discovered another spy within the complex, who helped him to formulate a plan to assassinate the Emperor. The two contacted Organa, who called the plan "an enormous risk." However, Ray and several other operatives attacked the Emperor, but the Sith Lord escaped. Eneb went after him and killed him. However, the real Emperor revealed that the person that Ray had killed was a mere decoy. Ray turned around and watched as the prison complex exploded, killing all inside. Palpatine proceeded to electrocute Ray, leaving him unable to complete any mission he had left.[[96]](#cite_note-SWA1-96)

### War intensifies[]

#### Battle of Vrogas Vas[]

:   "*You can kill me, but you can't kill what I stand for... and you won't stop justice.*"
:   ―Leia Organa, to Darth Vader[[97]](#cite_note-DV14-97)
