When news reached the Alliance Fleet that Darth Vader had made his appearance over [Vrogas Vas](/wiki/Vrogas_Vas "Vrogas Vas") and his ship had been forced to crash-land by Skywalker, Dodonna deployed a [battalion](/wiki/Battalion "Battalion") to back the [company](/wiki/Company "Company") of the [Rebel Refueling Base](/wiki/Rebel_Refueling_Base "Rebel Refueling Base"). When Organa heard this, she immediately set out to assist them, as did Solo, Chewbacca, and C-3PO, on the *Falcon*.[[98]](#cite_note-SW:VD-98) Soon after they arrived, Organa and Solo were told that Skywalker had brought Vader down at the cost of crashing his X-wing as well, but despite her worry about him, she would not spare any [speeders](/wiki/Speeder "Speeder"). As a Commander, she coordinated the effort and deployed [Cyan Squadron](/wiki/Cyan_Squadron "Cyan Squadron"), of which another ship was taken down by Vader.[[99]](#cite_note-DV13-99)

 [![The princess is reminded by Solo that her priorities should remain with Skywalker-not getting revenge against Vader.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3f/SoloRemindsOrgana-2015DarthVader13.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20151225055914) [![The princess is reminded by Solo that her priorities should remain with Skywalker-not getting revenge against Vader.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3f/SoloRemindsOrgana-2015DarthVader13.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20151225055914)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3f/SoloRemindsOrgana-2015DarthVader13.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20151225055914) 

The princess is reminded by Solo that her priorities should remain with Skywalker-not getting revenge against Vader.

 

Subsequently, Organa decided to go to where he was spotted last, along with a [platoon](/wiki/Platoon "Platoon") of other Rebel soldiers. Amidst the thick layer of mist, she and other troopers advanced until Vader [Force choked](/wiki/Force_choke "Force choke") her two companions and confronted her.[[100]](#cite_note-SW13-100) After a tense moment, however, Vader apparently sensed an ambush, allowing Organa to escape and tell her friends where she was (and thus, lure Skywalker to him). She escaped and found C-3PO, who handed her a [comlink](/wiki/Comlink "Comlink"); she used it to order all surviving rebel pilots to come to her position and hit it with everything they had at her signal. Organa then ordered C-3PO to return to Skywalker, and waited for Vader to appear before her again, and signaled all fighters to bombard their location.[[97]](#cite_note-DV14-97)

 [![Organa and her friends escape Vader and Vrogas Vas aboard the Millennium Falcon.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a6/EscapingVrogasVas-2015DarthVader15.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160725191532) [![Organa and her friends escape Vader and Vrogas Vas aboard the Millennium Falcon.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a6/EscapingVrogasVas-2015DarthVader15.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160725191532)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a6/EscapingVrogasVas-2015DarthVader15.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160725191532) 

Organa and her friends escape Vader and Vrogas Vas aboard the *Millennium Falcon*.

 

However, Imperial enforcer [Karbin](/wiki/Karbin "Karbin") arrived with a fleet and destroyed the Amber Wing.[[97]](#cite_note-DV14-97) Karbin himself went to the encounter of Organa and Vader and proceeded to duel each other. Organa used the opportunity to escape from their reach into the Jedi Temple and waited to get a clear shot.[[101]](#cite_note-SW14-101) However, C-3PO called her through the comlink and informed her that Solo, Chewbacca, and Skywalker were in trouble. Confronted with their loss, she left Vader and Karbin to their devices. Instead, Organa located the *Millennium Falcon* and found Solo, Skywalker, the droids, and Chewbacca cornered by Vader's ally, [Dr.](/wiki/Doctor "Doctor") [Aphra](/wiki/Chelli_Lona_Aphra "Chelli Lona Aphra"). As she had implemented a minefield of micro-[mines](/wiki/Mine "Mine") to trap them, Organa snuck up to her and knocked her out with a punch. With Aphra captured, Organa ordered all remaining Rebel forces to evacuate the planet; then, they boarded the *Falcon* and escaped.[[102]](#cite_note-DV15-102)

#### Defending Sunspot Prison[]

:   "*I want you to know... I won't give up on you. I'll get you help you need, Eneb. Whether you want it or not.*"
:   ―Leia Organa to Eneb Ray[[103]](#cite_note-SW_19-103)

After weeks of interrogation and four escape attempts, Organa and Starros brought Doctor Aphra to the [Sunspot Prison](/wiki/Sunspot_Prison "Sunspot Prison"), a Rebel Alliance penitentiary. Organa, Starros, and the prison's warden debated about how to interrogate the new prisoner. Meanwhile, a team led by former rebel spy Eneb Ray made their way into the prison, attacking the guards. This was reported to the warden, as well as Leia and Sana.[[104]](#cite_note-SW_16-104)

Organa and Starros engaged the invading droid forces, destroying many of them. Leia contacted the control room, wanting to know if they were given an all clear. However, instead of a response from the warden, Eneb Ray responded. He had taken over the control room and was holding the warden hostage. He proceeded to send [IG-RM droids](/wiki/IG-RM_bodyguard_and_enforcer_droid "IG-RM bodyguard and enforcer droid") to execute prisoners. Organa disabled them, but not before they opened fire. Afterwards, Ray released other prisoners, forcing Organa and Starros to engage them. After fighting many of the prisoners, Leia placed them in a single cell. Ray deactivated the sun shields in that cell, incinerating all the prisoners within it. Ray continued to make threats. Because of this, Organa freed Doctor Aphra, needing her to help retake the prison.[[105]](#cite_note-SW_17-105)

Soon after being freed, Aphra began to reprogram one of the enforcer droids while it was attacking Starros. Organa disabled it before it could kill the smuggler. After a brief argument, the three continued to make their way through the cell blocks. Meanwhile, Ray was personally going to cells and killing the inmates, revealing the truth about Emperor Palpatine to one inmate. Aphra, Sana, and Leia finally reached the control room and engaged the droids defending it. The trio, as well as the enforcer droid that Doctor Aphra reprogrammed, managed to retake the control room. Meanwhile, Han Solo and Luke Skywalker arrived on the base in the *Millennium Falcon*, only to be captured by Ray.[[106]](#cite_note-SW_18-106)

Sana, Aphra, and Leia managed to find Ray with the captured Skywalker and Solo. Ray had wrapped the duo in thermal detonators and threatened to kill them unless Leia shot Doctor Aphra. He then proceeded to reveal his identity, which had been previously hidden. Having thought him dead, Leia was surprised. Organa had R2-D2 activate an ion pulse, which took out the prison's gravity, as well as the trigger to the thermal detonators. Ray and Organa began fighting in midair. Through the combined efforts of Leia, Aphra, and Sana, Ray was defeated and arrested.[[103]](#cite_note-SW_19-103)

Afterwards, the remaining staff and prisoners were evacuated. However, Doctor Aphra escaped, thanks to the indifference of Organa and Starros. As Ray was escorted in binders, Leia told him that she hadn't given up on him. However, Ray was so broken mentally that he told her that the rebels had no chance of winning, and that she would eventually wish she had listened to him.[[103]](#cite_note-SW_19-103)

#### Temporary outpost[]

:   "*It's absolute* chaos *in here, Luke. We're still trying to get on our feet here and one of our cargo vessels is still* missing*.*"
:   ―Leia Organa to Luke Skywalker[[107]](#cite_note-Droid_Dilemma-107)

Sometime later the Rebel Alliance established a temporary outpost by the name of [LX-Robynsun V](/wiki/LX-Robynsun_V "LX-Robynsun V") on the Outer Rim planet [Reamma](/wiki/Reamma "Reamma"). The Alliance was still adjusting to the new outpost when a cargo vessel went missing. Leia assigned Skywalker to double back and search for it, as it was carrying vital medical supplies and other cargo. However, as Skywalker and R2-D2 prepared the search, the cargo vessel arrived, cancelling the mission.[[107]](#cite_note-Droid_Dilemma-107)

#### Hijacking of the *Harbinger*[]

Organa and Skywalker attended a meeting with Jan Dodonna, Gial Ackbar, and Mon Mothma aboard a [medical frigate](/wiki/EF76_Nebulon-B_escort_frigate "EF76 Nebulon-B escort frigate"). Ackbar reported that the planet of [Tureen VII](/wiki/Tureen_VII "Tureen VII") was under [siege](/wiki/Siege_on_Tureen_VII "Siege on Tureen VII") from the Empire. The planet had been providing aid to the rebellion secretly, and it was considered time for the Alliance to repay their debts to Tureen VII. The high-ranking members noted that the planet had come under a blockade, with the people of the world starving. After three attempts to break through the Imperial blockade failed, Skywalker and Organa came up with the idea to steal a Star Destroyer to infiltrate the blockade and provide relief to the people of Tureen VII. Although General Dodonna was initially hesitant, due to the large crew needed for operating such a vehicle, Leia asked for as much crew as could be spared. Due to the high rank of Organa and Skywalker, they were given permission to go through with this mission.[[108]](#cite_note-SW_23-108)

After the meeting, Leia took the *Millennium Falcon*, along with Han Solo, Chewbacca, Sana Starros, R2-D2, and C-3PO to attack the Star Destroyer known as the [*Harbinger*](/wiki/Harbinger_(Imperial_I-class) "Harbinger (Imperial I-class)"). Luke took the pilots of [Red Squadron](/wiki/Red_Squadron_(Rebel_Alliance) "Red Squadron (Rebel Alliance)") to also engage in the assault. The *Falcon* was used to fire proton bombs at an area near the Destroyer's main engine reactor. [Red Three](/wiki/Red_Three "Red Three"), Wedge Antilles, also fired torpedoes towards the main engine reactor. Although the shots hit their mark, the reactor did not overload. Skywalker then flew into the main engine reactor causing it to overload. The Imperial crew of the Star Destroyer abandoned the ship, giving the crew of the *Millennium Falcon* the opportunity to capture it. The ship flew into the Destroyer's hangar, with the crew of the *Falcon* attacking the ship from the inside. Meanwhile, Skywalker secured the reactor room as the sentients made their way there. As a [space](/wiki/Realspace "Realspace") battle raged outside, an explosion came from the *Harbinger*, making the Empire think it had been destroyed.[[109]](#cite_note-SW22-109)

A week afterwards, a patrol of two TIE fighters briefly spotted the stolen Star Destroyer but were quickly destroyed. Skywalker noted that the Empire may have known their location. However, Organa stated that if the government had known, there would have been more ships sent. At the time, the Destroyer was running on its secondary reactor and had no captain. Solo and Organa argued about who was to be the captain. Skywalker attempted to calm the duo by telling them of the situation at hand, noting that it would most likely be the last flight of the *Harbinger*.[[109]](#cite_note-SW22-109)

Days later, a reactor overload was becoming more and more likely. Luke, R2-D2, and Chewbacca were attempting to fix the issue as quickly as possible. However, an explosion occurred, and the astromech droid jettisoned the reactor, allowing the Star Destroyer to go to hyperspace. Han noted that the group had officially stolen their own Star Destroyer, with Leia responding that the hard part was yet to come.[[108]](#cite_note-SW_23-108)

After the *Harbinger* got out of hyperspace, the engines died. Chewbacca attempted to fix the backup reactor trying to get the Destroyer to Tureen VII. Solo attempted to order the crew to change course to the [Monsua Nebula](/wiki/Monsua_Nebula "Monsua Nebula") to give the crew more time to fix it. However, Organa ordered the crew to belay that order, knowing that the people of Tureen VII were dying and there was not enough time to stop and make repairs. The duo continued to argue about the merits of their ideas and who should be temporary captain of the ship. Solo proposed a race to the bridge of the Destroyer to determine who was to be the captain. Although Leia seemed to think that was a bad idea, she kicked Solo in the shin to give herself a head start.[[108]](#cite_note-SW_23-108)

As the two made their way through a hangar, Solo rode a speeder bike trying to get ahead of Organa. After being hit by the bike, Leia asked a member of the crew where the spacesuits were kept. She later donned one of the spacesuits and made her way to the bridge, getting there before Solo and declaring herself captain. As she was doing that, a rebel shuttle with the dead Admiral [Verette](/wiki/Verette "Verette") tied to the front appeared at the rendezvous point. Sana Starros destroyed the ship, thinking it was a trap. Meanwhile, an Imperial shuttle carrying [Task Force 99](/wiki/Task_Force_99 "Task Force 99") managed to sneak onto the Star Destroyer and board it.[[108]](#cite_note-SW_23-108)

Afterwards, Solo noted that the Star Destroyer's hyperdrive, backup reactor, shields, and ion cannons were all malfunctioning in some form, calling the *Harbinger* "the worst Star Destroyer in the entire galaxy." Organa wanted to know the status of the ion cannons, asking the Destroyer's maintenance team what the status was. Because the team had gone missing, a group led by Luke and Sana went to check it out. Han still wanted the *Harbinger* to stop for repairs, but considering all the options, Leia pressed on. Noting that the situation was ludicrous, Organa told Solo that she wanted him as the Destroyer's helmsman, calling him "the craziest pilot in the galaxy."[[110]](#cite_note-SW24-110)

As this conversation took place, Starros and Skywalker found Task Force 99 in the hallways of the ship. The squadron proceeded to attack Skywalker's group. Luke engaged the leader, Sergeant [Kreel](/wiki/Kreel "Kreel"), while Starros and the other members of the group dealt with other members of the squadron. Organa and Solo, meanwhile, were defending the bridge from the members [Aero](/wiki/Aero "Aero"), [Misty](/wiki/Misty "Misty"), and [Mic](/wiki/Mic "Mic"). Solo steered the *Harbinger* towards Tureen VII, ramming it into the planet's base security Star Destroyers. As a result, the Destroyer's front shields and an engine were lost. The Rebel Alliance sent [Blue Squadron](/wiki/Blue_Squadron_(Rebel_Alliance) "Blue Squadron (Rebel Alliance)") to defend the Star Destroyer, and as they engaged the base's TIE fighters, Darth Vader arrived in his [own](/wiki/Darth_Vader%27s_TIE_Advanced "Darth Vader's TIE Advanced") [personal TIE fighter](/wiki/TIE_Advanced_x1 "TIE Advanced x1"), destroying many of the Alliance X-wings.[[110]](#cite_note-SW24-110)

Organa ordered Red Squadron to defend the *Harbinger* to give the Star Destroyer more time to release the supplies to the surface of Tureen VII. Solo attempted to get the Destroyer's ion cannons online. Han and Leia attempted to hold the bridge, to no avail. Meanwhile, Skywalker engaged Sergeant Kreel, eventually using the Force to disable him. Later, the reactors came back to full power when Chewbacca tossed Task Force 99 member [Zuke](/wiki/Zuke "Zuke") into the reactor. Although the reactor power was restored, the controls specifically were disabled. R2-D2 was flying the ship remotely and operating the ion cannons because of that. Meanwhile, Starros and Chewbacca made their way to the *Millennium Falcon*, and Skywalker made his way to an X-wing to defend the *Harbinger*. C-3PO, on the other hand, was accidentally left behind, allowing himself to be captured by Task Force 99.[[111]](#cite_note-SW_25-111)

 [![Han and Leia in space](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9d/SW25cover.png/revision/latest?cb=20250726033358) [![Han and Leia in space](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9d/SW25cover.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250726033358)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9d/SW25cover.png/revision/latest?cb=20250726033358) 

Han and Leia in space

 

As the invading members of the task force made their way through the bridge, Solo detonated a thermal detonator on the bridge, allowing him and Organa to escape. The duo grabbed [breath masks](/wiki/Breath_mask "Breath mask") to give them oxygen in the vacuum of space. The two began to argue about their survival when the *Millennium Falcon* arrived to pick them up. Meanwhile, R2-D2 made his way to an escape pod and saved himself. The *Harbinger* finally was destroyed by the constant barrage of Imperial fire. Red and Blue Squadron, as well as the *Falcon*, jumped to hyperspace before any more destruction could take place.[[111]](#cite_note-SW_25-111)

#### Escape from Skorii-Lei[]

:   "*Rebellion is an idea bigger than any of us, it has to be to inspire. It is* alive. *Only as strong as its weakest link. What matters is that it survives us, that is grows* beyond us."
:   ―Leia Organa to Pash Davane[[112]](#cite_note-SWA2-112)

During the Galactic Civil War, Organa ended up injured and unconscious on the aquatic planet of [Skorii-Lei](/wiki/Skorii-Lei "Skorii-Lei"). The engineer-turned-janitor [Pash Davane](/wiki/Pash_Davane "Pash Davane") took in the wounded princess and considered what to do with her. After returning from her area's [fish market](/wiki/Skorii-Lei_Fish_Market "Skorii-Lei Fish Market"), Davane was attacked by Leia with her droid [Bruce](/wiki/Bruce "Bruce")'s arm. Leia threatened Pavane with a deactivated blaster to determine why she was there. The janitor revealed that she stitched up some of Organa's wounds, and in turn Leia revealed that she was transporting information vital to the Alliance. Although the two disagreed on ideological grounds, Pavane agreed to help Organa escape through the planet's oceans.[[112]](#cite_note-SWA2-112)

Sometime later, the two had put on wetsuits and prepared to leave when stormtrooper's arrived at Pash's house. Pash distracted and knocked out the soldiers and the duo escaped into the city. Hiding in a random house, Leia collapsed from her wounds. There, she and Pash discussed what motivated the former to fight the Empire despite all the loss she endured. Although ready to give Pash the data tape with vital Alliance information, Davane convinced her to continue into the water. Pursued by security forces underwater, the duo managed to escape and rendezvous with Skywalker, Solo, and Chewbacca. Leia was able to recover on the *Millennium Falcon* and managed to convince Pash to join the rebellion.[[112]](#cite_note-SWA2-112)

#### The matter of C-3PO's capture[]

After C-3PO was captured by SCAR Squadron, Solo, Skywalker, and Leia regrouped with the rebel fleet and decided not to go after him because he was a droid and SCAR Squadron was too dangerous. However, R2-D2 rebelled against this and went on a [solo mission](/wiki/Mission_to_rescue_C-3PO "Mission to rescue C-3PO") of his own to rescue his old friend.[[113]](#cite_note-SW_26-113)

#### The Screaming Citadel[]

:   "*Hey, don't make it about her and her freakshow.* We *saved the day.* We *freed people.* We're *together. That's something. That's everything.*"
:   ―Leia Organa on Sana Starros' and Chelli Lona Aphra's relationship[[114]](#cite_note-Doctor_Aphra_8-114)

Sometime after the hijacking of the *Harbinger*, the rebellion established a [temporary outpost](/wiki/Horox_III_rebel_outpost "Horox III rebel outpost") on the Outer Rim world of [Horox III](/wiki/Horox_III "Horox III"). After Skywalker again encountered the rogue archaeologist Aphra in a cantina, she offered to give him a meeting with a Jedi Master if he went with her to the forest planet of [Ktath'atn](/wiki/Ktath%27atn "Ktath'atn"). Unbeknownst to Organa and the rest of the alliance, Aphra [brought](/wiki/Mission_to_Ktath%27atn "Mission to Ktath'atn") Skywalker to meet the [Queen of Ktath'atn](/wiki/Unidentified_Queen_of_Ktath%27atn "Unidentified Queen of Ktath'atn"), who planned on feasting on the Jedi-in-training. Because she was unaware of his whereabouts, Organa questioned Skywalker's temporary astromech droid [S4](/wiki/Essfour "Essfour"). However, the droid refused to give up the information. Starros, who had received a message from Aphra, used a loophole in the droid's programming to force it to reveal that Skywalker had gone with Aphra in secret. Organa believed that Aphra had kidnapped Skywalker, so Organa, Starros, and Solo hatched a plan to rescue him.[[115]](#cite_note-The_Screaming_Citadel_1-115)

As the group prepared to depart, Starros informed them of the [Queen of Ktath'atn](/wiki/Queen_of_Ktath%27atn "Queen of Ktath'atn")'s yearly meetings with visitors to exchange organic oddities. After realizing what may become of Skywalker, the trio began the journey to Ktath'atn in the *Millennium Falcon*. However, upon arriving, they were immediately captured by Aphra's droid associates [0-0-0](/wiki/0-0-0 "0-0-0") and [BT-1](/wiki/BT-1 "BT-1").[[116]](#cite_note-SW_31-116)

However, the droids spared the rebels, and they reluctantly gave Solo permission to pilot Aphra's ship, the *[Ark Angel II](/wiki/Ark_Angel_II "Ark Angel II")*, to Aphra and Skywalker's [location](/wiki/Citadel_of_Ktath%27atn "Citadel of Ktath'atn"). When they arrived, the archaeologist and the Padawan were fleeing from mutated creatures. Starros attempted to shoot Aphra, but Organa and Skywalker prevented her from doing so. Organa threatened Skywalker with a [court-martial](/wiki/Court-martial "Court-martial") if he disobeyed orders again. She then asked the group which way to go, to which Solo responded, "Any direction away from [them](/wiki/Queen_of_Ktath%27atn%27s_hive "Queen of Ktath'atn's hive")!" The rebel group held off the Queen's hive and entered a room filled with what Aphra identified as [Abersyn symbiotes](/wiki/Abersyn_symbiote "Abersyn symbiote"). Aphra found some blueprints for the Citadel and asked Skywalker to follow her. However, the rogue archaeologist led Skywalker, and the rest of the rebels, into a trap for the Queen and her hive. The Queen took mental control of Skywalker and Solo, while Aphra allowed the rest of the group to escape.[[117]](#cite_note-Doctor_Aphra_7-117)

Organa immediately began formulating a plan to rescue them, asking Aphra's droid associates to assist her. 0-0-0 came up with the idea to transport an Abersyn symbiote in the dome of Skywalker's droid S4. Leia reluctantly agreed to his plan. BT-1 used explosive missiles to blow a hole in the room they were in, and the group made their escape. They encountered [Bombinax](/wiki/Bombinax "Bombinax"), the Queen's lieutenant, beating Aphra's Wookiee associate [Krrsantan](/wiki/Krrsantan "Krrsantan"). Organa shot at Bombinax to distract him and "save" Krrsantan. The group made their way inside the citadel and sealed the door. 0-0-0 immediately began performing a surgery on Krrsantan to transplant the symbiote into his body, much to Leia's chagrin. By the time Bombinax broke through the sealed door, the symbiote had made its way into Krrsantan's consciousness and easily dispatched him.[[117]](#cite_note-Doctor_Aphra_7-117)

0-0-0 managed to convince the feral Wookiee not to kill them, and instead to attack other Citadel personnel. With a new path forged in blood for them, the group made their way to rescue Luke and Han. However, by the time they arrived in the Queen's facility, Solo had been enthralled by the monarch. Reluctant to shoot him, she was temporarily captured by the Queen's guard. Before being infected, Sana was able to disable Han. As all of this was going on, Luke was able to use the Queen of Ktath'atn's parasites against her.[[118]](#cite_note-SW_32-118)

Through the power of her words, Leia was able to break the spell that Han was under. Still having the power of the Queen's thrall, Solo was able to control the other troops and force them to lower their weapons. Meanwhile, Luke struck down the Queen of Ktath'atn, disabling all under her control. With the control of her hive now ceded to Solo, the smuggler decided to release all who were under her control. Leia ordered 0-0-0 to remove the parasite from Han. The rebels and the rogue archaeologists parted ways afterwards, having freed the people of Ktath'atn.[[114]](#cite_note-Doctor_Aphra_8-114)

#### Surviving in the wild[]

:   "*We've got more than enough life left in us to land. I'm taking us down onto this planet.*"
:   ―Luke Skywalker, to Leia Organa[[40]](#cite_note-SW33-40)

 [![Skywalker and Organa on the ocean planet](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/Star_Wars_33_Textless.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170420190544) [![Skywalker and Organa on the ocean planet](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/Star_Wars_33_Textless.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170420190544)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/Star_Wars_33_Textless.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170420190544) 

Skywalker and Organa on the ocean planet

 

During a mission with Skywalker, he had to pilot into a nebula to get away from TIEs hunting them. The nebula disabled the ship, forcing them to crash on an [ocean planet](/wiki/Unidentified_ocean_planet "Unidentified ocean planet"). There they had to survive in the wild on an [island](/wiki/Unidentified_desert_island "Unidentified desert island"). Skywalker's experience with machinery such as [moisture vaporators](/wiki/Moisture_vaporator "Moisture vaporator") helped keep them alive. But they had to use the [dedlanite](/wiki/Dedlanite "Dedlanite") from their blasters for the moisture vaporators and thus couldn't use their blasters for hunting. One night, Organa and Skywalker lay on the ground looking up to the sky full of stars. Alderaan was still visible, as the light from the explosion hadn't reached this part of the galaxy. Later, there was an explosion in the ocean, and up to the beach came a [native species](/wiki/Unidentified_aquatic_species "Unidentified aquatic species") of the planet. They followed the creatures back into the water and saw that the Empire were destroying their underwater [worlds](/wiki/Unidentified_aquatic_species_city "Unidentified aquatic species city") in search of Organa and Skywalker. So, they lit a great fire on the beach to attract the Empire's attention. Up from the waters came an AT-AT and [shoretroopers](/wiki/Coastal_defender_stormtrooper "Coastal defender stormtrooper"). Organa and Skywalker managed to fight them off and take over their AT-AT. After disabling the AT-AT, they repaired the shuttle and returned to the Rebel Fleet.[[40]](#cite_note-SW33-40)

#### Potential Odona Base[]

:   "*You don't* owe *me anything, Han. In the Alliance, we don't keep a tally of debts! And we don't blame others when our choices turn out poorly. We make the best of it--together.*"
:   ―Leia Organa to Han Solo[[119]](#cite_note-SWA3-119)

Sometime later, Han Solo led Leia to the remote world of [Odona](/wiki/Odona "Odona") while searching for a new location for a rebel base. However, as their mission went on, the duo found themselves lost in the caves of the hostile planet, chased by a [six-legged creature](/wiki/Unidentified_Odona_creature "Unidentified Odona creature"). Solo saved the duo by shooting the ceiling of the cave, separating them from the creature. Organa was disappointed by Solo's lack of knowledge of the planet he purported to know so much about. As the duo bickered in their usual way, a trio of bounty hunters began shooting at them, wanting to collect Solo's bounty. The duo became separated, with an injured Han ending up back in the caves while Leia returned to the *Millennium Falcon*. The hunters, led by [Frax](/wiki/Frax "Frax"), a [Nikto](/wiki/Nikto "Nikto") with a vendetta against Solo, pursued him into the caves.[[119]](#cite_note-SWA3-119)

Meanwhile, Organa armed herself and searched for Solo in the caves. After rescuing Solo, an angry and wounded Frax killed his two partners for wanting to leave Solo alone. All made their way out to the snowy landscape. Leia decided to seal the other entrance of the cave and in response, Frax shot her, causing her to pass out. Sometime afterwards, Chewbacca and Alliance soldiers rescued her and Solo; Frax had frozen to death. As they recovered in a medical frigate, Solo told Organa that he intended to repay the life debt that he owed her for saving his life on the mission, to which she said that he didn't owe her anything.[[119]](#cite_note-SWA3-119)

#### Return to Horox III[]

:   "*This is* war*.*"
:   ―Leia Organa to Luke Skywalker, Han Solo, and Sana Starros[[120]](#cite_note-SW37-120)

Organa, Skywalker, Solo, Starros, Threepio, and Artoo returned to the rebel outpost on Horox III just to find it all [burned down](/wiki/Mission_to_Horox_III "Mission to Horox III") with no survivors. On a wall, "Greetings from SCAR Squadron. Long live the Empire" in [Aurebesh](/wiki/Aurebesh "Aurebesh") was written.[[120]](#cite_note-SW37-120)

#### The ashes of Jedha[]

On [Jedha](/wiki/Jedha "Jedha"), Organa and the *Millennium Falcon* rescued Skywalker and a few [Partisans](/wiki/Partisans "Partisans") and traveled to [NaJedha](/wiki/NaJedha "NaJedha"), where they took shelter. There, Organa discussed with [Ubin Des](/wiki/Ubin_Des "Ubin Des"), former member of the Rebellion, about assisting the Partisans in stopping the Empire from mining the rest of the kyber crystals from Jedha.[[121]](#cite_note-SW38-121)

Organa, Skywalker, and Solo were brought before the [Tognath](/wiki/Tognath "Tognath") named [Benthic](/wiki/Benthic "Benthic"), once [Saw Gerrera](/wiki/Saw_Gerrera "Saw Gerrera")'s second in command and now the leader of the Partisans. They all had to wear bags over their heads so they wouldn't know where the Partisans' base was located. Organa proposed that the Rebellion would help the Partisans defend Jedha by giving them supplies. After much hesitation, Benthic stated that they needed the Rebels' support and agreed.[[122]](#cite_note-SW39-122)

They then participated in a mission to blow up the newly deployed mining machine set up by the Empire. After Benthic and his team had sabotaged it from the inside, Organa and Solo arrived and blew the machine up. When they came back to the base, Skywalker was going to follow the pilgrim [Chulco Gi](/wiki/Chulco_Gi "Chulco Gi") to a Force temple. Leia, furious over Skywalker leaving at such an important time, called him irresponsible, but he left anyway.[[123]](#cite_note-SW40-123)

 [![Leia and Trios](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/StarWars62-CoverArt.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20181219064301) [![Leia and Trios](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/StarWars62-CoverArt.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20181219064301)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/StarWars62-CoverArt.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20181219064301) 

Leia and Trios

 

After the Partisans had successfully blown up the Empire's machine, they had enlisted the help of [Shu-Torun](/wiki/Shu-Torun "Shu-Torun") [Queen](/wiki/Monarch_of_Shu-Torun "Monarch of Shu-Torun") [Trios](/wiki/Trios "Trios"). She deployed the [Leviathan](/wiki/Leviathan_(Continent-class_crawler) "Leviathan (Continent-class crawler)"), a mining vehicle as big as a city, to the surface of Jedha. The Partisans tried to attack it, but it had no effect. Organa then had Chewbacca bring schematics of the Leviathan from Shu-Torun to the Partisans.[[124]](#cite_note-SW41-124)

Organa organized a briefing, detailing how they would attack the Leviathan. A small team would infiltrate the core security system, power down its anti-air weapons, and seal off the bridge of the crawler. Then a larger team would join, and together they would control the vehicle into the blast crate from the Death Star. Organa, together with Skywalker, Threepio, and Artoo snuck into the Leviathan as the smaller team. When they found the control nexus, Skywalker left to help the other team fight Imperials since he was no longer needed to shut down the crawler. Organa with the help of Threepio and Artoo shut down the weapons and allowed the *Millennium Falcon*, with the larger team, to land without getting shot down. Even though she heard there were fights going on close by, she had to stay and protect the control nexus. Suddenly, she heard a voice behind her. She turned around and standing there was Queen Trios of Shu-Torun with a blaster pointed at Organa.[[125]](#cite_note-SW42-125)

Instead of shooting Organa, she told Organa to punch her. Organa did so and blasted the surveillance camera, realizing that Trios had helped them. She then asked why Trios had leaked the plans for the crawler to them. Trios then told her how Darth Vader had assassinated her father and given her the throne. Vader gave her a piece of Alderaan to teach her a lesson. And he did, but not in the way he had intended. She decided that would never allow that to happen to Shu-Torun. Though she couldn't oppose them openly, she was sabotaging them in secret. Trios explained how she was willing to sacrifice the Leviathan to raise her above suspicion. Organa asked her if she were offering to be an inside contact for the Rebellion. Trios answered that she would be willing to do even more and offered Organa Shu-Torun's hidden resources. They shook hands, and Organa left with Skywalker who had arrived, to help the remaining Rebels. Trios then stayed behind so that she could open the passages for the Imperials late enough so that the Rebels could escape but early enough to remove suspicion from her. Skywalker then asked Organa who that was, and she answered, just what she was looking for, a little more hope. They met up with the rest and left the Leviathan on the *Millennium Falcon* just as it fell into the blast crate of the Death Star. Trios narrowly escaped in a shuttle as well. The Rebels regrouped on NaJedha and wished good luck to Benthic and his Partisans. Organa, Skywalker, Solo, Threepio, and Artoo then left the planet and flew off with the *Millennium Falcon*.[[126]](#cite_note-SW43-126)

#### Baraan-Fa and Crait[]

During the Empire's [attack on the Rebel fleet](/wiki/Attack_on_the_Rebel_fleet "Attack on the Rebel fleet"), Organa worked with Mothma to find a viable location for a new base. She and Mothma agreed on [Baraan-Fa](/wiki/Baraan-Fa "Baraan-Fa") and ordered the fleet there. Once there, Organa and Mothma continued to search for a new location for their base. Organa suggested [Sabanash](/wiki/Sabanash "Sabanash")'s wetlands or the [Moon of Ooloponi](/wiki/Moon_of_Ooloponi "Moon of Ooloponi"). She asked Mothma for a squadron to see if [Crait](/wiki/Crait "Crait") would be suitable for a base. Mothma was skeptical about Crait's status as a dead planet, but Organa told her that [Trusk Berinato](/wiki/Trusk_Berinato "Trusk Berinato") assured her and her father that [Crait's mines](/wiki/Mines_of_Crait "Mines of Crait") would be ideal for the Rebels. Mothma agreed to Organa's request.[[127]](#cite_note-Storms_of_Crait-127)

Organa [took](/wiki/Mission_to_Crait "Mission to Crait") her team, [Red Squadron](/wiki/Red_Squadron_(Rebel_Alliance) "Red Squadron (Rebel Alliance)"), and the *Millennium Falcon* to Crait with equipment. Upon their arrival, Organa met with Berinato and was given a tour of the mines. Following the tour, Organa had a drink with Berinato and told him that it was premature to believe the Rebels would use the mines as a base. She knew Berinato had dealings with the Empire and had stormtroopers on standby. She tried to convince Berinato to do the right thing, but he refused. Organa, Solo, and Red Squadron used [V-4X-D ski speeders](/wiki/V-4X-D_ski_speeder "V-4X-D ski speeder") against SCAR squadron. After dealing with SCAR squadron, Organ was confronted by Berinato, who attempted to capture Organa, but she was able to shoot his blaster out of his hand. She and the others left Crait[[127]](#cite_note-Storms_of_Crait-127) and some of their equipment.[[128]](#cite_note-Complete_Visual_Dictionary,_New_Edition-128) Organa informed Mothma of this.[[127]](#cite_note-Storms_of_Crait-127)

#### Mutiny on Mon Cala[]

Organa, her team, and Admiral Ackbar to Mon Cala to meet with [Grand Admiral](/wiki/Grand_Admiral "Grand Admiral") [Dors Urtya](/wiki/Dors_Urtya "Dors Urtya"), Mon Cala's regent and commander of its [Mercantile Fleet](/wiki/Mon_Cala_Mercantile_Fleet "Mon Cala Mercantile Fleet"). They landed on an island in a nature preservation zone, but their meeting was interrupted by stormtrooper patrol and an [Imperial gunship](/wiki/LAAT/le_patrol_gunship "LAAT/le patrol gunship"). Despite that, Organa and the others were able to lose the stormtroopers and rendezvous at a boat. Organa asked Urtya to give the Alliance their fleet to defeat the Empire. However, Urtya refused to let the fleet join the Alliance due to the Empire's continuing [occupation of Mon Cala](/wiki/Occupation_of_Mon_Cala "Occupation of Mon Cala").[[129]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_44-129)

Organa, her team, and Ackbar left Mon Cala on the *Millennium Falcon* and went to the [Mako-Ta Space Docks](/wiki/Mako-Ta_Space_Docks "Mako-Ta Space Docks"). There, Organa contacted Trios and asked her for information on the Imperial prison system to rescue King [Lee-Char](/wiki/Lee-Char "Lee-Char").[[129]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_44-129) She then prepared a report and attended a meeting of the Rebel High Council, where she informed them of Urtya's refusal to support the Alliance. However, Organa suggested rescuing King Lee-Char. Despite concerns from Mothma and General [Davits Draven](/wiki/Davits_Draven "Davits Draven"), Organa convinced them to agree to her mission.[[130]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_45-130)

Organa and her team went to the [Dex Acquisitions](/wiki/Dex_Acquisitions "Dex Acquisitions") [Depot](/wiki/Dex_Acquisitions_Depot "Dex Acquisitions Depot") on the planet [Meor Ain](/wiki/Meor_Ain "Meor Ain"), which she got inside by posing as a prisoner of Chewbacca, who was pretending to be a bounty hunter named "Violent Bok." There, they searched for the [Clawdite](/wiki/Clawdite "Clawdite") actor [Tunga Arpagion](/wiki/Tunga_Arpagion "Tunga Arpagion"). When they entered his cell to free him, Organa was stunned to see him impersonating her father.[[130]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_45-130) Knowing it was Arpagion, Organa punched the Clawdite in the face for his trick. They stunned Arpagion and brought him aboard the *Millennium Falcon*, where Organa convinced Arpagion to aid them in their mission by impersonating Moff [Tan Hubi](/wiki/Tan_Hubi "Tan Hubi"), whose bio-signature would allow them access to the prison to free the captive King. Then, Organa explained her plan, which was to attend an opera on Mon Cala where Hubi would be attending, where they would kidnap Hubi and have Arpagion double the Moff at the party while they took the real Moff to free Lee-Char.[[131]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_46-131)

 [![The Heroes of Yavin arriving on Strokill Prime](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/35/StrokillPrimesSurface-2015StarWars46.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190306072942) [![The Heroes of Yavin arriving on Strokill Prime](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/35/StrokillPrimesSurface-2015StarWars46.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190306072942)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/35/StrokillPrimesSurface-2015StarWars46.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190306072942) 

The Heroes of Yavin arriving on Strokill Prime

 

Organa sent R2 and C-3PO in as server droids to give Hubi a drug in his favorite drink, a [grabd accelerator](/wiki/Grabd_accelerator "Grabd accelerator"). She then watched Skywalker, Solo, and Chewbacca as they snuck through the ventilation and kidnapped Moff Hubi from the [refresher](/wiki/Refresher "Refresher") at the [Moncaladrome](/wiki/Moncaladrome "Moncaladrome"). After Arpagion took the Moff's place, Organa and her team left the Moncaladrome and went to the planet [Strokill Prime](/wiki/Strokill_Prime "Strokill Prime").[[131]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_46-131)

Organa, the captive Hubi, and her crew traveled in a submersible to the [Imperial base](/wiki/Unidentified_Imperial_base_(Strokill_Prime) "Unidentified Imperial base (Strokill Prime)"). Avoiding sea monsters, they arrived at the facility and infiltrated it using codes from Trios but found King Lee-Char imprisoned and on life support.[[132]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_47-132) Organa talked with Lee-Char, regretfully informing him of Raddus' death and pleading him to pledge to them the Mon Cala Mercantile Fleet to support the Rebellion. Lee-Char was eager to help but admitted he could not move because of all the machines he was hooked up to. Skywalker hunted down a camera droid where Lee-Char's message to his people will be recorded. However, Hubi clicked a button on the wall that alerted Imperial forces that the Moff Hubi on Mon Cala was an impostor. Stormtroopers stormed into the cell, killing Lee-Char as he finished his message and accidentally killing Moff Hubi. Organa led the crew back to their ship, barely escaping the planet.[[133]](#cite_note-SW48-133)

Meanwhile, Arpagion was exposed as an impostor, but was saved by the recently arrived rebels. Urtya, with a change of heart, played Lee-Char's recording and the Mercantile Fleet attempted to push through the Imperial blockade over the planet.[[133]](#cite_note-SW48-133) With the aid of Organa, Ackbar, and the rebel fleet, part of the fleet escaped to join the rebellion.[[134]](#cite_note-SW49-134)

#### Mako-Ta Space Docks[]

With twelve new Mon-Calamari cruisers, the rebels grouped their forces on the [Mako-Ta Space Docks](/wiki/Mako-Ta_Space_Docks "Mako-Ta Space Docks") and finished outfitting their ships with hyperdrives courtesy of Queen Trios. Organa and the rest of High Command decided to throw a party for the troops before their forces dispersed. After a speech from Mothma prepared Ackbar's [Alpha Group](/wiki/Alpha_Group "Alpha Group"), General Dodanna's [Beta Group](/wiki/Beta_Group "Beta Group"), General [Hera Syndulla](/wiki/Hera_Syndulla "Hera Syndulla")'s [Gamma Group](/wiki/Gamma_Group "Gamma Group"), and General [Vanden Willard's](/wiki/Vanden_Huyck_Willard "Vanden Huyck Willard") [Delta Group](/wiki/Delta_Group "Delta Group") to depart, they discovered that their hyperdrives had all been sabotaged and that Trios had gone missing. Organa helplessly watched as the cruisers saw their hangar doors, comm systems, [artillery batteries](/wiki/Artillery_battery "Artillery battery"), hyperspace systems, and propulsion engines be shut down and the Empire's [Death Squadron](/wiki/Death_Squadron "Death Squadron") led by Darth Vader and his command ship, the [*Executor*-class Star Dreadnought](/wiki/Executor-class_Star_Dreadnought "Executor-class Star Dreadnought") *[Executor](/wiki/Executor "Executor")* arrive in the system.[[135]](#cite_note-SW_50-135)

Vader quickly destroyed Willard's flagship *[Yavin's Hope](/wiki/Yavin%27s_Hope "Yavin's Hope")*. Trios fled back to her ship and ordered her men to launch, but a rebel strike team led by Organa and Colonel [Bandwin Cor](/wiki/Bandwin_Cor "Bandwin Cor") boarded her ship, killing her men. Trios managed to get to an escape pod and told Organa to forgive her, saying she would do anything to ensure that Shu-Torun would not become the next Alderaan before escaping.[[136]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_51-136)

Organa watched as ships commanded by [Lajaie](/wiki/Lajaie "Lajaie") and [Bob Hudsol](/wiki/Bob_Hudsol "Bob Hudsol") were destroyed. Eventually, the rebels found an override to the closed bay doors and Organa again looked on as Skywalker led the newly minted [Rogue Squadron](/wiki/Rogue_Squadron "Rogue Squadron") to combat the enemy. Then, a rebel technician broke into Trios' files and discovered an override code that would make all their systems operational again. However, the codes were only on the *Executor*. Organa devised a plan, in which she and Draven would lead a squad of [Special Forces](/wiki/Rebel_Alliance_Special_Forces "Rebel Alliance Special Forces") commandos to the *Executor*, in Trios' shuttle for disguise, to steal the codes and return to the ship.[[137]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_53-137)

As the group gets clearance to land on the *Executor*, Vader returns to the ship to meet with Trios. In the hangar, the rebels killed the Imperial officer who greeted them, but are soon faced by Vader. The rebels fled and attempted to access a computer inside, where they obtained the codes while the rearguard was caught by Vader. Organa led their remaining forces to the hangar to find a ship to escape, but they found only a lone TIE fighter. Draven then told Organa that he and the special forces would stay behind to let her escape with the codes. She flew back in the stolen TIE, but Skywalker got on her tail and tried to shoot her down. Unable to communicate with them because she did not have a TIE pilot helmet, Organa demonstrated her loyalties by shooting down another TIE. Skywalker deduced it was a friendly and ordered Rogue Squadron to form up on him and protect the TIE. They landed[[138]](#cite_note-SW_54-138) on the [MC80A Home One Type Heavy Star Cruiser](/wiki/MC80A_Home_One_Type_Heavy_Star_Cruiser "MC80A Home One Type Heavy Star Cruiser") [*Republic*](/wiki/Republic_(MC80A_Home_One_Type_Heavy_Star_Cruiser) "Republic (MC80A Home One Type Heavy Star Cruiser)").[[139]](#cite_note-SW_55-139) Organa alerted the commander of the ship, General Dodonna of the codes she obtained, and their ship escaped the system.[[138]](#cite_note-SW_54-138)

Organa and Skywalker were both shocked to hear Dodonna tell them that they could not risk their ship to go back and attempt to rescue their remaining forces. They eventually convinced him to go help, with the *Republic* serving as a distraction to allow Organa to lead a group of shuttles to rescue forces off the Space Docks. With the losses sustained by the Alliance leadership, Motham contacted Organa to promote her to the rank of general.[[139]](#cite_note-SW_55-139)

#### Saponza's Gang[]

:   "*I am Princess Leia Organa of the Rebel Alliance. I do hope you haven't been fooled by the Empire's propoganda. Vital medical supplies are being hoarded off-world at a Cartel Den. For this mission, and some others, heroes of the Rebellion will assist you.*"
:   ―Princess Leia Organa, recruiting Saponza's forces to aid in a mission to Dandoran[[140]](#cite_note-Commander-140)

Organa was responsible for recruiting [Saponza's Gang](/wiki/Tatooine_rebel_cell "Tatooine rebel cell") to the Alliance. Working with Solo, Mothma, [Jennica Pierce](/wiki/Jennica_Pierce "Jennica Pierce"), and the criminal underworld, the gang successfully rescued former Senator [Johhar Kessen](/wiki/Johhar_Kessen "Johhar Kessen") from Imperial custody. They also disrupted [Kosh](/wiki/Kosh "Kosh")'s contraband smuggling operation, and [liberated](/wiki/Battle_for_Tatooine "Battle for Tatooine") Tatooine from Imperial control. Following the gang's final victory at [Fort Ironhand](/wiki/Fort_Ironhand "Fort Ironhand"), Organa sent the gang a congratulatory holo message.[[140]](#cite_note-Commander-140)

#### Lotho Minor investigation[]

:   "*I think I'm ready to give up on this planet now.*"
:   ―Leia Organa[[141]](#cite_note-The_Planet_of_Misfit_Droids-141)

At some point, Leia, Han, Luke, Chewbacca, C-3PO were sent by the Alliance to Restore the Republic to investigate the planet [Lotho Minor](/wiki/Lotho_Minor "Lotho Minor") for a new base. When they arrived, Solo disparaged the planet and teased Organa, to which she retorted that the *Millenium Falcon* fit in on the garbage planet. Refusing to give up on the planet and ignoring Solo's complaints about strategy, they continued investigating until they ran into native [droids](/wiki/Droid "Droid") and a male Duros named [Akar Duel](/wiki/Akar_Duel "Akar Duel"). Duel, wanting to take the *Falcon*, had the droids pull their blasters on Organa and the others. After the droids turned on Duel once they learned from C-3PO that they could be independent, they boarded the *Falcon* to leave the planet, Organa concluding that Lotho Minor was not a good location for a rebel base.[[141]](#cite_note-The_Planet_of_Misfit_Droids-141)

#### Bogano[]

At some point, Leia visited [Bogano](/wiki/Bogano "Bogano"), a grassy planet in the [Outer Rim Territories](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories"), to find out if the world could host a rebel base. Upon arrival, Leia found her friend and fellow rebel Luke Skywalker. Although Skywalker was supposed to be checking out other worlds, he said the Force took him to Bogano. Leia and Luke then found a small animal and decided to follow it. The pair ended up arriving at the [Bogano Vault](/wiki/Bogano_Vault "Bogano Vault"), where Leia and Luke expressed their opinions about the planet. Leia turned out to be wrong about building a rebel base there, as the little animal led them to some stormtroopers who were dealing with several animals of the same species, showing that the Empire knew of the planet's existence.[[142]](#cite_note-The_Princess_and_the_Bog,_A_Twin_Tale,_Part_1-142) Along with Luke, Leia defeated the stormtroopers, who intended to sell the animals on the black market, and then left the planet to continue her quest of find a location for a rebel base.[[143]](#cite_note-The_Princess_and_the_Bog,_A_Twin_Tale,_Part_2-143)

### End of the Emperor's reign[]

#### A new base[]

:   "*Listen, I know we've all been spread pretty thin, but we've made it through. It's okay to feel tired. It's okay to feel weak. It doesn't erase the hero I see in each and every one of you. While we wait for better days, remember, you're not alone. The day we forget we have each other…is the day we lose.*"
:   ―Princess Leia Organa[[144]](#cite_note-FoD_Leia-144)

Roughly three [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") after the Battle of Yavin,[[3]](#cite_note-Timelines-3) Organa helped oversee the construction of the Rebellion's recently established [Echo Base](/wiki/Echo_Base "Echo Base") on the ice planet of [Hoth](/wiki/Hoth "Hoth"). When [Kes Dameron](/wiki/Kes_Dameron "Kes Dameron") and [Shara Bey](/wiki/Shara_Bey "Shara Bey") became trapped while carving out an ice tunnel for with an A-Wing laser cannon, Organa spoke to them after their rescue by [Heroes of Yavin](/wiki/Heroes_of_Yavin "Heroes of Yavin") Luke Skywalker and Chewbacca, reaffirming their value as fellow Rebels.[[145]](#cite_note-An_Echo_of_Victory-145) Present at the base was also a new rebel recruit named [Vulaada Klam](/wiki/Vulaada_Klam "Vulaada Klam"),[[146]](#cite_note-Aphra_2016_40-146) who helped herd [tauntauns](/wiki/Tauntaun "Tauntaun")[[147]](#cite_note-Epilogue-147)—which the rebels had begun using as mounts[[144]](#cite_note-FoD_Leia-144)—with her pet [Qaberworm](/wiki/Qaberworm "Qaberworm") [Gurtyl](/wiki/Gurtyl "Gurtyl"). Captain [Magna Tolvan](/wiki/Magna_Tolvan "Magna Tolvan") ordered the Qaberworm be killed at one point, but Organa noticed how skilled Klam and Gurtyl were in herding.[[147]](#cite_note-Epilogue-147) Additionally, Gurtyl was incredibly important to Klam.[[148]](#cite_note-Aphra_2016_27-148) In the end, Organa overruled Tolvan's order and allowed Klam to continue working with her pet, which Tolvan learned from a fellow rebel after returning to Echo Base after a mission.[[147]](#cite_note-Epilogue-147)

At some point during her time on Echo Base, the reactor in the base failed due to cold temperatures causing the heaters to become non-functional. Due to this, Rebel personnel had to be moved onto ships. Organa moved tauntauns onto the *Millennium Falcon*, despite Solo's complaints. She received transmissions from the repair crew through the *Falcon*'s cockpit. They informed her of the reactor being that of a [YT-2600](/wiki/YT-2600 "YT-2600"), and that it would explode and irradiate the base in a matter of ten minutes. Solo and Chewbacca volunteer to replace the [dissipator](/wiki/Electro_dissipator "Electro dissipator"), with a spare they stored on the *Falcon*. Minutes later, Solo informed Organa that they needed to evacuate the base immediately without telling her what they had done. Despite wanting Solo to return to the ship, Organa ordered the base to be evacuated without Solo. A few minutes later, Solo tells Organa that the reactor had been stabilized and that they were able to enter the base once again.[[149]](#cite_note-SW_12_2020-149)

With the hard working conditions and low temperatures weighing on Organa's mind, she made a speech to others at Echo Base about perseverance. Two days later, while on a tauntaun patrol with Han Solo and Hera Syndulla, Organa learned how to properly exercise control over the riding beast.[[144]](#cite_note-FoD_Leia-144)

After Chewbacca went missing, Organa and R2-D2 searched for him in the corridors of Echo Base. The two soon found a door which appeared to have been severely damaged. Organa entered and found Chewbacca in the arms of a sleeping [wampa](/wiki/Wampa "Wampa"). Organa woke the wampa accidentally. As Chewbacca and R2-D2 tried to repair the door, Organa distracted the wampa. She ran out into the corridor. The wampa followed, but with the help of R2, the door closed in on the wampa cave.[[150]](#cite_note-Beasts_of_Echo_Base-150)

#### Battle of Hoth[]

:   "*Han, we need you!*"  
    "*We need?*"  
    "*Yes.*"  
    "*Well, what about you need me?*"  
    "*I need? I don't know what you're talking about.*"  
    "*You probably don't.*"
:   ―Leia Organa and Han Solo[[151]](#cite_note-Episode_V-151)

 [![Organa in Echo Base](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/de/Rieekan-hd.png/revision/latest?cb=20130321041033) [![Organa in Echo Base](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/de/Rieekan-hd.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/320?cb=20130321041033)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/de/Rieekan-hd.png/revision/latest?cb=20130321041033) 

Organa in Echo Base

 

Following a run-in with one of Jabba's bounty hunters in [Ord Mantell](/wiki/Ord_Mantell "Ord Mantell"), Solo bade farewell to General [Carlist Rieekan](/wiki/Carlist_Rieekan "Carlist Rieekan") and Organa, but her lack of honesty about her feelings angered him. However, when no one could find Skywalker after his patrol, Solo set out[[151]](#cite_note-Episode_V-151) on the [Tauntaun](/wiki/Tauntaun "Tauntaun") [Murra](/wiki/Murra "Murra")[[152]](#cite_note-SWKTW-152) to find his friend during the night, worrying Organa.[[151]](#cite_note-Episode_V-151) While they were missing, [Rogue Two](/wiki/Rogue_Two "Rogue Two") [Zev Senesca](/wiki/Zev_Senesca "Zev Senesca")—the squadron leader of Skywalker's Rogue Squadron during his absence—erased their current betting pool concerning how soon Organa would tire of Solo's attempts at impressing her, replacing it with a pool concerning which of them would find Skywalker first. Though several of the pilots wrote their names, [Rogue Four](/wiki/Rogue_Four "Rogue Four") [Derek Klivian](/wiki/Derek_Klivian "Derek Klivian") objected to the pool, feeling it was a morbid game over their commander's life. Before Senesca could respond, Organa revealed she was standing at the doorway by stating the pool was not morbid. She walked in and explained that, by betting in the pool, the pilots were certain Skywalker was alive. Taking the marker from Senesca, she bet on every pilot, explaining it was what she and the other Rebel leaders did every day. Certain that Rogue Squadron would find Skywalker and Solo, and as everyone watched her, she gave the marker back and bid the Force be with them. After she left, every remaining pilot added their name to the pool.[[153]](#cite_note-Rogue_Two-153)

The following morning, Senesca located Skywalker and Solo, and Organa was relieved when they returned to the base. However, as an Imperial [probe droid](/wiki/XJ9-CS14 "XJ9-CS14") had alerted Vader and the [Imperial fleet](/wiki/Imperial_Navy "Imperial Navy") of their location, arriving soon on Hoth, Organa helped coordinate the ensuing evacuation, giving instructions to pilots,[[151]](#cite_note-Episode_V-151) and signaled the ships to leave the planet.[[154]](#cite_note-SYWtBaJ?-154) Once the base was [overrun](/wiki/Battle_of_Hoth "Battle of Hoth") by Imperial ground forces, Organa and C-3PO were forced to escape Hoth aboard the *Millennium Falcon* with Solo and Chewbacca.[[151]](#cite_note-Episode_V-151)

#### Escaping the Empire[]

:   "*You like me because I'm a scoundrel. There aren't enough scoundrels in your life.*"
:   ―Han Solo[[151]](#cite_note-Episode_V-151)

 [![Organa and Solo's first kiss](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cd/Hanleiafalcon.png/revision/latest?cb=20130324024232) [![Organa and Solo's first kiss](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cd/Hanleiafalcon.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130324024232)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cd/Hanleiafalcon.png/revision/latest?cb=20130324024232) 

Organa and Solo's first kiss

 

With a damaged [hyperdrive](/wiki/Hyperdrive "Hyperdrive"), the *Falcon* was unable to leave the [system](/wiki/Hoth_system "Hoth system") and escape the Imperial [blockade](/wiki/Blockade "Blockade"), which prompted Solo to pilot the ship into a nearby [asteroid field](/wiki/Hoth_asteroid_field "Hoth asteroid field"), hoping that the Imperials would be unwilling to follow them, to repair the ship in the cave of an asteroid of great size. Using a [fusioncutter](/wiki/Fusioncutter "Fusioncutter"), Organa helped in repairing the ship, when Solo appeared, drawing closer to her before both ended up in a passionate kiss that lasted until C-3PO's arrival. Organa withdrew and walked away, conflicted. Afterwards, Organa would reflect upon what happened in the [cockpit](/wiki/Cockpit "Cockpit") when the ship was attacked by [mynocks](/wiki/Mynock "Mynock").[[151]](#cite_note-Episode_V-151)

Rushing to shoo them away, Organa, Solo, and Chewbacca exited the ship, but Solo quickly realized that they were inside something other than a [cave](/wiki/Cave "Cave"). Narrowly escaping the "cave," which was really the inside of an [exogorth](/wiki/Exogorth "Exogorth")[[151]](#cite_note-Episode_V-151) named [Sy-O](/wiki/Sy-O "Sy-O"), who wanted them to stay as beloved parts of its internal ecosystem,[[155]](#cite_note-This_Is_No_Cave-155) and the asteroid Sy-O resided in, the *Millennium Falcon* was once again pursued by Imperial forces. Unable to make the jump to hyperspace due to unfinished repairs, Solo decided to land on the back of the command [bridge](/wiki/Bridge_(starship) "Bridge (starship)") of the *[Avenger](/wiki/Avenger "Avenger")*, shutting down all systems to avoid detection. The plan worked; as the Imperial fleet prepared to exit the [Anoat system](/wiki/Anoat_system "Anoat system"), Solo detached the ship from the hull. With a faulty hyperdrive, the group decided to go to the [Bespin system](/wiki/Bespin_system "Bespin system"), where an old acquaintance of Solo, [Lando Calrissian](/wiki/Landonis_Balthazar_Calrissian "Landonis Balthazar Calrissian"), owned a [mining](/wiki/Mining "Mining") colony. However, they were unaware that they were being tracked by [Boba Fett](/wiki/Boba_Fett "Boba Fett"), one of the [mercenaries](/wiki/Mercenary "Mercenary") hired by Vader to locate them.[[151]](#cite_note-Episode_V-151)

#### Escaping to Cloud City and Rendezvous Point Delta-Three[]

:   "*But this isn't your ship. With Han gone, I'm commandeering it for the Rebel fleet, which means you don't get a say in where it goes. And, of course, you betrayed us to the Empire. No one here is likely to forget that anytime soon.*"
:   ―Leia Organa speaking to Lando Calrissian after the escape from Bespin[[156]](#cite_note-SW_1_2020-156)

 [![Leia on Cloud City](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/71/LeiaBespin-TESB40.png/revision/latest?cb=20211224205540) [![Leia on Cloud City](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/71/LeiaBespin-TESB40.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20211224205540)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/71/LeiaBespin-TESB40.png/revision/latest?cb=20211224205540) 

Leia on Cloud City

 

Arriving on [Bespin](/wiki/Bespin "Bespin"), Organa and the others were greeted by Calrissian, whom Organa was immediately skeptical of. He agreed to repair the hyperdrive of the *Millennium Falcon*, and in the meantime, Organa and the others stayed at [Cloud City](/wiki/Cloud_City "Cloud City"). However, unbeknownst to them, Calrissian had made a deal with Vader to hand over the rebels in exchange for non-interference from the Empire. Captured by Vader, where the Dark Lord waited for Skywalker's arrival, Leia and the others were taken to a [carbon-freezing](/wiki/Carbon-freezing "Carbon-freezing") [facility](/wiki/Carbon-freezing_chamber "Carbon-freezing chamber"), where Solo was to be frozen in [carbonite](/wiki/Carbonite "Carbonite") to test if the chambers were suitable for trapping Skywalker. As the smuggler was lowered into the freezing pit, Organa's parting words were "I love you," to which Solo responded that he knew. ([Listen](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/10/ILoveYouIKnow-ESB.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250405134536 "ILoveYouIKnow-ESB.flac") ([help](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Media_help "wikipedia:Wikipedia:Media help")·[info](/wiki/File:ILoveYouIKnow-ESB.flac "File:ILoveYouIKnow-ESB.flac"))).[[151]](#cite_note-Episode_V-151)

On their way to Vader's ship, Organa caught sight of a recently arrived Luke Skywalker and tried to warn him, but she, Chewbacca, and C-3PO were taken away by Imperial forces. Before long, Calrissian betrayed Vader by disarming the stormtroopers with the help of his men, setting the Rebels free. Though Chewbacca almost strangled Calrissian, Organa let him live when he told them of Solo's location at the [East Platform](/wiki/East_Platform "East Platform"). With R2-D2 joining them, they attempted to save the frozen Solo from being taken away by Fett, but they were too late—the bounty hunter had already left on the *[Slave I](/wiki/Slave_I "Slave I")* with Solo. All the while, [Skywalker dueled Vader](/wiki/Duel_on_Cloud_City "Duel on Cloud City") until he lost his [right hand](/wiki/Limb "Limb"), [lightsaber](/wiki/Skywalker_lightsaber "Skywalker lightsaber"), and learned that the Dark Lord was his father.[[151]](#cite_note-Episode_V-151)

 [![Leia Organa senses Luke Skywalker's distress.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/89/Leia19.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120110005332) [![Leia Organa senses Luke Skywalker's distress.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/89/Leia19.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20120110005332)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/89/Leia19.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120110005332) 

Leia Organa senses Luke Skywalker's distress.

 

Jumping down a shaft, Skywalker eventually ended up hanging on a [weather scanner vane](/wiki/Weather_scanner_vane "Weather scanner vane") below Cloud City and called Organa out of instinct. The princess, who was [escaping](/wiki/Escape_from_Cloud_City "Escape from Cloud City") aboard the *Millennium Falcon* with Chewbacca, R2-D2, C-3PO, and Calrissian, sensed Skywalker's presence through the Force, and they turned around to retrieve Skywalker at her insistence. Once they rescued Skywalker, the ship was chased by TIE/ln starfighters into orbit and confronted by the *Executor*. Thanks to the astromech droid, the hyperdrive worked, and the *Falcon* escaped the Imperial threat.[[151]](#cite_note-Episode_V-151) Aboard the *Falcon*, Organa was still angry at Calrissian for making his deal with the Empire and introduced him to Skywalker. She then comforted her friend, who chose not to tell her that Vader was his father, instead revealing to her that Obi-Wan Kenobi had not responded when he reached out. Organa was certain the Jedi Master would answer and that, if he did not, Skywalker was strong enough to find his own path. Knowing they could not save Solo but that they could help the rebellion, Organa ignored Calrissian's concerns about the Empire and chose to return to the Rebel fleet, commandeering the *Falcon* for the Alliance. She also reminded Calrissian that he had betrayed them to the Imperials, which was something she felt they would not move past for some time, though the Cloud City administrator felt he deserved credit for getting the team off Bespin.[[156]](#cite_note-SW_1_2020-156)

They arrived in the Mid Rim to meet with the [Fourth Division](/wiki/Fourth_Division "Fourth Division") at [Rendezvous Point Delta-Three](/wiki/Rendezvous_Point_Delta-Three "Rendezvous Point Delta-Three"). There, they assisted in helping the Division's and [Green Squadron's](/wiki/Green_Squadron_(Rebel_Alliance) "Green Squadron (Rebel Alliance)") ships in escaping Commander [Ellian Zahra](/wiki/Ellian_Zahra "Ellian Zahra")'s [Hunter Fleet](/wiki/Hunter_Fleet "Hunter Fleet")'s blockade. Organa then all of Zahra's TIEs chase after the *Falcon*. Organa and Skywalker manned the turrets as Calrissian and Chewbacca flew the *Falcon* into an attack run. Organa, the *Falcon*, the 4th division were able to escape. Though her other forces [had destroyed](/wiki/Battle_near_Malastare "Battle near Malastare") the [Eighth Division](/wiki/Eighth_Division "Eighth Division"), Zahra was forced to report her failure to Vader, who was aware of her hatred for Organa. Seeking to keep Skywalker alive, Vader allowed her to kill the Rebel princess if she could but informed her that the *Falcon* was off limits. Having escaped to [Backup Rendezvous Point Gamma-Nine](/wiki/Backup_Rendezvous_Point_Gamma-Nine "Backup Rendezvous Point Gamma-Nine"), Organa then went to meet with Commander [Grek](/wiki/Grek_(commodore) "Grek (commodore)") aboard his ship. They discussed how the Empire found them and the Eighth Division at Malastare, and Organa realized that the Empire had broken their codes. Thus, the rebels knew if any cell contacted another, both groups could be found and destroyed. Organa and the others were unable to warn the other scattered rebels because of this, and Calrissian even feared they could be all that remained of the Rebel Alliance.[[156]](#cite_note-SW_1_2020-156)

A short time afterward, Calrissian promised he would head to Tatooine to learn if Fett had delivered Solo to Jabba yet. If not, he intended to look for leads on the bounty hunter. Organa elected to stay behind to help the Rebel fleet, though she had Chewbacca go with their new ally to make sure he went to the desert world and then right back. Organa then spoke with Skywalker about getting a [prosthetic hand](/wiki/Cybernetics "Cybernetics"), though the young Jedi was still questioning himself after learning Vader was his father.[[157]](#cite_note-SW_2_2020-157) Organa, 3PO, and R2 accompanied Skywalker when he received the new hand and watched as Calrissian and Chewbacca left to find Solo aboard the *Millennium Falcon*.[[151]](#cite_note-Episode_V-151) Organa then spoke to Commander Grek's crew, pilots, and the Pathfinders about the Empire's continuing hunt for the Alliance. She proposed to find and contact the other cells without using their codes. Organa agreed to use Grek's [Operation Starlight](/wiki/Operation_Starlight "Operation Starlight").[[157]](#cite_note-SW_2_2020-157)

#### Return to Cloud City[]

 [![Organa frozen in carbonite](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d8/LeiaInCarbonite-2020StarWars3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20221013021624) [![Organa frozen in carbonite](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d8/LeiaInCarbonite-2020StarWars3.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/190?cb=20221013021624)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d8/LeiaInCarbonite-2020StarWars3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20221013021624) 

Organa frozen in carbonite

 

Organa, along with Calrissian, Skywalker, and R2 returned to Cloud City to assist Skywalker in recovering his lightsaber. After landing in Cloud City, she went to the [carbon-freezing chamber](/wiki/Carbon-freezing_chamber "Carbon-freezing chamber"). There, Organa studied how to work the decarbonization sequence. She was then found by a stormtrooper and stunned. Organa was frozen in carbonite.[[158]](#cite_note-SW_3_2020-158)

Organa and other prisoners were then freed from the carbonite by Skywalker. Organa led the prisoners in fighting the [Imperial Garrison's](/wiki/Imperial_Garrison_(Cloud_City) "Imperial Garrison (Cloud City)") stormtroopers and escaping aboard a *Sentinel*-class landing shuttle.[[159]](#cite_note-SW_4_2020-159)

Aboard a [Nebulon-B frigate](/wiki/EF76_Nebulon-B_escort_frigate "EF76 Nebulon-B escort frigate"), Organa greeted Skywalker after his [mission](/wiki/Mission_to_Tempes "Mission to Tempes") to [Tempes](/wiki/Tempes "Tempes"). Relieved at his return, she asked him to show the Alliance officers onboard his [newly acquired lightsaber](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker%27s_yellow_lightsaber "Luke Skywalker's yellow lightsaber"), to give her and them hope.[[160]](#cite_note-SW_6_2020-160)

#### Encounter with Zahra[]

Commander Grek received a transmission from the [Seventh Division](/wiki/Seventh_Division "Seventh Division"). Organa gave the orders to respond to the transmission, despite knowing that it would compromise their position. Organa, along with the Fourth Division joined the Seventh shortly after the [Hunter Fleet](/wiki/Hunter_Fleet "Hunter Fleet") began [their assault](/wiki/Battle_at_Elessia "Battle at Elessia") on the division.[[161]](#cite_note-SW_7_2020-161) During the battle, Organa's ship is boarded by Commander Zahra. She deactivated the safety controls on the ship's main reactor, and asked for Organa specifically. Knowing that the ship would explode if the reactor's limiters aren't reactivated, Organa agreed and entered the engine room with [Grek's blaster](/wiki/DL-44_heavy_blaster_pistol "DL-44 heavy blaster pistol").

 [![Organa being confronted by Commander Zahra](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ae/ZahraLeiaConfrontation-2020StarWars8.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20201206224434) [![Organa being confronted by Commander Zahra](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ae/ZahraLeiaConfrontation-2020StarWars8.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20201206224434)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ae/ZahraLeiaConfrontation-2020StarWars8.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20201206224434) 

Organa being confronted by Commander Zahra

 

As she entered, Zahra explained that she blamed Organa for the deaths of Tarkin and of her family. Before she can fully enact revenge, she is ordered to board her flagship, the *[Tarkin's Will](/wiki/Tarkin%27s_Will "Tarkin's Will")*, before the ship flees the battle. Skywalker comes to Organa's rescue and Zahra flees. Organa mentioned to Skywalker how much hatred she could see in her eyes, and how she felt this enemy was different.[[162]](#cite_note-SW_8_2020-162)

#### Operation Starlight[]

After the battle, Organa began Operation Starlight by discussing a plan to reunite the scattered Rebel divisions without using communication the Empire could intercept them with. She let C-3PO discuss [their plan to steal](/wiki/Heist_at_the_Imperial_Museum "Heist at the Imperial Museum") a [linguistic droid](/wiki/Autonomous_Translator_Module,_Mark_II "Autonomous Translator Module, Mark II") that could speak [Trawak](/wiki/Trawak "Trawak"), an extinct language. Organa sent Calrissian to use the *Millennium Falcon* for the mission.[[163]](#cite_note-SW_9_2020-163)

After the mission was a success and the [droid](/wiki/Linguistics_droid "Linguistics droid") was reactivated, Organa discussed with it the terms of his service and how he would translate messages for the Rebel Alliance. She then sent [Starlight Squadron](/wiki/Starlight_Squadron "Starlight Squadron") on a mission to check rendezvous points for Rebel cells and given them the new Trawak codes if found.[[164]](#cite_note-SW_10_2020-164) When Starlight Squadron is [ambushed](/wiki/Ambush_near_Felucia "Ambush near Felucia") and [Lobot](/wiki/Lobot "Lobot") started to die from being interfaced with the linguistic droid, Organa decided to have the droid contact the squadron, despite the possibility of Lobot dying. A fight broke out between Calrissian and Kes Dameron due to this, where Organa ordered Calrissian to be imprisoned for the time being. After C-3PO reconstructed the Trawak language and turned the linguistic droid off, Organa checked to see if Lobot was still alive, and had him taken to the medical bay where she realized he was. When Starlight Squadron was able to recontact the group aboard the frigate, they informed Organa and Dameron that Shara Bey had to be left behind on the *Tarkin's Will*. Organa reassured Dameron that his wife would be safe.[[165]](#cite_note-SW_11_2020-165)

Aboard the *Redemption*, Organa and Dameron talked about the people they loved, Poe Dameron, Shara Bey, and Han Solo. They exchanged stories about them, before being informed of a signal from Lieutenant Bey. Organa let Dameron speak to her first, after which he informed Organa of intelligence Bey had gathered during her stay on the *Tarkin's Will*.[[149]](#cite_note-SW_12_2020-149)

#### Auction for Han Solo[]

Organa received a message from Amilyn Holdo which indicated that Solo was to be [put on auction](/wiki/Auction_for_Han_Solo "Auction for Han Solo") by [Crimson Dawn](/wiki/Crimson_Dawn "Crimson Dawn"). She showed Skywalker, Chewbacca, and C-3PO the holomessage aboard the *Millennium Falcon*. Translated by C-3PO, Chewbacca told Organa and Skywalker about his past encounters with Crimson Dawn, and that he suggested enlisting Calrissian's help in dealing with them. She sent Chewbacca to talk to him. Skywalker talked with Organa, concerned over the mission and for her wellbeing. She reassured him that both would be okay.[[166]](#cite_note-SW_14_2020-166)

In the cockpit of the *Millennium Falcon*, Organa and Calrissian discussed about their approach to getting Han Solo back. Once they exited hyperspace, they noticed that multiple capital ships from multiple crime syndicates had arrived to bet on Han Solo. They tried to fly to the far side of the planet to avoid detection, but a Black Sun ship exited hyperspace right in front of them. The *Millennium Falcon* was able to escape oncoming Black Sun fighters, and crash land on the [Jekara](/wiki/Jekara "Jekara")'s surface.[[166]](#cite_note-SW_14_2020-166)

#### Operation Yellow Moon[]

:   "*You make the Alliance proud every day. By representing our cause—and by doing your duty. But duty won't give you comfort, Leia—and you need that. We all do. The comfort of friends—and of love. You were Bail and Breha's greatest joy, Leia—the love you shared was what sustained them through the dark years. Don't deny yourself another chance at love because of what the Empire did to them. Don't give Palpatine that victory, too.*"
:   ―Mon Mothma, encouraging Organa not to give up her love for Solo[[18]](#cite_note-Moving_Target-18)

Following Mothma and the Rebel leadership's order to scatter the fleet, Organa and C-3PO were on Captain [Volk Aymeric](/wiki/Volk_Aymeric "Volk Aymeric")'s Nebulon-B frigate, the *[Remembrance](/wiki/Remembrance "Remembrance")*, when the ship and the rest of the convoy were [attacked](/wiki/Skirmish_in_an_unidentified_system "Skirmish in an unidentified system") by TIE fighters; despite the *[Ranolfo](/wiki/Ranolfo "Ranolfo")*'s critical condition, Aymeric was forced to abandon them to protect Organa. She was then informed that she had to rendezvous with the rest of the Alliance leadership on [Zastiga](/wiki/Zastiga "Zastiga"), her transport pilots being Nien Nunb and Lieutenant Ematt. On the *Mellcrawler*, they reached the planet, wherein Organa was greeted by R2-D2 and Skywalker, who told her that Calrissian was attempting to infiltrate [Jabba's Palace](/wiki/Boba_Fett%27s_Palace "Boba Fett's Palace") to acquire more information on Solo's location, just before escorting her to the top-clearance meeting.[[18]](#cite_note-Moving_Target-18)

 [![Meeting with Alliance High Command](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c9/Death_Star_II_revealed.png/revision/latest?cb=20210613165516) [![Meeting with Alliance High Command](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c9/Death_Star_II_revealed.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20210613165516)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c9/Death_Star_II_revealed.png/revision/latest?cb=20210613165516) 

Meeting with Alliance High Command

 

During the gathering, Organa and the Generals were informed of the construction of the [second Death Star](/wiki/DS-2_Death_Star_II_Mobile_Battle_Station "DS-2 Death Star II Mobile Battle Station"), located over [Endor](/wiki/Endor "Endor")—which, they knew, had to be destroyed before it became operational. After swearing to secrecy, Organa was escorted by Skywalker to her quarters, where she devised a strategy to present at the meeting the day after—[Operation Yellow Moon](/wiki/Operation_Yellow_Moon "Operation Yellow Moon")—to divert the Imperial attention to her, instead of the upcoming mission to Endor. After a confidential exchange with Mothma, Organa was allowed to take part in the mission, her crew consisting of Nien Nunb, [Kidi Aleri](/wiki/Kidi_Aleri "Kidi Aleri"), [Antrot](/wiki/Antrot "Antrot"), and Major [Lokmarcha](/wiki/Lokmarcha "Lokmarcha").[[18]](#cite_note-Moving_Target-18)

While in hyperspace Leia read up on intel for their mission. A fight broke out between Kidi and Lokmarcha. Kidi was discussing her former colleagues in the Imperial Intel Agency and how she wished for them to be given amnesty after the war. The [Dressellian](/wiki/Dressellian "Dressellian") said that they would face prison or a firing squad if he was in charge.
