Leia settled the fight and told them that they would face that issue after every single General, Admiral, and Moff had surrendered, and the [Imperial Starfleet](/wiki/Imperial_Navy "Imperial Navy") and [Stormtrooper Corps](/wiki/Stormtrooper_Corps "Stormtrooper Corps") had been defeated.[[18]](#cite_note-Moving_Target-18)

They soon reached [Basteel](/wiki/Basteel "Basteel")'s capital, [Eladro City](/wiki/Eladro_City "Eladro City"), where she met with [Bon Yoth](/wiki/Bon_Yoth "Bon Yoth") to know where to place the first [hyper-transceiver](/wiki/Hyperwave_transceiver "Hyperwave transceiver")—in the cave system above [his house](/wiki/Bon_Yoth%27s_house "Bon Yoth's house"). They had to climb one Kilometer up to the surface. During this, some sort of night feeders attacked her. She quickly got up to the surface where they ran from the light. The temperature began to drop as the sun set, but Nein Numb arrived in the *Mellcrawler* just as the sun finally set. They were Successful in their ordeal, but now tailed by [Khione](/wiki/Khione "Khione") and her *[Shieldmaiden](/wiki/Shieldmaiden "Shieldmaiden").* They continued onto the [Sesid system](/wiki/Sesid_system "Sesid system"), where they placed another transceiver in a [volcanic](/wiki/Volcano "Volcano") island on [Sesid](/wiki/Sesid "Sesid"). They were soon chased by Imperials until the intervention of [Aurelant](/wiki/Aurelant "Aurelant") and his [Draedan](/wiki/Draedan "Draedan") [pirates](/wiki/Pirate "Pirate") on the *[Daggadol](/wiki/Daggadol "Daggadol")*. At first, they thought the Draedans would sell them off, but thanks to his maneuver to get them off-planet on Sesid's special escape pods they made their way to [Jaresh](/wiki/Jaresh "Jaresh"), where they met with [Nyessa](/wiki/Nyessa "Nyessa"), placed the last transceiver, and took part of the Riot on Jaresh, after which the *Shieldmaiden* tried and failed catch the *Mellcrawler*.[[18]](#cite_note-Moving_Target-18)

 [![Prisoner of the Shieldmaiden](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e8/Leia_on_the_Shieldmaiden.png/revision/latest?cb=20210613164745) [![Prisoner of the Shieldmaiden](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e8/Leia_on_the_Shieldmaiden.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/190?cb=20210613164745)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e8/Leia_on_the_Shieldmaiden.png/revision/latest?cb=20210613164745) 

Prisoner of the *Shieldmaiden*

 

After briefing her team about the true mission Organa decided to change the operation, warning any incoming Rebel ships to abandon the place. Once in the rendezvous point on [Galaan](/wiki/Galaan "Galaan")'s orbit, they warned the *[Sapphire Rogue](/wiki/Sapphire_Rogue "Sapphire Rogue")* and other ships before being caught in the *Shieldmaiden*'s tractor beam. They were taken aboard the star destroyer and taken to interrogation rooms. Khione went into Leia's cell and brought Lokmarcha inside. The commando had hidden an ion bomb inside of his clothing and sacrificed himself. Leia took the captain's uniform and Antrot, Nein, and Kidi pretended to be her prisoners. When stormtroopers realized the ploy, Antrot ran as a distraction and was shot as Nein launched off in the shuttle *[Tydirium](/wiki/Tydirium "Tydirium")*. All the ships they had warned, returned, and destroyed the Shieldmaiden.[[18]](#cite_note-Moving_Target-18)

With Aleri's help, Organa then contacted Skywalker, who informed her that most of the fleet was nearly assembled, and that Solo was still frozen in carbonite in Jabba's palace. They arranged a rendezvous on [Kothlis](/wiki/Kothlis "Kothlis"), where he would inform her of his plan to rescue Solo.[[18]](#cite_note-Moving_Target-18) Although Mothma tried to talk Organa out of the dangerous plan,[[29]](#cite_note-BtPotDS!-29) they nevertheless carried on with it.[[11]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-11)

#### Visit to Ord Mantell[]

Carrying out the rescue of Han Solo, Leia required an adequate disguise to fool Jabba the Hutt. Because of this, Organa, Chewbacca, and the droid R2-D2 traveled to Ord Mantell to meet [Maz Kanata](/wiki/Maz_Kanata "Maz Kanata"), who was the one to provide her with the disguise. Leia proceeded to ask Kanata how she would provide them with a cover story for Jabba, with Maz cautioning patience. At that moment, the bounty hunter [Boushh](/wiki/Boushh "Boushh") fired shots at the group. While hiding behind crates, Kanata explained to Leia that the bounty hunter would be the source of her disguise. Chewbacca and Organa engaged the bounty hunter while R2-D2 operated a crane. Leia managed to shoot the blaster out of Boushh's hand, leading to the bounty hunter charging the princess with a lance. After fighting Boushh for a bit, Leia ducked out of the fight to let R2-D2 disable the bounty hunter with a crane. Afterwards, Organa used Boushh's armor as her disguise. She thanked Kanata for her help in getting her an outfit, and then left aboard the *Millennium Falcon*.[[167]](#cite_note-Bounty_Hunted-167)

#### Detour to Arkanis[]

En route from Ord Mantell to Tatooine, Leia was contacted by [Evaan Verlaine](/wiki/Evaan_Verlaine "Evaan Verlaine"). Rebel Alliance command received word from [Lando Calrissian](/wiki/Landonis_Balthazar_Calrissian "Landonis Balthazar Calrissian") that his ship had been shot down by bounty hunters on [Arkanis](/wiki/Arkanis "Arkanis"), and he was on the run. Leia contacted Lando to tell him they were coming for him. In a clearing, Lando ran into Leia in Boushh's outfit, believing her to be the bounty hunter. He tried to fight but Leia knocked him down before revealing herself. She led him back toward the *Falcon*, finally giving him an earful about Han's predicament. Everything at Cloud City was a "beautiful double cross" that had relied on Han surviving in his usual ways, Lando explained, but he hadn't anticipated the carbonite freezing. Leia chastised him for relying on schemes, and Lando countered that scoundrels try to make things work as best as they can. They heard Chewbacca captured by bounty hunters in the distance, who dragged him to a cantina to meet with their boss, [Bossk](/wiki/Bossk%27wassak%27Cradossk "Bossk'wassak'Cradossk"). Lando suggested she call in the Rebels to help, but she worried the Empire had too much of a presence in the area and that such an attack might have alerted Jabba and ruined any rescue plans.

Leia entered the cantina, disguised as Boushh to congratulate Bossk and question him about Calrissian. The Trandoshan said he could get to the smuggler later as Jabba's price on the Wookiee was substantial. "Boushh" left saying he would see Bossk on Tatooine. Suspicious, Bossk sent his crew after their associate, and they found "him" at a campfire with Calrissian tied up. The trap sprung, they fired on a decoy as Leia stunned them from behind with a [bolo](/wiki/Bola "Bola")-gun. But Bossk jumped down from his ship above. The two exchanged gunfire while Lando begged to be set free to fight. Leia hit some rocks that knocked Bossk down and jammed his blaster. As she tried to negotiate a swap for Chewbacca, Bossk's crew came to and fired at her. She shot both, wounding instead of killing them. As Lando got free, she knocked him to the ground and shot him in the chest. Believing Calrissian was dead, Bossk agreed to the swap, and the bounty hunters left. Lando sat up unharmed and impressed, remarking that Leia had "a little scoundrel in her."[[168]](#cite_note-Age_of_Rebellion_-_Princess_Leia_1-168)

#### Solo's rescue[]

:   "*We have powerful friends. You're gonna regret this.*"
:   ―Leia Organa, to Jabba the Hutt[[11]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-11)

 [![Organa plans the infiltration of Jabba's palace.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b1/ThePrincessGambit-ChrisTrevas.png/revision/latest?cb=20220503001202) [![Organa plans the infiltration of Jabba's palace.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b1/ThePrincessGambit-ChrisTrevas.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/190?cb=20220503001202)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b1/ThePrincessGambit-ChrisTrevas.png/revision/latest?cb=20220503001202) 

Organa plans the infiltration of Jabba's palace.

 

Following Calrissian, R2-D2, and C-3PO's infiltration at Jabba's Palace to [rescue Solo](/wiki/Rescue_of_Han_Solo "Rescue of Han Solo"), Organa arrived with Chewbacca as her "prisoner" to collect part of the bounty Jabba had put on Solo's head.[[11]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-11) Unknown to Organa, Fett had tipped off the [crime lord](/wiki/Crime_lord "Crime lord"); Jabba already knew that whoever was under Boushh's helmet wasn't him. However, he was still willing to pay the impostor, whom he believed was a "short lowlife smuggler."[[29]](#cite_note-BtPotDS!-29) Jabba offered 25,000 credits for Chewie, but Leia demanded 50,000 and no less. This angered Jabba, who knocked C-3PO to the ground. When Jabba asked her why he needed to pay 50,000, Leia took out a thermal detonator and threatened the crime lord, alarming his guests. Jabba laughed and offered 35,000 for the Wookiee, an offer Organa accepted. Chewie was taken by two [Gamorrean](/wiki/Gamorrean "Gamorrean") guards to be imprisoned.[[11]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-11)

Later that evening, Organa released Solo from his carbonite coffin. After revealing her identity, the two kissed. However, they were immediately caught by Jabba and his [court](/wiki/Jabba%27s_criminal_empire "Jabba's criminal empire"), prompting Organa to use her [armor](/wiki/Armor "Armor") to signal Skywalker and Calrissian that she had been captured.[[29]](#cite_note-BtPotDS!-29) After unsuccessfully trying to plead with Jabba, Solo was sent to the dungeons and placed in the same cell as Chewbacca.[[11]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-11) Meanwhile, having now seen Organa's true identity, Jabba decided that she would become his new favorite slave. As a guard brought her to Jabba, Organa tried to threaten him, but the Hutt replied sarcastically and licked her face. Jabba then ordered two of his servants, [Jess](/wiki/Jess "Jess") and [Damaris](/wiki/Damaris_Viell "Damaris Viell"), to have Organa prepared for enslavement.[[169]](#cite_note-Dune_Sea_Songs-169)

After being taken to the women's quarters, Organa was cleaned and dressed in a [dancing-girl costume](/wiki/Dancing-girl_costume "Dancing-girl costume").[[169]](#cite_note-Dune_Sea_Songs-169) During this time, Jess told her about how Jabba's favorite slave before her, [Oola](/wiki/Oola "Oola"), was killed when the gangster fed her to his [rancor](/wiki/Pateesa "Pateesa").[[170]](#cite_note-The_Chronicler-170) Jess also assured Organa that she would be treated well if she didn't cause trouble. Organa rejected her advice and insisted that Skywalker would rescue her soon. Once she was taken back to the audience chamber, Organa was chained to Jabba's [throne](/wiki/Jabba_the_Hutt%27s_dais "Jabba the Hutt's dais") and kept beside the gangster.[[169]](#cite_note-Dune_Sea_Songs-169) At some point, Jabba's [majordomo](/wiki/Majordomo "Majordomo") [Bib Fortuna](/wiki/Bib_Fortuna "Bib Fortuna") grumbled to Organa that he hoped she would be a better dancer than Oola.[[171]](#cite_note-Fortuna_Favors-171) Throughout the night, Organa resisted Jabba's attempts to draw her closer, though eventually they both grew tired and fell asleep.[[169]](#cite_note-Dune_Sea_Songs-169)

 [![Organa during her enslavement to Jabba the Hutt.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/33/JabbaLeia.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220213231503) [![Organa during her enslavement to Jabba the Hutt.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/33/JabbaLeia.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20220213231503)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/33/JabbaLeia.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220213231503) 

Organa during her enslavement to Jabba the Hutt.

 

The following morning, Jabba and Organa were awoken by Skywalker's arrival at the palace.[[172]](#cite_note-Star_Wars:_Return_of_the_Jedi_(paperback_novel)-172) He was presented before them by Fortuna, who was mind-tricked into granting Skywalker's entry. Organa watched in silence as Skywalker tried to convince Jabba to release his friends. Jabba refused to bargain with the Jedi and dropped him into a pit with his [rancor](/wiki/Rancor "Rancor"). While Skywalker managed to kill the beast, Jabba was enraged and punished Organa by strangling her with the chain that bound her. He declared that Skywalker, Solo, and Chewbacca were to be taken to the [Great Pit of Carkoon](/wiki/Great_Pit_of_Carkoon "Great Pit of Carkoon") and eaten alive by the [sarlacc](/wiki/Sarlacc "Sarlacc").[[11]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-11)

Though she was spared from execution, Organa was forced to accompany Jabba on his [sail barge](/wiki/Sail_barge "Sail barge"), the *[Khetanna](/wiki/Khetanna "Khetanna")*. Her friends were transported on a smaller [skiff](/wiki/Bantha-II_cargo_skiff "Bantha-II cargo skiff"). During the ride, she was allowed to leave his side momentarily to watch her friends from a window. Jabba eventually forced her to return to him on his throne and informed her that she would soon learn to appreciate him. The crime lord celebrated his plans by making Organa share a drink with him.[[11]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-11)

 [![Organa strangled Jabba to death.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e6/Leia_Kills_Jabba_ALNL.png/revision/latest?cb=20170906032506) [![Organa strangled Jabba to death.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e6/Leia_Kills_Jabba_ALNL.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20170906032506)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e6/Leia_Kills_Jabba_ALNL.png/revision/latest?cb=20170906032506) 

Organa strangled Jabba to death.

 

When they finally reached their destination, Organa patiently waited until Skywalker started attacking with his [new lightsaber](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker%27s_green_lightsaber "Luke Skywalker's green lightsaber"). She destroyed the barge's controls to throw the vessel into darkness and jumped over Jabba's tail. Grabbing the slack of the very chain with which Jabba had enslaved her, Organa threw its length around the crime lord's huge neck.[[11]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-11) Fueled by her hatred for Jabba, Organa unknowingly drew upon the dark side of the Force to gain strength while she strangled him to death.[[13]](#cite_note-Bloodline-13) Fortuna watched in awe as she choked and killed Jabba before growing fearful she would attack him next.[[171]](#cite_note-Fortuna_Favors-171) R2-D2 then broke the chain, and they headed for the top surface of the sail barge[[11]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-11) upon being called for by Skywalker, interrupting Fortuna's attempt to approach Organa; the majordomo, who had longed to kill Jabba himself, was considering applauding her method of execution to try and get into the Princess's good graces, as he had started to think she was going to claim the Hutt's throne for herself.[[171]](#cite_note-Fortuna_Favors-171) On the top surface, the astromech droid and C-3PO jumped off the vehicle's edge while Organa met with Skywalker. Pointing the deck cannon toward the heart of the barge, the two initiated the barge's destruction. They swung to the skiff where Calrissian, Chewbacca, and Solo awaited them. Picking up the two droids, they drove the [skiff](/wiki/Skiff "Skiff") off just as the *Khetanna* exploded[[11]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-11) while Fortuna, who nonetheless would manage to survive, watched.[[171]](#cite_note-Fortuna_Favors-171)

Organa later briefed the Rebel chronicler [Dora Mar](/wiki/Dora_Mar "Dora Mar") about the rescue mission. Organa told Mar about Jess, though she was unsure about whether or not she had survived. The princess also talked about Oola and asked Mar to make a record of her as well. Though Mar pointed out that the two weren't part of the Rebellion, Organa insisted they be added to their records because they were part of the story and wanted them to be remembered.[[170]](#cite_note-The_Chronicler-170)

#### Battle of Endor[]

:   "*Luke, don't talk that way. You have a power that I don't understand and can never have.*"  
    "*You're wrong, Leia. You have that power, too. In time, you will learn to use it as I have. The Force is strong in my family. My father has it. I have it. And… my sister has it. Yes. It's you, Leia.*"
:   ―Leia Organa and Luke Skywalker[[11]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-11)

Upon leaving Tatooine, Organa departed for Sullust with the rest of the crew (except for Skywalker and R2-D2) aboard the *Millennium Falcon* to reunite with the rest of the Rebel Alliance's fleet, assembling for its greatest operation yet—the assault on the second Death Star, located in the [Endor system](/wiki/Endor_system "Endor system"). During the briefing, she volunteered for Solo's ground assault to deactivate the [deflector shield](/wiki/Deflector_shield "Deflector shield") protecting the [space station](/wiki/Space_station "Space station"), as did Chewbacca and Skywalker (and his droids).[[11]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-11) Before the mission, Mothma tried to talk some sense into Organa on behalf of her deceased parents, even though she knew that Organa would refuse to listen to her advice.[[29]](#cite_note-BtPotDS!-29)

 [![Organa meets the Ewok Wicket on Endor.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a4/Ewok70.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110916181705) [![Organa meets the Ewok Wicket on Endor.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a4/Ewok70.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110916181705)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a4/Ewok70.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110916181705) 

Organa meets the Ewok Wicket on Endor.

 

Aboard the *Tydirium*, the team landed on the moon, as willed by Vader, aware of his son's presence on the shuttle. Making their way through the [forest](/wiki/Tree "Tree"), they came across Imperial [scout troopers](/wiki/Scout_trooper "Scout trooper"), whom Organa and Skywalker pursued on a stolen speeder bike. Though they took care of the troopers, the two were separated as she was thrown off her speeder and knocked unconscious. An [Ewok](/wiki/Ewok "Ewok"), [Wicket](/wiki/Wicket_Wystri_Warrick "Wicket Wystri Warrick"), woke her up, and Organa quickly befriended him. Though they were discovered by two other scouts, Organa and Wicket managed to get rid of them.[[11]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-11) While on their way to Wicket's home, [Bright Tree Village](/wiki/Bright_Tree_Village "Bright Tree Village"), they came across two other Ewoks who had been stopped by two stormtroopers. Wicket climbed a nearby tree and, with help from Organa, trapped the stormtroopers in a vine. When Organa, Wicket, and the two other Ewoks arrived at Bright Tree Village, they presented her with a dress as a gift for helping them escape the stormtroopers.[[173]](#cite_note-Ewok_Escape-173)

After a few hours, she realized that her friends were to become a banquet in C-3PO's honor, whom the Ewoks thought to be their [god](/wiki/Deity "Deity"). She tried to intervene, but they threatened her with [spears](/wiki/Spear "Spear"). They were only freed after Skywalker used the Force to levitate the [protocol droid](/wiki/Protocol_droid "Protocol droid") as a proof of his deific "[magic](/wiki/Magick "Magick")" to the tribe. Later that night, Organa listened as C-3PO told the Ewoks their story, prompting [Chief](/wiki/Chief "Chief") [Chirpa](/wiki/Chirpa "Chirpa") to proclaim them a part of the tribe.[[11]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-11)

 [![Organa about to learn the truth of her parentage](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1e/Luke_Leia_BTV_RotJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20190111003017) [![Organa about to learn the truth of her parentage](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1e/Luke_Leia_BTV_RotJ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190111003017)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1e/Luke_Leia_BTV_RotJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20190111003017) 

Organa about to learn the truth of her parentage

 

It was then that Skywalker decided the time had come for him to leave his friends and face Vader, and Organa followed him out of the tribal gathering and asked him what was troubling him. Skywalker then revealed that not only was Vader his father but hers as well, and that he was her brother, something she had somehow always known; he then left the village to face the Sith Lord in combat alone. Solo then appeared to question Organa, and became jealous of Skywalker, but soon apologized and comforted her.[[11]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-11)

The next day, Organa fought alongside the rest of the team in the [battle](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor "Battle of Endor") that followed their initial infiltration at the [shield generator](/wiki/Death_Star%27s_shield_generator "Death Star's shield generator") and subsequent capture by Imperial reinforcements. While the Ewoks provided a distraction long enough for them to take hold of their position at the doors, only for Solo's efforts to hotwire the machinery to fail, she was injured by a blaster shot[[11]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-11) fired by stormtrooper [GR-792](/wiki/GR-792 "GR-792")—who missed a killing shot because fellow trooper [RZ-440](/wiki/RZ-440 "RZ-440") accidentally kicked his leg[[174]](#cite_note-Ending_Protocol-174)—that hit her shoulder. Seemingly cornered by the two approaching stormtroopers, Organa hid her blaster from sight as they approached and listened as Solo confessed his love, after which she blasted both stormtroopers,[[11]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-11) killing GR-792 and knocking out RZ-440.[[174]](#cite_note-Ending_Protocol-174) With Chewbacca's stolen [All Terrain Scout Transport](/wiki/Tempest_Scout_2 "Tempest Scout 2"), they tricked the [officers](/wiki/Imperial_officer "Imperial officer") into letting them enter and destroy the shield generator, which in turn allowed Calrissian and Nunb, along with Antilles, to fly into the Death Star's core and destroy it from the inside.[[11]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-11)

#### Victory and marriage[]

:   "*Han?*"  
    "*I want you.*"  
    "*Me? For what?*"  
    "*Forever. Marry me.*"
:   ―Han's proposal to Leia[[51]](#cite_note-Princess_and_Scoundrel-51)

In the aftermath, Solo reassured Organa that Skywalker had surely survived, but she already knew it, as she felt her brother's presence through the Force. Solo told her he would not interfere in their relationship, but she informed Solo that Skywalker was her brother, and they shared a kiss. Afterwards, they arranged for the Alliance to join them at Bright Tree Village, where they celebrated their victory, and where Skywalker ultimately reunited with them. Organa and her friends took the chance to stand together after everything they had been through, smiling together at their victory.[[11]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-11)

 [![Organa's wedding dress](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2f/Leia-wedding-dress.png/revision/latest?cb=20221023004208) [![Organa's wedding dress](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2f/Leia-wedding-dress.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20221023004208)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2f/Leia-wedding-dress.png/revision/latest?cb=20221023004208) 

Organa's wedding dress

 

During the celebrations on Endor, Organa tried to discourage their Ewok allies from eating captured stormtroopers, and so she sent for Solo and Chewbacca to meet with General [Hera Syndulla](/wiki/Hera_Syndulla "Hera Syndulla") to gather food rations from her. Syndulla agreed but Solo had to admit that the *Ghost* was a better ship than the *Millennium Falcon*, and Solo reluctantly agreed. When Solo and Chewbacca returned with the food portions, Organa eased Solo by stating that the *Millennium Falcon* was the better ship and distributed the food portions to the Ewoks.[[175]](#cite_note-An_Imperial_Feast-175)

After the battle, Leia told Skywalker that the battle would have gone very differently if it weren't for the Ewoks. Two troubled Ewoks, Wicket and [Kneesaa](/wiki/Kneesaa_a_Jari_Kintaka "Kneesaa a Jari Kintaka"), approached them and told them they needed help resetting the traps used in the Battle of Endor. After agreeing to help, they encountered a giant [Gorax](/wiki/Gorax "Gorax") and fled from it.[[176]](#cite_note-Traps_and_Tribulations-176)

It cornered them at the edge of the forest, overlooking a swamp. There was a log trap—an improvised battering ram held by ropes—nearby, however, and Wicket and Kneesaa had already reached it. As Skywalker distracted the Gorax, Leia helped the Ewoks. While Skywalker used his Force powers to distract the giant, Leia struggled to cut through the ropes holding up the battering ram. Skywalker lent Leia his lightsaber to cut the ropes, and the Gorax was pushed into the swamp by the log trap.[[176]](#cite_note-Traps_and_Tribulations-176)

Two days after the Battle of Endor, Solo suddenly proposed to Organa shortly after [discovering](/wiki/Assault_on_an_Imperial_outpost "Assault on an Imperial outpost") an [Imperial outpost](/wiki/Imperial_outpost_(Endor) "Imperial outpost (Endor)").[[51]](#cite_note-Princess_and_Scoundrel-51) Leia and Han had a [small wedding ceremony](/wiki/Wedding_of_Han_Solo_and_Leia_Organa "Wedding of Han Solo and Leia Organa")[[177]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-177) in the Ewok village Temple, where Leia wore a [meadow green dress](/wiki/Leia_Organa%27s_wedding_dress "Leia Organa's wedding dress"),[[51]](#cite_note-Princess_and_Scoundrel-51) that was only attended by those they trusted.[[177]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-177) This included Mothma, Calrissian, Chewbacca and Logray. The wedding was officiated by Skywalker and much of it was translated by C-3PO. During the ceremony Skywalker asked for a moment of silence for those who were not there to join them. Leia thought of her parents and felt as though her mother was attaching the Rhindon Sword to her waist and her father was pressing a kiss to her forehead.[[51]](#cite_note-Princess_and_Scoundrel-51)

Though they did not keep the ceremony a secret, Han and Leia did not make it publicly known.[[177]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-177) After their wedding, the couple left Endor to have their honeymoon aboard the *[Halcyon](/wiki/Halcyon "Halcyon")* at the urging of Mon Mothma, only for their time aboard the luxury [Star Cruiser](/wiki/Star_Cruiser "Star Cruiser") to involve a battle with Imperial forces. Organa began to unlock her Force powers during the battle.[[51]](#cite_note-Princess_and_Scoundrel-51)

#### Naboo[]

:   "*People like you are the reason can prevail. Hope is the reason we are going to win. Welcome to the New Republic.*"
:   ―Leia Organa to Iden Versio and Del Meeko after the battle of Theed[[178]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-178)

Twenty days after the Battle of Endor, following the [Beltire Liberation](/wiki/Beltire_Liberation "Beltire Liberation") and the [Battle of Cawa City](/wiki/Battle_of_Cawa_City "Battle of Cawa City"), in the company of Lieutenant [Shara Bey](/wiki/Shara_Bey "Shara Bey"), Organa was tasked by Mothma to conduct a diplomatic mission to Naboo—to recruit the assistance of the old Republic member in restoring the Senate and founding the [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic"). Her first return to Naboo in years, they were greeted by Governor [Donta Gesset](/wiki/Donta_Gesset "Donta Gesset") on behalf of [Queen](/wiki/Monarch_of_Naboo "Monarch of Naboo") [Sosha Soruna](/wiki/Sosha_Soruna "Sosha Soruna"). Led into the [Theed Royal Palace](/wiki/Theed_Royal_Palace "Theed Royal Palace"), the Queen eagerly accepted Organa's invitation. It was then that a planet-wide blackout, with all orbital [sensors](/wiki/Sensor "Sensor") jammed, was caused by Imperial [climate disruption arrays](/wiki/Climate_disruption_array "Climate disruption array"), as part of [Operation: Cinder](/wiki/Operation:_Cinder "Operation: Cinder"), spearheaded by [Lerr Duvat](/wiki/Lerr_Duvat "Lerr Duvat").[[179]](#cite_note-SE2-179)

 [![Organa saving Shara Bey above Naboo](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3a/BattleOverNaboo-ShatteredEmpire3.png/revision/latest?cb=20151101104930) [![Organa saving Shara Bey above Naboo](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3a/BattleOverNaboo-ShatteredEmpire3.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20151101104930)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3a/BattleOverNaboo-ShatteredEmpire3.png/revision/latest?cb=20151101104930) 

Organa saving Shara Bey above Naboo

 

Alerted by Captain [Korro](/wiki/Korro "Korro"), Bey and Organa correctly surmised that it was the work of the Imperial remnant and asked for pilots and ships. The demilitarization of Naboo years before, however, forced them to use [N-1 starfighters](/wiki/N-1_starfighter "N-1 starfighter") left in the palace that dated back to the [Invasion of Naboo](/wiki/Invasion_of_Naboo "Invasion of Naboo") thirty-six years before, and to manually pilot the ships without the assistance of astromech droids. Momentarily sensing a [dark presence](/wiki/Maul "Maul"), this being Darth Maul, Organa volunteered for the mission, while the [Security Forces](/wiki/Royal_Naboo_Security_Forces "Royal Naboo Security Forces") evacuated the city. Alongside Soruna and Bey, she set out to destroy the Imperial [satellites](/wiki/Satellite "Satellite"), with Bey acting as a distraction for the incoming TIE/ln fighters.[[180]](#cite_note-SE3-180)

During the [battle](/wiki/Battle_of_Theed "Battle of Theed"), she saved Bey. They were, in turn, saved from a new wave of TIE fighters by Calrissian and Nunb on the *[Mellcrawler II](/wiki/Mellcrawler_II "Mellcrawler II")* and by other ships of the Rebel Fleet, which had been alerted of Operation: Cinder after an [assault](/wiki/Raid_at_the_Wretch_of_Tayron "Raid at the Wretch of Tayron") on a ISB black site. Just as Soruna destroyed the last of the satellites, the fleet destroyed Duvat's [*Imperial II*-class Star Destroyer](/wiki/Imperial_II-class_Star_Destroyer "Imperial II-class Star Destroyer") *[Torment](/wiki/Torment "Torment")*, saving Naboo and letting Organa and Bey reunite with Solo and [Kes Dameron](/wiki/Kes_Dameron "Kes Dameron"), respectively.[[180]](#cite_note-SE3-180)

However, the surviving Imperials were still intent on carrying out Operation: Cinder and the rebels were forced to protect the city of Theed from them. Leia devised a plan to vanquish the Imperials by triggering an [ion pulse](/wiki/Ion_pulse "Ion pulse") from a security system installed years prior, which would deactivate all weapons and vehicles outside the Theed Royal Palace. However, the power relays necessary to activate it had been damaged and needed repairing. Joined by Danger Leader [Shriv Suurgav](/wiki/Shriv_Suurgav "Shriv Suurgav") and recent Imperial defectors [Iden Versio](/wiki/Iden_Versio "Iden Versio") and [Del Meeko](/wiki/Del_Meeko "Del Meeko"), Leia took Del and together the two teams managed to restore power. Leia then took up a position on the front lines and ordered all rebel forces to fall back to the palace as the pulse was detonated, rendering all Imperial tech useless and saving the day. After the battle, Leia revealed that she knew both Iden and Del were members of Inferno Squad, a unit which had caused more than a bit of trouble for the rebellion in the past. However, she surmised that fighting the Empire meant something to both and formally welcomed them into the New Republic after they expressed a desire to fight for the right side.[[178]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-178)

### Jedi training[]

#### Training on Ajan Kloss[]

:   "*I treasured each moment I spent with my brother. The things he taught me [....] I use them every day. Once you touch the Force, it's part of you always. Over the years, I continued to learn, to grow. There were times on the Senate floor when the meditations I'd practiced with Luke were the only thing that kept me from causing a galactic incident.*"
:   ―Leia, to Rey[[181]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-181)

 [![After the Battle of Endor, Organa undertook Jedi training from her brother.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4c/LukeTrainingLeia-RotJAVA.png/revision/latest?cb=20250327040015) [![After the Battle of Endor, Organa undertook Jedi training from her brother.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4c/LukeTrainingLeia-RotJAVA.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250327040015)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4c/LukeTrainingLeia-RotJAVA.png/revision/latest?cb=20250327040015) 

After the Battle of Endor, Organa undertook Jedi training from her brother.

 

After the Battle of Endor, Organa began [training](/wiki/Jedi_training "Jedi training") in the ways of the Jedi under the tutelage of her brother. At Skywalker's suggestion the two of them trained on Ajan Kloss.[[7]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-7) She went on to construct her [own](/wiki/Leia%27s_lightsaber "Leia's lightsaber") lightsaber that produced a blue-colored blade, and she would train in lightsaber combat becoming skilled enough to fight on par with Skywalker and even best him in a sparring match on occasion.[[23]](#cite_note-TROS-23) She also practiced meditation with Skywalker,[[181]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-181) and learned enough about the basics of the Force to levitate herself and sense other sentient beings.[[182]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-182) Luke offered her guidance about how the Force worked and helped her understand, from his personal experience, that the Force offered visions of the future, past, and even of the departed. Leia believed this helped explain the visions of their mother she retained after her death. In her training, she demonstrated an ability to learn and adapt quickly, as noted by Skywalker that she was a fast study.[[7]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-7)

#### Discovering a holocron[]

 [![During her time as a Jedi apprentice, Leia learned about Qi'ra's war against the Sith.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b5/JediLeia-HiddenEmpire5.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250318003509) [![During her time as a Jedi apprentice, Leia learned about Qi'ra's war against the Sith.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b5/JediLeia-HiddenEmpire5.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250318003509)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b5/JediLeia-HiddenEmpire5.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250318003509) 

During her time as a Jedi apprentice, Leia learned about Qi'ra's war against the Sith.

 

Sometime during her training with her brother, Organa and Skywalker discovered[[183]](#cite_note-Hidden_Empire_5-183) a [holocron](/wiki/The_Archivist%27s_Holocron "The Archivist's Holocron") that contained the story of [Qi'ra](/wiki/Qi%27ra "Qi'ra") and her [attempts](/wiki/War_against_the_Sith "War against the Sith") to destroy the Sith. Organa was confused by the sight of it because it didn't look like other holocrons they'd seen, but Skywalker assured her it was one and activated it for her, promising it would answer her questions. It contained recollections by "[The Archivist](/wiki/The_Archivist "The Archivist")".[[184]](#cite_note-Crimson_Reign_1-184) As the Archivist described Qi'ra's goals to kill Vader and Palpatine, Skywalker lamented that she never came to them for help. Organa suggested that this was because Qi'ra only relied on herself, saying she hadn't seemed like the trusting type.[[185]](#cite_note-Hidden_Empire_1-185) The Archivist suggested that the Rebel Alliance had perhaps been engineered by Palpatine, which Skywalker said was wrong, but Organa pointed out that while he didn't create it, he definitely used it.[[186]](#cite_note-Hidden_Empire_2-186) When the Archivist described the presence of Darth Vader as feeling like you were in the presence of an animal eating its own young, both Organa and Skywalker latched onto that idea and contemplated it more.[[187]](#cite_note-Hidden_Empire_3-187)

At the end of the story, the Archivist said that Qi'ra had failed to take down the Sith and saw her hidden empire of Crimson Dawn destroyed, even theorizing that Qi'ra had been killed by the Empire or its [remnants](/wiki/Imperial_Remnants "Imperial Remnants") as she had never seen her again. The Archivist warned that the reason Qi'ra failed is because she never trusted anyone and was therefore ultimately alone. Organa was shocked by the contents of the story. She and Skywalker both agreed that the Archivist was wrong in saying Qi'ra failed, Organa pointing out that Qi'ra's Syndicate War kept Palpatine occupied long enough for the Alliance to regroup. Organa expressed her wishes that Qi'ra had come to come to the Alliance, and wished that Qi'ra had been alive to see them win against the Empire, unaware that Qi'ra was actually still alive.[[183]](#cite_note-Hidden_Empire_5-183)

#### End of her path[]

 [![Leia constructed a blue-bladed lightsaber.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/54/Leia_Jedi_training-TROSAdaptation1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250226194647) [![Leia constructed a blue-bladed lightsaber.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/54/Leia_Jedi_training-TROSAdaptation1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250226194647)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/54/Leia_Jedi_training-TROSAdaptation1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250226194647) 

Leia constructed a blue-bladed lightsaber.

 

Organa, however, had visions of serving the galaxy in different ways and had another life calling to her rather than the life of a Jedi. But the catalyst of her choice to end her training was on the last night she was with Skywalker. While to dress together, Organa had a vision and sensed the death of her [unborn son](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo") if she were to complete her Jedi path. While Skywalker hoped that his sister would resume her training later, Organa gave him her lightsaber to convince him otherwise, asking to pass it on to a promising student someday. However, Skywalker hadn't yet done this, and Organa didn't know where he had stored her lightsaber.[[181]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-181)

While she ended her training, Organa treasured every moment she spent with Skywalker. She also went on to use what Skywalker taught her in her everyday life as well as into her career in the Galactic Senate of the New Republic and continued to learn over her years.[[181]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-181)

### New Republic[]

#### Return to Politics[]

:   "*Be patient. Be strong. Fight back where you can. The Imperial war machine falls apart one gear, one gun, one stormtrooper at a time. The New Republic is coming. And we want your help to finish the fight.*"
:   ―Leia Organa's holovid[[20]](#cite_note-Aftermath-20)

After ending her Jedi training, Organa returned to the political arena.[[5]](#cite_note-DB-Leia-5) At some point, shortly before an [Imperial emergency summit](/wiki/Akiva_Summit "Akiva Summit") on [Akiva](/wiki/Akiva "Akiva"), Organa recorded a [propaganda](/wiki/Propaganda "Propaganda") holovid to announce the destruction of the second Death Star, the death of Emperor Palpatine, and the birth of the New Republic to the whole galaxy, encouraging people to contribute to the defeat of the Empire.[[20]](#cite_note-Aftermath-20)

Following the [rebellion on Akiva](/wiki/Rebellion_on_Akiva "Rebellion on Akiva"), Leia served as the senator[[177]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-177) for the [Alderaan sector](/wiki/Alderaan_sector "Alderaan sector")[[188]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-188) in the reconstituted [Galactic Senate](/wiki/New_Republic_Senate "New Republic Senate") in [Chandrila](/wiki/Chandrila "Chandrila")'s [Hanna City](/wiki/Hanna_City "Hanna City"). As Senator, she arranged for the wrecked pieces of the second Death Star to be diverted to the [Alderaan Flotilla](/wiki/Alderaan_Flotilla "Alderaan Flotilla"), which used them to build a space station that became their new home.[[177]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-177) While a senator, [Captain](/wiki/Captain "Captain") [Lina Graf](/wiki/Lina_Graf "Lina Graf") approached Organa and Chancellor Mothma for a ship to take her to [Mustafar](/wiki/Mustafar "Mustafar") to find her brother [Milo Graf](/wiki/Milo_Graf "Milo Graf"), explaining that she believed he was there because of a dream she had. Mothma refused to send a ship based on a dream, but Organa, recognizing that she would still go, gave her the name of a a bar on [Emita](/wiki/Emita "Emita") where she could find the pilot and smuggler [Jaxxon T. Tumperakki](/wiki/Jaxxon_T._Tumperakki "Jaxxon T. Tumperakki"), explaining that he was crazy enough to take her. Graf then went there to ask Tumperakki for help, giving him Organa's name, though he initially said that his days of dealing with Organa and her friends were over.[[189]](#cite_note-GoVC_2-189)

#### Balancing family and service[]

Knowing that her husband and his co-pilot Chewbacca had undertaken a campaign to [liberate](/wiki/Liberation_of_Kashyyyk "Liberation of Kashyyyk") Kashyyyk, Leia tried unsuccessfully to marshal support in the Galactic Senate for troops and ships to free the planet. However, the New Republic was too preoccupied with fighting the Empire and holding on to liberated worlds.[[177]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-177)

While her husband Solo had received information from the smuggler [Imra](/wiki/Imra "Imra") that the Empire had reduced their military presence on Kashyyyk, Leia warned that Imra could not be trusted. Leia's warning proved correct when Han and Chewbacca stumbled onto a trap on Kashyyyk. While Han managed to escape, Chewbacca was captured and locked inside the automated prison of [Ashmead's Lock](/wiki/Ashmead%27s_Lock "Ashmead's Lock"). Han later contacted Leia while traveling on the edge of [Wild Space](/wiki/Wild_Space "Wild Space"). Their conversation was interrupted when Han came under attack from Imperial forces.[[177]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-177)

Despite the family crisis with Han, Leia accompanied Chancellor Mon Mothma on a secret meeting with the Imperial [Grand Vizier](/wiki/Grand_Vizier "Grand Vizier") [Mas Amedda](/wiki/Mas_Amedda "Mas Amedda") on the ocean planet of [Velusia](/wiki/Velusia "Velusia"). When a dejected Amedda offered to surrender, Chancellor Mothma and Princess Leia rejected his offer and ordered him to find a way to secure the Galactic Empire's surrender. After returning to Chandrila, Leia requested an audience with the New Republic starfighter pilot [Norra Wexley](/wiki/Norra_Wexley "Norra Wexley"). When the [New Republic Defense Force](/wiki/New_Republic_Defense_Force "New Republic Defense Force") refused to help her find Solo, Norra resigned from the [Navy](/wiki/New_Republic_Defense_Fleet "New Republic Defense Fleet") and embarked on a mission to find Han with her son [Temmin Wexley](/wiki/Temmin_Wexley "Temmin Wexley"), his [B1-series battle droid](/wiki/B1-series_battle_droid "B1-series battle droid") [Mister Bones](/wiki/Mister_Bones "Mister Bones"), the former Imperial [loyalty officer](/wiki/Loyalty_officer "Loyalty officer") [Sinjir Rath Velus](/wiki/Sinjir_Rath_Velus "Sinjir Rath Velus"), [Zabrak](/wiki/Zabrak "Zabrak") bounty hunter [Jas Emari](/wiki/Jas_Emari "Jas Emari"), and the New Republic soldier [Jom Barell](/wiki/Jom_Barell "Jom Barell").[[177]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-177)

Princess Leia later attended a high-level New Republic meeting with Admiral Ackbar, Mon Mothma, and the advisers [Hostis Ij](/wiki/Hostis_Ij "Hostis Ij") and [Auxi Kray Korbin](/wiki/Auxi_Kray_Korbin "Auxi Kray Korbin") to discuss the war effort. Though Leia was frustrated with the endless bickering within the New Republic leadership, she regarded it as a lesser evil to the dictatorial rule of the late Darth Sidious. While meditating with a potted plant from Endor, Leia receives a revelation that [her unborn child](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo") would be a boy, a fighter, and an angel.[[177]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-177)

Following the successful New Republic capture of the planet [Kuat](/wiki/Kuat "Kuat") and the vital [Kuat Drive Yards](/wiki/Kuat_Drive_Yards "Kuat Drive Yards"), Princess Leia contacted Admiral Ackbar by hologram to congratulate his victory. They were then joined by Chancellor Mothma, who informed them that she had been contacted by [Grand Admiral](/wiki/Grand_Admiral "Grand Admiral") [Rae Sloane](/wiki/Rae_Sloane "Rae Sloane"), the leader of the Galactic Empire. With the Empire facing defeat, Grand Admiral Sloane agreed to participate in [bilateral peace talks](/wiki/Imperial%E2%80%93Republic_peace_talks "Imperial–Republic peace talks") on Chandrila. While Leia was skeptical that Sloane was the mysterious [Operator](/wiki/Gallius_Rax "Gallius Rax"), she reluctantly joined her comrades in accepting Sloane's offer.[[177]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-177)

#### Searching for Han Solo[]

:   "*Senator Organa. It's been a while.*"  
    "*Building a republic is busy work.*"  
    "*So is chasing after an Imperial Fleet.*"  
    "*It's about to get busier, Commander. I need a favor. One of our Generals has gone missing. I tracked him to Takodana, but he isn't answering his comm. I need you to find Han Solo.*"
:   ―Leia Organa, to Iden Versio[[178]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-178)

Sometime later, Senator Organa lost contact with her husband, Han Solo. She tracked him to [Takodana](/wiki/Takodana "Takodana") but was worried when he didn't answer his comm. She sent Commander Versio and the newly reformed [Inferno Squad](/wiki/Inferno_Squad_(Resistance) "Inferno Squad (Resistance)") with [finding and locating](/wiki/Skirmish_on_Takodana "Skirmish on Takodana") Solo.[[178]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-178)

#### Liberation of Kashyyyk[]

Later, Leia and Chancellor Mon Mothma received the liberated rebel prisoners from Ashmead's Lock, who had been freed by Norra and her team. While at Hanna City Spaceport, Leia asked Norra about her husband. Norra reassured the Princess that Solo and Chewbacca were safe but that they had stayed behind on Kashyyyk to free the Wookiees. Unknown to Leia and Mothma, the prisoners were part of [Fleet Admiral](/wiki/Fleet_Admiral "Fleet Admiral") Gallius Rax's plot to assassinate the New Republic military and political leadership on Chandrila. Rax, who was the Operator, had secretly fitted the prisoners with inorganic bio-chips that would allow him to remotely control their actions.[[177]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-177)

A month later, the Galactic Senate accepted Rae Sloane's offer for bilateral peace talks between the Republic and the Empire. Chancellor Mothma timed the peace talks to take place after [Liberation Day](/wiki/Liberation_Day_(New_Republic) "Liberation Day (New Republic)"), a public holiday held to celebrate the rescue of the Ashmead's Lock prisoners. Sympathetic to the plight of the enslaved Wookiees, Leia tried to lobby the Chancellor into sending military forces to liberate Kashyyyk. However, Mon Mothma refused to launch an official incursion to avoid jeopardizing the upcoming peace talks. When Mothma offered to negotiate the liberation of Kashyyyk with Sloane, Leia insisted that the freedom and dignity of the Wookiees was non-negotiable.[[177]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-177)

Prior to the Liberation Day celebrations, Leia received news from the New Republic [slicer](/wiki/Slicer "Slicer") [Conder Kyl](/wiki/Conder_Kyl "Conder Kyl") that a New Republic probe droid in the [Kashyyyk system](/wiki/Kashyyyk_system "Kashyyyk system") had intercepted of the Imperial Grand Moff of Kashyyyk [Lozen Tolruck](/wiki/Lozen_Tolruck "Lozen Tolruck") ordering the Star Destroyers orbiting Kashyyyk to bombard the planet after the Wookiees had revolted en masse. Wanting to rescue her husband and Chewie, Leia convinced Evaan Verlaine to fly as her co-pilot aboard the *Millennium Falcon* to Kashyyyk. This timely decision saved her from being assassinated by Rax's unwilling agents.[[177]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-177)

Leia later contacted Captain Wedge Antilles via hologram to request the help of [his squadron](/wiki/Phantom_Squadron "Phantom Squadron") on Kashyyyk. Upon arriving in Kashyyyk, Leia's ship the *Millennium Falcon* and Phantom Squadron flew rings around the Imperial Star Destroyers *[Dominion](/wiki/Dominion "Dominion")*, *[Vitiator](/wiki/Vitiator "Vitiator")*, and *[Neutralizer](/wiki/Neutralizer "Neutralizer")*. Their starships were soon reinforced by Admiral Ackbar's flagship *[Home One](/wiki/Home_One "Home One")*. Solo and his team managed to hijack the *Dominion* and use it to destroy the *Vitiator*. As a result, the *Neutralizer* surrendered to the New Republic, ending Imperial rule on Kashyyyk.[[177]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-177)

Leia had an emotional reunion with her husband aboard the *Dominion*'s hangar bay. After exchanging jokes about rescuing each other, the couple reaffirmed their love for each other. When Solo asked about naming their baby, Leia insisted that their child was not a bandit and called him an angel. The couple then kissed. Later on Kashyyyk, Leia and Han bid farewell to their friend Chewbacca, who stayed behind on his homeworld to reunite with [his family](/wiki/Chewbacca%27s_family "Chewbacca's family"). After learning of the recent [attack on Chandrila](/wiki/Attack_on_Chandrila "Attack on Chandrila"), the couple returned to the capital with Wedge in tow.[[177]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-177)

Later, Princess Leia gave Norra and [her team](/wiki/Norra_Wexley%27s_team "Norra Wexley's team") her personal and financial backing during their hunt for Grand Admiral Sloane, who they believed was responsible for the attack on Chandrila. Due to her actions at Kashyyyk, Leia had become a political pariah with the New Republic establishment. While the New Republic was no longer offering bounties for Imperial fugitives, she still vowed to do everything that was necessary to help her newfound friends.[[177]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-177)

### Tidings from Jakku[]

Several months later, Leia was heavily pregnant. She was tended to by the protocol droid [T-2LC](/wiki/T-2LC "T-2LC"), known as "Elsie," who served as her nanny and called her "mum." At the advice of Doctor [Harter Kalonia](/wiki/Harter_Kalonia "Harter Kalonia"), Han bought his wife [jogan fruits](/wiki/Jogan_fruit "Jogan fruit"). While talking with her husband about political developments in the wider galaxy, the two received news via hologram from Norra Wexley that the Imperial fugitive Grand Admiral Sloane had fled to the barren [Inner Rim](/wiki/Inner_Rim_Territories "Inner Rim Territories") world of [Jakku](/wiki/Jakku "Jakku"). Leia encouraged Norra to continue her investigation but to be careful.[[188]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-188)

Norra and her team traveled to Jakku, where they discovered that most of the Galactic Empire had relocated there. While Norra, Jas Emari, and Mister Bones infiltrated Jakku, Sinjir and Temmin returned to Chandrila with news about the Imperial presence. After receiving Sinjir and Temmin, Leia contacted Chancellor Mothma and told her to come to her domicile. After Mothma had questioned Temmin and Sinjir, Leia defended their mission. Chancellor Mothma responded that the New Republic was responsible for hunting Sloane, not Princess Leia and her friends. However, Mothma praised Leia for her efforts to liberate Jakku.[[188]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-188)

Leia opined that the New Republic had the chance to end the war now that the Empire was gathered on Jakku. Chancellor Mothma agreed to raise the matter with the Galactic Senate but decided to send a fact-finding mission first. Unknown to Leia, Mothma's political rival, Senator Tolwar Wartol, had installed a listening device inside T-2LC. Seeking to discredit Chancellor Mothma, Wartol leaked information about the Imperial presence on Jakku to the media. Later, Leia and Han allowed Temmin and Sinjir to borrow the *Millennium Falcon* and travel to Jakku. However, Wartol sent guards to stop them from leaving to sow discord among Mothma's allies.[[188]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-188)

### War's end[]

While watching the morning news with her husband, Leia and Han saw Senator Wartol informing the media about the Imperial presence on Jakku. After meeting with Sinjir and reassuring him that they had not double-crossed him and Temmin, Leia shared Sinjir's assessment that there was a listening device inside her domicile. Sinjir enlisted the services of his lover Conder, who was a slicer who had previously helped Leia. Conder found a listening device inside T-2LC, and Solo removed it. Leia and Solo promptly informed Chancellor Mothma, who went to confront Senator Wartol.[[188]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-188)

Leia and her unborn child stayed behind on Chandrila while Han, Sinjir, Temmin, Conder, and Jom Barell undertook an [undercover mission](/wiki/Mission_to_Nakadia "Mission to Nakadia") on [Nakadia](/wiki/Nakadia "Nakadia"), the new capital of the New Republic. The five investigated five senators who had opposed Chancellor Mothma's resolution to send New Republic forces to Jakku. They subsequently uncovered a conspiracy by the [Black Sun](/wiki/Black_Sun "Black Sun") and [Red Key](/wiki/Red_Key_Raiders "Red Key Raiders") crime syndicates to prolong the Galactic Civil War by bribing and coercing the senators. Han and his team foiled the conspiracy by rescuing Senator [Nim Tar](/wiki/Nim_Tar "Nim Tar")'s [child](/wiki/Nim_Tar%27s_child "Nim Tar's child"). Sinjir then posed as an adviser to the Chancellor and offered them pardons and political favors if they changed their votes. This ploy worked and the New Republic dispatched military forces to Jakku, beginning the [final battle](/wiki/Battle_of_Jakku "Battle of Jakku") of the Galactic Civil War.[[188]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-188)

While awaiting her husband's return, Leia found that she could sense her unborn son through the Force. She likened his presence to a pulsing living band of light. Sometimes that light dimmed, and other times it was thrust through a vein of darkness. Leia also found that her son could sense her emotions. After Solo returned from Nakadia, the couple talked about the Battle of Jakku. When Solo remarked that it felt weird staying back, Leia reassured him that they had their own adventure and were seeing the start of a new era. Leia then felt her baby turn inside her again, troubled by something she could not feel and understand.[[188]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-188)

In the final days of her pregnancy, Leia asked both Lando Calrissian and Chancellor Mothma to get gifts for the baby, even guilting Mothma, who had considered delegating the task to her secretary [Auxi](/wiki/Auxi_Kray_Korbin "Auxi Kray Korbin"), for not picking up the gift herself. However, Mothma eventually choosing to comply with Leia's demands would lead to the saving of her life, as Senator Wortal had planted a bomb to go off in Mothma's office. Leia ran to the Senate tower, terrified that her mentor was dead. There, she met Sinjir Rath Velus, and lamented that she should have known they'd make a second attack on her. Upon seeing Mothma alive and well, Leia ran to her old friend, only stopping to help Sinjir, physically removing a sparking baton from a guard's hand to help him through the crowd. Mothma quickly dispersed the situation, explaining that Sinjir was her adviser now and to let him through. The two women embraced each other, thankful that Mon was still alive.[[188]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-188)

With the Battle of Jakku turning in the New Republic's favor, Chancellor Mothma received a peace overture from Grand Vizier Mas Amedda. Leia along with Chancellor Mothma and her new advisers attended the surrender ceremony which took place at the [crystal](/wiki/Crystal "Crystal") [cave](/wiki/Cave "Cave") north of Hanna City, under an ancient [tintolive tree](/wiki/Tintolive_tree "Tintolive tree"). Leia watched as the Chancellor and Grand Vizier signed the [Imperial Instruments of Surrender](/wiki/Imperial_Instruments_of_Surrender "Imperial Instruments of Surrender") and the [Galactic Concordance](/wiki/Galactic_Concordance "Galactic Concordance"), which formally ended the Galactic Civil War and facilitated the Empire's surrender. During the signing, Leia entered the third hour of her labor. However, she only told Han after the ceremony. They then rushed off to the birthing chamber at the heart of Hanna City.[[188]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-188)

### Motherhood[]

:   "*I just never should have sent him away. That's when I lost him. That's when I lost you both.*"
:   ―Leia Organa to Han Solo, on their son, Ben[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-10)

 [![Han Solo and Leia Organa had a son, Ben Solo, who inherited his mother's strength with the Force.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8e/Han_Leia_and_Ben.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161210085037) [![Han Solo and Leia Organa had a son, Ben Solo, who inherited his mother's strength with the Force.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8e/Han_Leia_and_Ben.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161210085037)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8e/Han_Leia_and_Ben.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161210085037) 

Han Solo and Leia Organa had a son, Ben Solo, who inherited his mother's strength with the Force.

 

Leia gave birth to her son Ben Solo on the day the Empire surrendered to the New Republic. The two were visited by several friends and families. There were rumors that her brother Luke visited before departing on an untold mission. Others claimed that his absence was conspicuous. Stories of Ben's birth circulated within the public sphere. One story claimed that the Princess underwent three entire days of labor. Another tale claimed that it was a fast and painless birth, with Leia merely needing to calm herself and meditate to make the moment as untroubled as a mountain lake. Other stories claimed that her son was born with a full shock of black hair and a full set of teeth.[[188]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-188)

Soon after Ben's birth, Han Solo stood in the nursery looking at his son when Ben began to cry. Leia entered the room when Han called for her, asking her to use the Force to quell his sobs. Leia told her husband instead to pick him up, and upon doing so, Ben burped and stopped crying, snuggling into his father. When Han lamented that he'd never have what Leia had with him due to her connection to the Force, Leia simply told her husband that what he had was different because he was his father and that he didn't need the Force at all.[[188]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-188)

After Ben's birth, Han and Leia decided to remain on Chandrila, although Sinjir Rath Velus noted that Leia was eager to go out and help liberate worlds still in the thrall of Imperial Remnants.[[188]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-188)

Leia found Ben to be a normal baby who went through the normal range of emotions.[[188]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-188) Leia developed many memories with her son, being present for his first steps and word. As well as when he harnessed the force through a toddler rage throwing a toy across a room.[[181]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-181)

In [7 ABY](/wiki/7_ABY "7 ABY"),[[190]](#cite_note-Last_Shot_date-190) Han and Leia were paid a visit by their longtime friend Lando Calrissian, who recruited Han to help him save Cloud City. Leia gave Han her blessings as he joined Calrissian's crew. Later, Leia helped them by ordering New Republic Captain [Krull](/wiki/Krull "Krull") to allow the group of "New Republic agents" to pass through their blockade and leave [Substation Grimdock](/wiki/Substation_Grimdock "Substation Grimdock"), and later revealed to them that the pilot they hired, [Taka Jamoreesa](/wiki/Taka_Jamoreesa "Taka Jamoreesa"), was an undercover New Republic bodyguard. Upon Han's return, Leia was pleased by her husband's vow to spend more time together.[[21]](#cite_note-Last_Shot-21)

As Ben grew, he shared his mother's [Force sensitivity](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive"). However, he struggled with the dark side. Organa sent her son to train under her brother in [15 ABY](/wiki/15_ABY "15 ABY"),[[191]](#cite_note-Ben_Solo_training_date_note-191) as Skywalker had begun to rebuild the Jedi Order, in the hope that he would learn to control his obsession.[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-10)

### New Republic senator[]

#### Assisting Syndulla[]

:   "*The honorable Senator Organa has become aware of an unfortunate situation and wishes to present this data transcript, which she hopes may resolve the matter.*"
:   ―C-3PO to the court[[22]](#cite_note-Part_Seven-22)

 [![Senator Organa-Solo supported the actions of General Syndulla and Captain Teva](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/10/CarsonAndHera-Ahsoka-PartFive.png/revision/latest?cb=20230914103606) [![Senator Organa-Solo supported the actions of General Syndulla and Captain Teva](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/10/CarsonAndHera-Ahsoka-PartFive.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20230914103606)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/10/CarsonAndHera-Ahsoka-PartFive.png/revision/latest?cb=20230914103606) 

Senator Organa-Solo supported the actions of General Syndulla and Captain Teva

 

In [9 ABY](/wiki/9_ABY "9 ABY"), [Grand Admiral](/wiki/Grand_Admiral "Grand Admiral") [Thrawn](/wiki/Mitth%27raw%27nuruodo "Mitth'raw'nuruodo") of the Galactic Empire planned to return to the galaxy, having previously been taken to [Peridea](/wiki/Peridea "Peridea") due to the [actions](/wiki/Liberation_of_Lothal "Liberation of Lothal") of Organa's old ally, Commander Ezra Bridger.[[192]](#cite_note-Part_One-192) Around this time, Leia's name was included on a list of heroes on the gauntlet of [Baylan Skoll](/wiki/Baylan_Skoll "Baylan Skoll"), a former Jedi Knight and an ally to the effort to find Grand Admiral.[[193]](#cite_note-Part_Three-193)

After being informed of rumors regarding Thrawn's return, General Hera Syndulla spoke with Mon Mothma and other senators, requesting resources to aid in searching for the missing Jedi and the Grand Admiral, though the request was soon declined.[[193]](#cite_note-Part_Three-193) In response, Syndulla took a small squadron of X-wings and decided to continue with the search regardless. Organa was soon informed of this, though supported Syndulla's actions and decided to cover for her. The New Republic were quick to respond to this however, and Organa soon contacted Captain [Carson Teva](/wiki/Carson_Teva "Carson Teva") and told him that she could only cover for them for so long. Teva passed the message down to Syndulla, who searched for her friends Sabine Wren and Ahsoka Tano. Tano was eventually found and pursued the hunt for Thrawn and Bridger, whilst Syndulla was left to deal with the consequences from the New Republic.[[194]](#cite_note-Part_Five-194)

During the prosecution of Syndulla by Senator Hamato Xiono for disobeying direct orders, Organa sent C-3PO to represent her in the trial and defend her friend. Before claiming that Organa had only recently become aware of the situation, the protocol droid presented a data transcript on the senator's behalf to prove that Organa had personally authorized Syndulla's reconnaissance mission to Seatos while she was unaware of Xiono's vote against it. C-3PO also added that Organa was willing to overlook the alleged mistake, with the request that further concerns be addressed directly to her. As Xiono reluctantly claimed to be satisfied, Mothma dismissed the case despite knowing that Organa did not authorize the mission beforehand as claimed.[[22]](#cite_note-Part_Seven-22)

#### Late New Republic Era[]

##### An unlikely ally[]

:   "*I don't have time for a conversation about galactic politics with someone so profoundly ignorant of their greater implications.*"  
    "*Nor do I have time to discuss these matters with someone so intolerant of other points of view.*"
:   ―Leia and Casterfo exchanging views about the Galactic Empire[[13]](#cite_note-Bloodline-13)

 [![Organa resumed her political career by becoming a senator in the New Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3f/SenatorLeiaOrgana-TheRiseOfKyloRen1.png/revision/latest?cb=20200110050504) [![Organa resumed her political career by becoming a senator in the New Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3f/SenatorLeiaOrgana-TheRiseOfKyloRen1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200110050504)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3f/SenatorLeiaOrgana-TheRiseOfKyloRen1.png/revision/latest?cb=20200110050504) 

Organa resumed her political career by becoming a senator in the New Republic.

 

Twenty-three years after the Battle of Jakku, Organa was still a senator in the Galactic Senate of the New Republic on [Hosnian Prime](/wiki/Hosnian_Prime "Hosnian Prime"), as part of the [Populists](/wiki/Populists "Populists"), a powerful, yet unofficial, political faction. The Populists believed that individual member planets should retain their full sovereignty, while the [Centrists](/wiki/Centrists "Centrists") favored a stronger galactic government and a larger military. After Mothma, former [chancellor](/wiki/Chancellor_(New_Republic) "Chancellor (New Republic)"), left the office, the tension between the two factions threatened to cripple the Senate.[[13]](#cite_note-Bloodline-13)

During this period, Organa attended a [dedication ceremony](/wiki/Bail_Organa_statue-dedication_ceremony "Bail Organa statue-dedication ceremony") of a new statue of her father, Bail Organa, on Hosnian Prime. At this ceremony, Organa addressed the Senate and attempted to inspire the senators to stop bickering and begin to act. However, her efforts proved unsuccessful, further demonstrating that the Senate was no longer effective. Losing faith that the government could function any longer, Organa resolved to resign as senator at the end of her term.[[13]](#cite_note-Bloodline-13)

Following the ceremony, Organa met privately with the Centrist senator Lady [Carise Sindian](/wiki/Carise_Sindian "Carise Sindian"), who informed her that Lord [Mellowyn](/wiki/Mellowyn "Mellowyn"), the [Supreme governor](/wiki/Supreme_governor "Supreme governor") of [Birren](/wiki/Birren "Birren") had died without leaving any heirs. Since Mellowyn was a distant kinsman of her adoptive father Bail Organa, Leia was his next in line to inherit the position per the rules of the [Elder Houses](/wiki/Elder_Houses "Elder Houses"). While Organa was not interested in matters relating to royalty, Sindian wanted to preserve that tradition. Organa reassured Sindian that she would have her staff investigate the matter immediately.[[13]](#cite_note-Bloodline-13)

Later during a session of the Senate, Organa was present when [Yendor](/wiki/Yendor_Brethen "Yendor Brethen"), a Twi'lek emissary from the planet [Ryloth](/wiki/Ryloth "Ryloth"), appeared before the Senate to ask for help in investigating a [Nikto](/wiki/Nikto "Nikto") [cartel](/wiki/Rinnrivin_Di%27s_cartel "Rinnrivin Di's cartel") that was threatening his home planet. The cartel was run by a [Kajain'sa'Nikto](/wiki/Kajain%27sa%27Nikto "Kajain'sa'Nikto") known as [Rinnrivin Di](/wiki/Rinnrivin_Di "Rinnrivin Di"), who operated from the planet [Bastatha](/wiki/Bastatha "Bastatha"). After Yendor's request was made, the Senate debated whether Yendor's accusations were true and whether the Senate should act upon them. Feeling partially responsible that she was part of the government that allowed this to happen, Senator Organa volunteered to personally investigate Rinnrivin Di's cartel on Bastatha. She was pleased to think that she would see some action again before she retired, until Senator [Ransolm Casterfo](/wiki/Ransolm_Casterfo "Ransolm Casterfo"), the junior senator from the Centrist planet [Riosa](/wiki/Riosa "Riosa"), suggested that the investigation to be bipartisan and volunteered to accompany Organa.[[13]](#cite_note-Bloodline-13)

Soon after the session of the Senate ended, Organa went to visit Casterfo in his office—contrary to senatorial protocol, where he would be expected to visit her in the morning. Upon her visit, Casterfo welcomed Organa into his office, which she discovered to be full of Imperial memorabilia. Disgusted by his infatuation with the Empire, Organa and Casterfo entered a heated debate where Casterfo showed his support not for Palpatine, but the dream of the Empire, and that he wished that the Empire had been reformed under better leadership. Organa began to argue that Palpatine was not the only problem with the Empire, and that he had only been a child while she was fighting in the war. Organa then left Casterfo's office, the two of them agreeing that C-3PO and the rest of Organa's staff would plan for their [trip to Bastatha](/wiki/Mission_to_Bastatha "Mission to Bastatha") at another time.[[13]](#cite_note-Bloodline-13)

##### Mission to Bastatha[]

:   "*Rinnrivin Di, I presume?*"  
    "*Princess Leia Organa. I apologize for your unorthodox journey here. However, I thought you unlikely to accept a straightforward invitation*"
:   ―Leia's first meeting with Rinnrivin Di[[13]](#cite_note-Bloodline-13)

A few days later, Organa and Casterfo, along with Leia's chief of staff [Greer Sonnel](/wiki/Greer_Sonnel "Greer Sonnel"), 16-year-old office intern [Korr Sella](/wiki/Korr_Sella "Korr Sella"), X-wing pilot [Joph Seastriker](/wiki/Joph_Seastriker "Joph Seastriker"), and C-3PO, began to prepare their trip to Bastatha. The trip on board Organa's personal ship the *[Mirrorbright](/wiki/Mirrorbright "Mirrorbright")* was an awkward one, as Casterfo and Organa attempted to avoid each other after their confrontation in Casterfo's office earlier. However, by the time they reached the planet, Casterfo apologized for being insensitive to Organa's personal experiences in the war, and they agreed to leave the past in the past so that they could do what they came to do.[[13]](#cite_note-Bloodline-13)

Organa and Casterfo remained civil with each other as they exited the *Mirrorbright* to greet the local authorities, and they were welcomed to Bastatha by Nikto [Magistrates](/wiki/Magistrate "Magistrate") [Tosta](/wiki/Tosta "Tosta") and [Xun](/wiki/Xun "Xun"). The senators and their staff were all welcomed to dinner, and they were taken to a luxurious casino. The group was offered a splendid meal, but Organa insisted on playing her hand in a game of [Sabacc](/wiki/Sabacc "Sabacc"). The Niktos believed that she would likely lose some money in the challenging game, but Organa, having learned the game from the best, intended to impress her hosts with her cunning rather than her decorum.[[13]](#cite_note-Bloodline-13)

While Leia's actions won the favor of her Nikto hosts, Ransolm was uncomfortable with his colleague for fraternizing with what he regarded as "lowlives." During their time at the casino, Leia noticed a party of visitors from the planet [Daxam IV](/wiki/Daxam_IV "Daxam IV"). One of the party was an [elderly woman](/wiki/Arliz_Hadrassian "Arliz Hadrassian") who appeared to be watching her while trying to remain unnoticed. After exiting the casino, Organa and Casterfo argued about her style of fraternizing with constituents and the alleged "terrorist" activities of the Rebel Alliance. Later, Leia received news from Greer that a "business delegation" was coming to meet her.[[13]](#cite_note-Bloodline-13)

This "business delegation" turned out to be a party of kidnappers sent by Rinnrivin. Without firing shots, Rinnrivin's underlings spirited Organa away on a [hoversled](/wiki/Hoversled "Hoversled") for a private audience with Rinnrivin at [his underground headquarters](/wiki/Rinnrivin%27s_headquarters "Rinnrivin's headquarters"). The crime lord attempted to ingratiate himself with the New Republic senator by serving vintage [Toniray](/wiki/Toniray "Toniray") [wine](/wiki/Wine "Wine") from Alderaan and presenting a [holocube](/wiki/Holocube "Holocube") of her killing Jabba, an act which had won her the respect of the Nikto species, who called her "Huttslayer." However, Leia rebuffed Rinnrivin's attempts to bribe her into persuading the New Republic to ease its ban on the sale of illegal [spice](/wiki/Spice "Spice").[[13]](#cite_note-Bloodline-13)

Organa's meeting with Rinnrivin was interrupted by Casterfo, who had tracked her down using a [tracking device](/wiki/Homing_beacon "Homing beacon") he had planted in her cloak. Following a brief scuffle with Rinnrivin's guards, the two senators escaped on a hoversled and alerted the Bastatha authorities. Rinnrivin and his henchmen escaped before the [Bastatha security forces](/wiki/Bastatha_security_forces "Bastatha security forces") could secure his underground lair. However, Leia and her team managed to find information about Rinnrivin's operations including his funnelling of funds to shadow corporations in the Outer Rim. They suspected that Rinnrivin was part of a larger criminal network.[[13]](#cite_note-Bloodline-13)

##### First Senator and the Napkin Bombing[]

Following their return from Bastatha, Organa and Casterfo addressed the Galactic Senate and called for further investigations into Rinnrivin's cartel. Their speeches were greeted by partisan infighting with the Populists accusing Casterfo of endangering Leia's life and the Centrists accusing Leia of withholding critical information. Later, Lady Carise took the floor to advocate the creation of "[First Senator](/wiki/First_Senator "First Senator")," a powerful position that would wield considerable power over the economy and military. While many senators distrusted Lady Carise's motives, Casterfo managed to sway the Senate into adopting the motion by pointing to the endemic deadlock in the New Republic. As a result, the Populist attempt to block the motion was defeated.[[13]](#cite_note-Bloodline-13)

While Organa and her Populist colleagues [Tai-Lin Garr](/wiki/Tai-Lin_Garr "Tai-Lin Garr") and [Varish Vicly](/wiki/Varish_Vicly "Varish Vicly") were dismayed by the results, they decided to change tactics by nominating a Populist for First Senator to prevent a Centrist from holding that position. Since Organa was considered a powerful and charismatic senator, Tai-Lin and Varish convinced her to run for First Senator. Despite her reluctance, Organa agreed to form an exploratory committee to consider the possibility at the urging of her staff including C-3PO, her aide Korrie, and her pilot Sonnel. Leia later contacted her husband, Han, by hologram to discuss the recent developments. Though Han expressed disappointment, he understood her devotion to keeping the New Republic in one piece.[[13]](#cite_note-Bloodline-13)

 [![A propaganda poster supporting Organa as First Senator](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5d/First_Senator_Leia_poster.png/revision/latest?cb=20161022184516) [![A propaganda poster supporting Organa as First Senator](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5d/First_Senator_Leia_poster.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20161022184516)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5d/First_Senator_Leia_poster.png/revision/latest?cb=20161022184516) 

A propaganda poster supporting Organa as First Senator

 

The following day, Leia met with Lady Carise to conclude their discussion on the Supreme governorship of Birren. During the meeting, Leia revealed that she had been adopted by Bail and Breha Organa. Since Leia and her son Ben had little interest in inheriting the governorship, Leia agreed to support Lady Carise's claim to the title in return for keeping her parentage a secret. While conversing with Lady Carise, Organa admitted that the position of First Senator might not be such a bad idea. In addition, Leia dispatched Greer and the starfighter pilot Seastriker to the watery planet [Pamarthe](/wiki/Pamarthe "Pamarthe") to investigate whether Rinnrivin was hiring pilots from there. Instead, the two Republic pilots learned that Rinnrivin was hiring a shadowy militia group known as the [Amaxine warriors](/wiki/Amaxine_warriors_(New_Republic_Era) "Amaxine warriors (New Republic Era)"), who operated from a base in the Centrist world Daxam IV.[[13]](#cite_note-Bloodline-13)

Greer and Joph discussed their findings with Leia and noted that the Amaxines tended to operate in predominantly Centrist worlds. Suspecting that several Centrist senators were colluding with Rinnrivin's cartel, Organa decided to turn to Casterfo for help since she regarded him as the only Centrist she could trust. During a private dinner at Hosnian Prime's [hanging gardens](/wiki/Hanging_gardens "Hanging gardens"), Organa discussed her concerns about the connection between the Amaxines and Rinnrivin's cartel with Casterfo and convinced the senator to visit Daxam IV. During the dinner, Casterfo confided in Leia and told her about his harsh childhood on Riosa, which had led him to hate Darth Vader and the Emperor. In return, Leia told him about her torture at the hands of Vader but omitted the fact that the late Sith Lord was her father. Because of this meeting, the two became unlikely friends.[[13]](#cite_note-Bloodline-13)

The following day, Leia and Tai-Lin met in the New Republic senatorial complex's banquet hall to discuss her planned nomination for First Senator. There, Leia discovered a hand-scribbled note with the word "RUN." Acting quickly, Leia managed to evacuate the senatorial complex's conference hall moments before a bomb destroyed half of the building. While nobody was killed due to Leia's quick thinking, several senators and staff were wounded by the blast. Leia survived the bombing unscathed apart from some concussion. After receiving treatment for concussion, Leia transmitted a voice message for again to assure him that she was safe.[[13]](#cite_note-Bloodline-13)

##### Missions to Ryloth and Harloff Minor[]

The Populists and Centrists accused each other of staging the bombing for political capital. Despite this bickering, Organa and Casterfo resolved to continue their investigation into Rinnrivin's cartel and the Amaxines. After seeing news footage showing an alleged Twi'lek bomber, Leia decided to travel to Ryloth to search the [planet's archives](/wiki/Ryloth_archives "Ryloth archives") with C-3PO, Korrie, and Joph for information about Rinnrivin's cartel.
