She never cared much for being royalty, for her priority was to help those who needed her, and not wealth nor recognition.[[77]](#cite_note-PL5-77) A woman of action, eager to get things done and making positive differences in the galaxy, Leia was impatient, a trait she shared with her brother, Luke.[[18]](#cite_note-Moving_Target-18) He believed that Leia's strength of will, which allowed her to continue despite events such as the destruction of Alderaan and the loss of her son, was a manifestation of her power in the Force.[[195]](#cite_note-Visual_Guide-195) However, she also admitted to herself that some of her strength was fueled by desperation and even hatred at times.[[13]](#cite_note-Bloodline-13) She truly hated her birth father for everything he had done and refused to remember Darth Vader as her father, seeing Bail Organa as the individual who deserved that name. While she did fear that she could become like Vader if she learned the secrets of the Force, she resolved to never become like the Sith Lord. Even though she did experience a hunger to grow in her Force power after using it on Madurs, which concerned her, she knew she had unlocked her powers out of a desire to help others.[[51]](#cite_note-Princess_and_Scoundrel-51)

Leia immensely regretted that her actions on the first Death Star indirectly led to the destruction of her homeworld. She was conscious of the fact that she alienated many people because of that. Constantly questioning whether she did the right thing, she came to the realization that she would willingly sacrifice those innocent lives again if it meant stopping the Empire. In her eyes, the cause was greater than any one person.[[112]](#cite_note-SWA2-112) She stated to Ellian Zahra that she didn't kill to settle scores, control people, or make them afraid, but only when she had no choice and always in the name of justice.[[228]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_(2020)_24-228) As Leia grew older, however, she placed more value in protecting lives than destroying her enemies; "jumping in an X-wing and blowing something up" could not be a winning strategy against forces like the First Order if there were no people to fight for the cause. She had the wisdom to realize that the Resistance having a leader with this foresight was better than having a hero who took unnecessary risks.[[182]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-182) Aware of how others looked to her for leadership, she looked to other members of the Resistance like Poe Dameron to take on these responsibilities when she was gone.[[50]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-50)

## Powers and abilities[]

:   "*I'm sure Luke wasn't on that thing when it blew.*"  
    "*He wasn't. I can feel it.*"
:   ―Han Solo and Leia Organa after seeing the Death Star II explode[[11]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-11)

### Force powers[]

 [![Leia became quite skilled with her lightsaber under her brother's tutelage.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6e/LeiasOrgana-TLC.png/revision/latest?cb=20230407041242) [![Leia became quite skilled with her lightsaber under her brother's tutelage.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6e/LeiasOrgana-TLC.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20230407041242)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6e/LeiasOrgana-TLC.png/revision/latest?cb=20230407041242) 

Leia became quite skilled with her lightsaber under her brother's tutelage.

 

As the biological daughter of the [Chosen One](/wiki/Chosen_One "Chosen One"), Leia, like her twin brother, Luke Skywalker, was immensely strong in the Force.[[154]](#cite_note-SYWtBaJ?-154) After the Battle of Endor, Organa believed she did not have anything akin to her brother's power in the Force and felt she could not be like him, but Solo assuaged her fears by telling her she did not have to be like her brother. During the skirmish on Madurs, after all of her attempts to control the Force had failed, she simply allowed herself to exist within it as defeat seemed inevitable, which allowed her to call out for help and summon an edont. Afterward, Organa understood she had been able to use the Force because she felt it inside herself, instead of looking for it outside, and resolved to speak to her brother about learning its secrets.[[51]](#cite_note-Princess_and_Scoundrel-51)

Leia possessed a strong Force sense. At a young age, she unknowingly used the Force to sense others' feelings and thoughts, showing wisdom and insight beyond her years.[[41]](#cite_note-Kenobi_Part_I-41)[[43]](#cite_note-Kenobi_Part_II-43)[[44]](#cite_note-Kenobi_Part_III-44) She was also able to resist interrogation by both Reva Sevander[[45]](#cite_note-Kenobi_Part_IV-45) and many years later, (unknowingly) by her father, Darth Vader.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) Luke believed that her strong "gut feelings" were another manifestation of her abilities;[[195]](#cite_note-Visual_Guide-195) after her birth, she was left with a lasting impression of images and feelings of her birth mother, that she was "very beautiful, kind, but sad."[[11]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-11) After Skywalker revealed on Endor that they were siblings, she was shocked but deep down, she had always known this to be true.[[30]](#cite_note-DB-Leia-bio-30) She sensed the lingering dark presence of [Darth Maul](/wiki/Maul "Maul") in the Theed Royal Palace, dating back to the former Sith's duel against Obi-Wan Kenobi and [Qui-Gon Jinn](/wiki/Qui-Gon_Jinn "Qui-Gon Jinn") during the [Battle of Naboo](/wiki/Battle_of_Naboo "Battle of Naboo").[[180]](#cite_note-SE3-180) Many years later, Leia's power remained strong; she felt a disturbance in the Force when the Hosnian System was destroyed by Starkiller Base.[[212]](#cite_note-TFA-novel-212) Through the Force, she later sensed Han Solo's death on Starkiller Base at the hands of their son while she was on D'Qar.[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-10) When her brother died, she sensed it as well, and sensed that he died at peace.[[182]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-182)

Leia actively demonstrated the ability to sense her brother's presence through the Force. When Luke failed to contact Kenobi while hanging underneath Bespin's Cloud City, weak and helpless, he called out to Leia with the Force, apparently out of instinct. She sensed him, and thus asked to direct the *Millennium Falcon* to his location.[[151]](#cite_note-Episode_V-151) After the second Death Star blew up, she assured Solo that Skywalker had not been on it at the time.[[11]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-11)

 [![Organa used the Force to survive the vacuum of space.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cc/Leia_can_fly.png/revision/latest?cb=20181206073317) [![Organa used the Force to survive the vacuum of space.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cc/Leia_can_fly.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20181206073317)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cc/Leia_can_fly.png/revision/latest?cb=20181206073317) 

Organa used the Force to survive the vacuum of space.

 

Though not formally trained at this time, Leia could use her Force abilities in other ways; she could use a lightsaber with enough skill to fight in the battle of [Nar Shaddaa](/wiki/Nar_Shaddaa "Nar Shaddaa"). She unconsciously drew upon the dark side to gain the strength to compress the neck of Jabba the Hutt with a chain to the point of asphyxiation.[[13]](#cite_note-Bloodline-13)

After being blown into space, Leia used the power of the Force to both remain alive in the [vacuum](/wiki/Vacuum "Vacuum") of space and fly back to the safety of her vessel, where she was able to press the button to enter her ship. The exposure and effort left her in vital need of medical attention.[[182]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-182)

Despite not completing her Jedi training, Leia was able to preserve her consciousness after death much like her brother, likely being taught by him how to do it.[[23]](#cite_note-TROS-23)

Despite her short time training, Leia became skilled enough in lightsaber combat to briefly get the better of her brother, although according to Luke, she wasn't as naturally talented in lightsaber combat as he was.[[225]](#cite_note-TROSEE-225) She first demonstrated lightsaber skills while rescuing Luke from Grakkus Jahibakti Tingi, where she used one to fight off the stormtroopers Kreel had brought in.[[95]](#cite_note-SW12-95) On the last night of her training, Leia was able to fight on par against her brother, and even best him in one duel when they were practicing together.[[23]](#cite_note-TROS-23)

### Other abilities[]

 [![Organa was a natural leader from her youth.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/SomebodyHastoSaveOurSkins-SWL12.png/revision/latest?cb=20250622184549) [![Organa was a natural leader from her youth.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/SomebodyHastoSaveOurSkins-SWL12.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250622184549)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/SomebodyHastoSaveOurSkins-SWL12.png/revision/latest?cb=20250622184549) 

Organa was a natural leader from her youth.

 

Renowned for her leadership and diplomatic skills, Organa was a capable mediator[[179]](#cite_note-SE2-179) and had training in public speaking. She felt very comfortable leading dangerous missions. Often, Organa used her strategic and quick thinking to carry out carefully laid plans of infiltration or trick enemies.

Thanks to her aunts' insistent lessons, Organa was proficient in self-defense as well, including how to resist interrogation.[[34]](#cite_note-TPtSatFB-34) As competent with weaponry as she was with words, Organa had great accuracy when using [blaster pistols](/wiki/Blaster_pistol "Blaster pistol"), rarely missing her shots.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)[[151]](#cite_note-Episode_V-151)[[11]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-11) She could use blasters of all shapes and sizes, shooting several stormtroopers during her escape from the Death Star and destroying a TIE fighter with an AT-AT's heavy [laser cannon](/wiki/Laser_cannon "Laser cannon") during the Attack on Cymoon 1.[[86]](#cite_note-SW3-86)

 [![Organa was a symbol of hope and leadership her entire adult life.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c2/Motivate_WotF.png/revision/latest?cb=20181206072033) [![Organa was a symbol of hope and leadership her entire adult life.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c2/Motivate_WotF.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20181206072033)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c2/Motivate_WotF.png/revision/latest?cb=20181206072033) 

Organa was a symbol of hope and leadership her entire adult life.

 

Organa had years of flight training;[[34]](#cite_note-TPtSatFB-34) indeed, she could pilot a *Lambda*-class shuttle,[[92]](#cite_note-SW8-92) and the *Millennium Falcon*,[[86]](#cite_note-SW3-86) even admirably by evading TIE/ln starfighters while Solo and Chewbacca hastily tried to repair its hyperdrive during their escape from Hoth.[[154]](#cite_note-SYWtBaJ?-154) Much like seasoned Rebel pilot Shara Bey, Organa could manually pilot a Naboo N-1 starfighter through Naboo's planet-wide storms without an astromech droid and destroy several climate-disruption arrays before saving Bey from a TIE fighter.[[180]](#cite_note-SE3-180) She rarely used such skills, though, as she was usually provided with, or resorted to, help from pilots to get to her destinations.[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9)[[75]](#cite_note-PL1-75)[[179]](#cite_note-SE2-179)[[18]](#cite_note-Moving_Target-18)

During her youth on Alderaan, Organa learned how to ride, becoming an Alderaanian junior champion in steeplechase.[[18]](#cite_note-Moving_Target-18) Leia also knew how to plant and care for [orchids](/wiki/Orchid "Orchid") as her adoptive mother, Breha planted [Malastarian](/wiki/Malastare "Malastare") orchids. Leia also learnt and studied dance and would practice with her father until her feet were sore.[[14]](#cite_note-Princess_of_Alderaan-14)

## Equipment[]

 [![Leia's lightsaber emitted a blue blade.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/74/LeiasLightsaberFull-TLC.png/revision/latest?cb=20201215151554) [![Leia's lightsaber emitted a blue blade.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/74/LeiasLightsaberFull-TLC.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/350?cb=20201215151554)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/74/LeiasLightsaberFull-TLC.png/revision/latest?cb=20201215151554) 

Leia's lightsaber emitted a blue blade.

 

Leia wielded a [Defender sporting blaster pistol](/wiki/Defender_sporting_blaster_pistol "Defender sporting blaster pistol"),[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) which was called "[Satine's Lament](/wiki/Satine%27s_Lament "Satine's Lament"),"[[229]](#cite_note-USW-229) which she used to defend herself from Imperial stormtroopers,[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) used it again during the Battle of Theed,[[180]](#cite_note-SE3-180) and to stun Poe Dameron aboard the *Raddus*.[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-10)

While rescuing Luke Skywalker from Grakkus Jahibakti Tingi, Organa used a lightsaber to fight off stormtrooper, with her commenting that she had always wanted to use one.[[95]](#cite_note-SW12-95)

During her Jedi training, under her brother, Organa wielded her own lightsaber which had a blue blade.[[23]](#cite_note-TROS-23) The lightsaber hilt was coloured silver and copper with mother-of-pearl inlays. It had an elegant symmetry with silver and gold hues that referenced her upbringing on Alderaan.[[230]](#cite_note-Lightsaber_Collection-230)

 [![Leia Organa wore a green dress during her wedding to Han Solo](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/LeiaOrganasweddingdress-back.png/revision/latest?cb=20241027013742) [![Leia Organa wore a green dress during her wedding to Han Solo](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/LeiaOrganasweddingdress-back.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20241027013742)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/LeiaOrganasweddingdress-back.png/revision/latest?cb=20241027013742) 

Leia Organa wore a green dress during her wedding to Han Solo

 

At the award ceremony on Yavin 4, Organa wore a simple flowing white [dress](/wiki/Delva_Racine_original_hanging_sleeve_dress "Delva Racine original hanging sleeve dress") with hanging sleeves, designed by [Delva Racine](/wiki/Delva_Racine "Delva Racine")[[231]](#cite_note-GG-231). Her snow gear on Hoth included a Rebel-issue all weather vest and gray military snow [boots](/wiki/Boot "Boot") with bindings. While on Bespin, Calrissian provided Organa with a refined leisure [suit](/wiki/Clothing "Clothing"), consisting of a burgundy tunic and a delicate blue [cloak](/wiki/Cloak "Cloak").[[232]](#cite_note-VE-232)

For her wedding to Han Solo, Organa wore a green dress, embroidered with flowers, with the sides open, giving Organa room to move her leg. Organa carried a bouquet of wildflowers and had her hair hung loose except for two braids framing her face with lacing run through them which were the same as the lacing that tied her bouquet together.[[51]](#cite_note-Princess_and_Scoundrel-51)

## Behind the scenes[]

### Overview and Carrie Fisher[]

:   "*I didn't stop being Leia.* […] *I have stayed in character for the last thirty-five years.*"
:   ―Carrie Fisher in a 2015 interview[[233]](#cite_note-Uncut_Interview-233)

 [![Carrie Fisher, who portrayed Princess Leia throughout the Skywalker Saga](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a9/Carrie_Fisher.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120612164203) [![Carrie Fisher, who portrayed Princess Leia throughout the Skywalker Saga](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a9/Carrie_Fisher.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20120612164203)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a9/Carrie_Fisher.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120612164203) 

Carrie Fisher, who portrayed Princess Leia throughout the Skywalker Saga

 

Leia Organa was portrayed by [Carrie Fisher](/wiki/Carrie_Fisher "Carrie Fisher") in the [original trilogy](/wiki/Original_trilogy "Original trilogy") and the [sequel trilogy](/wiki/Sequel_trilogy "Sequel trilogy"). Director [George Lucas](/wiki/George_Lucas "George Lucas") oversaw the auditioning process, and the runner-up for the role behind Fisher was [Terri Nunn](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Terri_Nunn "wikipedia:Terri Nunn"), who became the lead singer of the band [*Berlin*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Berlin_(band) "wikipedia:Berlin (band)").[[234]](#cite_note-Fisher_interview-234)

In [*Star Wars*: Episode III *Revenge of the Sith*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_III_Revenge_of_the_Sith "Star Wars: Episode III Revenge of the Sith"), the infant Leia was played by [Aidan Barton](/wiki/Aidan_Barton "Aidan Barton") (the son of editor [Roger Barton](/wiki/Roger_Barton "Roger Barton")), who also played her brother, Luke. [Julie Dolan](/wiki/Julie_Dolan "Julie Dolan") voices her in the video game *[Star Wars: Uprising](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Uprising "Star Wars: Uprising")*, the animated series *[Star Wars Rebels](/wiki/Star_Wars_Rebels "Star Wars Rebels")*, and the LEGO series *[LEGO Star Wars: The Freemaker Adventures](/wiki/LEGO_Star_Wars:_The_Freemaker_Adventures "LEGO Star Wars: The Freemaker Adventures")*. [Carolyn Hennesy](/wiki/Carolyn_Hennesy "Carolyn Hennesy") voices her in the animated series *[Star Wars Resistance](/wiki/Star_Wars_Resistance "Star Wars Resistance")*.[[235]](#cite_note-Station_Theta_Black-235) In *[Rogue One: A Star Wars Story](/wiki/Rogue_One:_A_Star_Wars_Story "Rogue One: A Star Wars Story")*, Leia was played by [Ingvild Deila](/wiki/Ingvild_Deila "Ingvild Deila").[[236]](#cite_note-Credits-236) In the animated microseries *[Star Wars Forces of Destiny](/wiki/Star_Wars_Forces_of_Destiny "Star Wars Forces of Destiny")*, Leia was voiced by [Shelby Young](/wiki/Shelby_Young "Shelby Young").[[237]](#cite_note-Entertainment_Weekly-237) Voice actress [Misty Lee](/wiki/Misty_Lee "Misty Lee") voiced Leia in the video game *[Star Wars Battlefront II](/wiki/Star_Wars_Battlefront_II "Star Wars Battlefront II")*, with [Rachel Butera](/wiki/Rachel_Butera "Rachel Butera") voicing Organa in the Resurrection DLC.[[238]](#cite_note-Rachel_Butera_Battlefront-238) In the [Disney+](/wiki/Disney%2B "Disney+") series [*Obi-Wan Kenobi*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Star Wars: Obi-Wan Kenobi"), a 10-year-old Leia is portrayed by [Vivien Lyra Blair](/wiki/Vivien_Lyra_Blair "Vivien Lyra Blair").[[239]](#cite_note-Part_I-239)

Following Fisher's death in [December](/wiki/December "December") [2016](/wiki/2016 "2016"), [*Star Wars*: Episode VIII *The Last Jedi*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_VIII_The_Last_Jedi "Star Wars: Episode VIII The Last Jedi") director [Rian Johnson](/wiki/Rian_Johnson "Rian Johnson") confirmed that Fisher had completed shooting all her scenes the previous [July](/wiki/July "July") and that Leia would appear in Episode VIII.[[240]](#cite_note-Sun28Dec-240) On [January 6](/wiki/January_6 "January 6"), [2017](/wiki/2017 "2017"), it was reported that Disney was "scrambling" in the wake of Fisher's death and that [*Star Wars*: Episode IX *The Rise of Skywalker*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IX_The_Rise_of_Skywalker "Star Wars: Episode IX The Rise of Skywalker") director [Colin Trevorrow](/wiki/Colin_Trevorrow "Colin Trevorrow") would soon meet with [Kathleen Kennedy](/wiki/Kathleen_Kennedy "Kathleen Kennedy") and other executives to determine how to adjust the story of Episode IX, which, in turn, could possibly affect Episode VIII.[[241]](#cite_note-trevorrowmeeting-241) Soon after that meeting, [Lucasfilm](/wiki/Lucasfilm "Lucasfilm") announced that they had ruled out recreating Fisher's character digitally for any future films.[[242]](#cite_note-PageSixRuledOut-242) On [March 24](/wiki/March_24 "March 24"), 2017, Disney CEO [Bob Iger](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bob_Iger "wikipedia:Bob Iger") said that Fisher's role in *The Last Jedi* has not been altered following her death, and that her performance remains as was planned.[[243]](#cite_note-IgerLastJedi-243) On [April 7](/wiki/April_7 "April 7"), 2017, Carrie Fisher's brother [Todd Fisher](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Todd_Fisher "wikipedia:Todd Fisher") revealed that Leia Organa would appear in *Star Wars*: Episode IX via already recorded footage.[[244]](#cite_note-Comicbook-244) However, Kennedy soon confirmed that Fisher would not be in the film,[[245]](#cite_note-KK_Episode_IX-245) and that the team had "pretty much started over" on it considering her passing.[[246]](#cite_note-KK_Episode_IX_start_over-246) The casting announcement for Episode IX later revealed that Fisher would appear in the film after all using unseen footage from *The Force Awakens*.[[247]](#cite_note-Episode_9_Cast_Announced-247)

On [October 29](/wiki/October_29 "October 29"), [2014](/wiki/2014 "2014"), for a [Halloween](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Halloween "wikipedia:Halloween")-themed update, a costume of Leia was added to [*The Sims 4*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Sims_4 "wikipedia:The Sims 4") for playable Sims to wear in-game. The costume is purely cosmetic and offers no gameplay changes.[[248]](#cite_note-Sims_4-248)

### Character development[]

In George Lucas's [rough draft](/wiki/The_Star_Wars_rough_draft "The Star Wars rough draft") of [the original film](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IV_A_New_Hope "Star Wars: Episode IV A New Hope"), Leia was a fourteen-year-old princess (the same age as Queen Amidala in [*The Phantom Menace*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_I_The_Phantom_Menace "Star Wars: Episode I The Phantom Menace")), the spoiled daughter of [King](/wiki/King "King") [Kayos](/wiki/Kayos "Kayos") and Queen Breha of [Aquilae](/wiki/Aquilae_(The_Star_Wars) "Aquilae (The Star Wars)"). In that draft, she had two brothers, Biggs and Windy, whose identities were substantially revised into their current form by the fourth draft (though they did not appear in intervening versions). The [third draft](/wiki/The_Star_Wars:_From_The_Adventures_of_Luke_Starkiller "The Star Wars: From The Adventures of Luke Starkiller") established her as Leia Organa, Princess of the peaceful world of [Organa Major](/wiki/Ogana_Major "Ogana Major"). In the fourth draft, Organa Major was renamed [Alderaan](/wiki/Alderaan "Alderaan"). Interestingly, when George Lucas was writing background material for licensees in [1977](/wiki/1977 "1977"), he wrote that she had several brothers, and that she was unaware whether her parents had escaped the destruction of her homeworld. No one from the House of Organa, however, had reached the Rebels yet.[[249]](#cite_note-The_Making_of_Star_Wars-249)

According to producer [Gary Kurtz](/wiki/Gary_Kurtz "Gary Kurtz"), Luke and Leia were not supposed to be siblings originally; Luke's sister was originally going to be a different person on the other side of [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy"), who was going to show up in a later episode that never came to be. Leia being Luke's sister was added to [*Star Wars*: Episode VI *Return of the Jedi*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_VI_Return_of_the_Jedi "Star Wars: Episode VI Return of the Jedi") "to wrap up everything neatly".[[250]](#cite_note-Threat-250)

### Make-up and costumes[]

 [![Leia's signature A New Hope hairstyle](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9b/Princessleiaheadwithgun.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20240522043127) [![Leia's signature A New Hope hairstyle](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9b/Princessleiaheadwithgun.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20240522043127)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9b/Princessleiaheadwithgun.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20240522043127) 

Leia's signature *A New Hope* hairstyle

 

Organa's "cinnamon bun"[[251]](#cite_note-Time-251) or "donut" hairstyle came after a long design process that considered various styles. One drawing by concept artist [Ralph McQuarrie](/wiki/Ralph_McQuarrie "Ralph McQuarrie") saw Organa with what [*Star Wars* Insider](/wiki/Star_Wars_Insider "Star Wars Insider") described as "unkempt contemporary looks." Other ideas included pulled back locks and austere hair. Fisher herself would recall being made to try out at least thirty hair styles. In the end, the iconic donut style came at the suggestion of hairdresser [Patricia McDermott](/wiki/Patricia_McDermott "Patricia McDermott"), who thought up the style and tried it on Fisher during costume fittings shortly before filming on *A New Hope* began.[[252]](#cite_note-222_Archive-252) George Lucas commented on Leia's "cinnamon bun" hairstyle in [*Time*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Time_(magazine) "wikipedia:Time (magazine)") magazine: "In the 1977 film, I was working very hard to create something different that wasn't fashion, so I went with a kind of Southwestern [Pancho Villa](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pancho_Villa "wikipedia:Pancho Villa") woman revolutionary look, which is what that is. The buns are basically from turn-of-the-century [Mexico](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mexico "wikipedia:Mexico")."[[251]](#cite_note-Time-251) Fisher herself, however, stated Lucas approved of the hairstyle by simply saying "That's okay."[[252]](#cite_note-222_Archive-252) In [2017](/wiki/2017 "2017"), the traveling Smithsonian exhibition "[Star Wars and the Power of Costume](https://www.sites.si.edu/s/archived-exhibit?topicId=0TO36000000L5MoGAK)" included a photo of Mexican revolutionary colonel [Clara de la Rocha](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Clara_de_la_Rocha "wikipedia:Clara de la Rocha") as one of the inspirations for the style, alongside photos of [Native American Hopi tribe](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hopi "wikipedia:Hopi") women with a similar "squash blossom" hairstyle.[[253]](#cite_note-CNN_Style-253)

The costume designer for the films had a "no lingerie in space" policy, which prevented Fisher from wearing a brassiere. To maintain decorum, adhesive tape was used in place of the banned garment.[[254]](#cite_note-Newsweek-254)

### *Obi-Wan Kenobi* television series[]

:   "*The [goal] was to craft [Leia Organa] in such way that honored what Carrie Fisher had done. But also you got to play a little bit of the nature/nurture question, where you see she's the best of her mother and her father, but you also get to get to see her adopted parents and how they have formed who she becomes too. She's very much a byproduct of all those people. And we're getting to see the untold story of how Obi-Wan was a part of her growing up too.*"
:   ―Joby Harold[[255]](#cite_note-Vader_terrifying-255)

 [![Leia Organa character poster for Obi-Wan Kenobi](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/57/LeiaOrgana-OWKPoster.png/revision/latest?cb=20220531192420) [![Leia Organa character poster for Obi-Wan Kenobi](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/57/LeiaOrgana-OWKPoster.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/190?cb=20220531192420)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/57/LeiaOrgana-OWKPoster.png/revision/latest?cb=20220531192420) 

Leia Organa character poster for *Obi-Wan Kenobi*

 

During production of *Obi-Wan Kenobi*, writer [Joby Harold](/wiki/Joby_Harold "Joby Harold") tried to think of something that would be seismic enough to make Obi-Wan Kenobi leave Tatooine, which led to him writing young Leia Organa as a call to action for Kenobi.[[255]](#cite_note-Vader_terrifying-255) She was meant to bring out a maternal sense in Kenobi that told him life is not just about living by the book. She was also meant to bring out a human side to Kenobi and help him learn to trust people.[[256]](#cite_note-Return-256) Harold was excited about filling in the gaps in Organa's story that were alluded to in her message to Kenobi in *A New Hope*,[[257]](#cite_note-TheWrap-257) such as why she asked Kenobi for help.[[258]](#cite_note-HW-258) Harold also wanted Organa to be as important as Luke Skywalker was. The goal was to craft Organa in a way that honored Carrie Fisher's portrayal[[255]](#cite_note-Vader_terrifying-255) in the [original trilogy](/wiki/Original_trilogy "Original trilogy")[[9]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-9) and showed that she has the best of Padmé Amidala and Anakin Skywalker. Harold also wanted to show how Organa's adoptive parents formed who she becomes.[[255]](#cite_note-Vader_terrifying-255) Harold found it challenging to write her in a way that come across as her being spirited and not just an adult writing for a child.[[258]](#cite_note-HW-258) He looked at the films [*Paper Moon*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paper_Moon_(film) "wikipedia:Paper Moon (film)") and [*Midnight Run*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Midnight_Run "wikipedia:Midnight Run") for influence on Organa and Kenobi's relationship after the former's rescue on Daiyu.[[255]](#cite_note-Vader_terrifying-255) A code name was used to keep Organa's appearance a secret.[[258]](#cite_note-HW-258)

Director [Deborah Chow](/wiki/Deborah_Chow "Deborah Chow") offered the role to young actress Vivien Lyra Blair and she spent a summer filming for the series.[[259]](#cite_note-Vivien_Facebook-259) In a chemistry test between Blair and [Ewan McGregor](/wiki/Ewan_McGregor "Ewan McGregor"), the actor who played Kenobi in the series, they recited the lines for one of their conversations on Daiyu. Chow felt that Blair had the essence of Organa and Carrie Fisher. McGregor said that Blair had all the wit and cheek of Fisher's portrayal of Organa. The two actors got to know each other better during shooting, which went hand in hand with Organa and Kenobi's relationship in the series.[[256]](#cite_note-Return-256)

### Feminist icon[]

:   "*I am a huge fan of every single character but, how cool was Princess Leia? She was the beginning of the strong woman role.*"
:   ―Meredith Salenger[[260]](#cite_note-Redemption229-260)

In [January](/wiki/January "January") 2017, images of Leia, both as a princess and a general, were prominently featured during the Women's March not only in the United States, but also overseas. According to feminist writer Anne Thériault, Princess Leia was the most empowering feminist character of all, one who "keeps fighting when things seem impossible."[[261]](#cite_note-Women's_March-261) Actress [Meredith Salenger](/wiki/Meredith_Salenger "Meredith Salenger"), who portrayed the female Jedi [Barriss Offee](/wiki/Barriss_Offee "Barriss Offee") in several *Star Wars* animated series, praised Organa as "the beginning of the strong woman role" seen in modern storytelling.[[260]](#cite_note-Redemption229-260)

### Her biological mother[]

:   "*The part that I never really developed is the death of Luke and Leia's mother. I had a backstory for her in earlier drafts, but it basically didn't survive. When I got to Jedi, I wanted one of the kids to have some kind of memory of her because she will be a key figure in the new episodes I'm writing. But I really debated on whether or not Leia should remember her.*"
:   ―George Lucas[[262]](#cite_note-Annotated-262)

George Lucas stated that he wanted one of the Skywalker twins to recall their mother, hence Leia describing her as "very beautiful, kind but sad" in *Return of the Jedi*.[[262]](#cite_note-Annotated-262)

When *Revenge of the Sith* came out, many people did not understand how it was possible that Leia claims to remember her mother when she had known her for barely a minute. There has been some debate about whether Leia is discussing her biological mother Padmé Amidala or her foster mother Breha Organa. [StarWars.com](/wiki/StarWars.com "StarWars.com"), the official *Star Wars* website, stated in a Q & A section that Leia is remembering Padmé, but this may no longer be [canonical](/wiki/Canon "Canon").[[263]](#cite_note-SW_QA-263)

In an interview in the November 2005 edition from the UK magazine *[Total Film](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Total_Film "wikipedia:Total Film")*, producer [Rick McCallum](/wiki/Rick_McCallum "Rick McCallum") was asked about this incongruence, to which McCallum teased that the ultimately-unrealized *[Star Wars: Underworld](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Underworld "Star Wars: Underworld")* television series could have answered that.[[264]](#cite_note-264)

### Continuity[]

[*Dark Droids* 1](/wiki/Dark_Droids_1 "Dark Droids 1") has Leia Organa already aware of the [Death Star II](/wiki/DS-2_Death_Star_II_Mobile_Battle_Station "DS-2 Death Star II Mobile Battle Station").[[265]](#cite_note-DD_1-265) However *[Moving Target: A Princess Leia Adventure](/wiki/Moving_Target:_A_Princess_Leia_Adventure "Moving Target: A Princess Leia Adventure")*, in which Leia is informed of the Death Star II, takes place after *Dark Droids*.[[18]](#cite_note-Moving_Target-18)

[35.1](#cite_ref-Princess_Leia:_Royal_Rebel_35-1) *[Princess Leia: Royal Rebel](/wiki/Princess_Leia:_Royal_Rebel "Princess Leia: Royal Rebel")* 36. ↑ [36.0](#cite_ref-So_Much_More_36-0) [36.1](#cite_ref-So_Much_More_36-1) [IDWStarWarsAdventuresLogoSmaller](/wiki/Star_Wars_Adventures_(2017) "Star Wars Adventures (2017)") "[So Much More](/wiki/So_Much_More "So Much More")" — [*Star [↑](#cite_ref-Hyperspace_Stories_2_37-0) [*Hyperspace Stories* 2](/wiki/Hyperspace_Stories_2 "Hyperspace Stories 2") 38. [↑](#cite_ref-10_BBY_38-0) The events of *[Leia, Princess of Alderaan](/wiki/Leia,_Princess_of_Alderaan "Leia, Princess of Alderaan")* take place shortly after **Leia Organa's** sixteenth birthday. Leia claims these events happened seven years ago, meaning when she was 9 or coming up to her ninth birthday. *[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Galactic_Atlas "Star Wars: Galactic Atlas")* places Leia's birth to [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY") meaning these events took place in [10 BBY](/wiki/10_BBY "10 BBY"). 39. [↑](#cite_ref-Leia_Date_39-0) *[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Galactic_Atlas "Star Wars: Galactic Atlas")* places **Leia Organa's** birth in [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY"). The events of *[Leia, Princess of Alderaan](/wiki/Leia,_Princess_of_Alderaan "Leia, Princess of Alderaan")* commence just after Organa's sixteenth [birthday](/wiki/Birthday "Birthday"), which places the events of the novel in [3 BBY](/wiki/3_BBY "3 BBY"). 40. ↑ [40.0](#cite_ref-SW33_40-0) [40.1](#cite_ref-SW33_40-1) [40.2](#cite_ref-SW33_40-2) [*Star Wars* (2015) 33](/wiki/Star_Wars_(2015)_33 "Star Wars (2015) 33") 41. ↑ [41.0](#cite_ref-Kenobi_Part_I_41-0) [41.1](#cite_ref-Kenobi_Part_I_41-1) [41.2](#cite_ref-Kenobi_Part_I_41-2) [41.3](#cite_ref-Kenobi_Part_I_41-3) [41.4](#cite_ref-Kenobi_Part_I_41-4) [41.5](#cite_ref-Kenobi_Part_I_41-5) [41.6](#cite_ref-Kenobi_Part_I_41-6) [Obi-Wan Kenobi new series logo](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Star Wars: Obi-Wan Kenobi") *[Star Wars: Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Star Wars: Obi-Wan Kenobi")* — "[Part I](/wiki/Part_I "Part I")" 42. [↑](#cite_ref-KenobiDate_42-0) *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates the events of *[Star Wars: Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Star Wars: Obi-Wan Kenobi")* to [9 BBY](/wiki/9_BBY "9 BBY"). [↑](#cite_ref-Coruscant_Date_49-0) *[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Galactic_Atlas "Star Wars: Galactic Atlas")* places **Leia Organa's** birth in [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY"). The events of *[Leia, Princess of Alderaan](/wiki/Leia,_Princess_of_Alderaan "Leia, Princess of Alderaan")* commence just after Organa's sixteenth [birthday](/wiki/Birthday "Birthday"), which places the events of the novel in [3 BBY](/wiki/3_BBY "3 BBY"). [↑](#cite_ref-Ben_Solo_training_date_note_191-0) *[Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: The Visual Dictionary](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Rise_of_Skywalker:_The_Visual_Dictionary "Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: The Visual Dictionary")* establishes that Ben Solo began his [Jedi training](/wiki/Jedi_training "Jedi training") nineteen years before the [Hosnian Cataclysm](/wiki/Hosnian_Cataclysm "Hosnian Cataclysm"). Since *[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Galactic_Atlas "Star Wars: Galactic Atlas")* dates the Hosnian Cataclysm to [34 ABY](/wiki/34_ABY "34 ABY"), Solo started his training in [15 ABY](/wiki/15_ABY "15 ABY"). 192. [↑](#cite_ref-Threat_250-0) [Premium-Era-real](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0e/Premium-Era-real.png/revision/latest?cb=20241019125517) [Gary Kurtz interview: The original Star Wars producer speaks](https://web.archive.org/web/20130804083652/https://www.filmthreat.com/interviews/8) by Chris Gore on *[Film Threat](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Film_Threat "wikipedia:Film Threat")* ([March 5](/wiki/March_5 "March 5"), [2000](/wiki/2000 "2000")): "So the story was quite a bit more poignant and the ending was the coronation of Leia as the queen of what was left of her people, to take over the royal symbol. That meant she was then isolated from all of the rest and Luke went off then by himself. It was basically a kind of bittersweet ending. She's not his sister that dropped in to wrap up everything neatly. His sister was someone else way over on the other side of the galaxy and she wasn't going to show up until the next episode." [↑](#cite_ref-Vivien_Facebook_259-0) [Facebook icon](https://facebook.com) Vivien Lyra Blair ([@vivienlyrablairofficial](https://www.facebook.com/vivienlyrablairofficial)) on [Facebook](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Facebook "wikipedia:Facebook") ([post](https://www.facebook.com/photo/?fbid=461414942460436&set=a.181989547069645) on [May 29](/wiki/May_29 "May 29"), [2022](/wiki/2022 "2022")): "Like most little girls I was drawn to Leia. 💫 When I went to #disneyland and flew the Millennium Falcon for the first time around 6 years old I was hooked on the whole galaxy! ✨ So when Deborah offered me the role I was speechless. She had to ask me for sure if I was saying yes! Then I got to spend the summer playing with droids, meeting an amazing crew, acting with a cast that made me feel special and respected and learning so much. And now I've met the fans who've made this journey even more incredible! 👀 The memories of this #obiwankenobi adventure will always be a part of me. Thank you to everyone that helped make this happen and thank you for believing in me😻" ([backup link](https://archive.ph/2qER9)) 260. ↑ [260.0](#cite_ref-Redemption229_260-0) [260.1](#cite_ref-Redemption229_260-1) [SWInsider](/wiki/Star_Wars_Insider "Star Wars Insider") "[The Redemption of Barriss Offee](/wiki/The_Redemption_of_Barriss_Offee "The Redemption of Barriss Offee")" — [*Star Wars Insider* 229](/wiki/Star_Wars_Insider_229 "Star Wars Insider 229") 261. [↑](#cite_ref-Women's_March_261-0) [Premium-Era-real](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0e/Premium-Era-real.png/revision/latest?cb=20241019125517) [How Princess Leia became an unofficial symbol for the Women's March](https://www.washingtonpost.com/news/arts-and-entertainment/wp/2017/01/23/how-princess-leia-became-an-unofficial-symbol-for-the-womens-march) by Gibson, Caitlin on [The Washington Post](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Washington_Post "wikipedia:The Washington Post") ([January 23](/wiki/January_23 "January 23"), [2017](/wiki/2017 "2017")) ([backup link](https://web.archive.org/web/20180810155437/https://www.washingtonpost.com/news/arts-and-entertainment/wp/2017/01/23/how-princess-leia-became-an-unofficial-symbol-for-the-womens-march) archived on [August 10](/wiki/August_10 "August 10"), [2018](/wiki/2018 "2018")) 262. ↑ [262.0](#cite_ref-Annotated_262-0) [262.1](#cite_ref-Annotated_262-1) *[Star Wars: The Annotated Screenplays](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Annotated_Screenplays "Star Wars: The Annotated Screenplays")* 263.
